## 灵恩派（Charismatic Movement）

天父，我奉主耶稣基督的名来到你面前，敬拜你、归向你；你是赐智慧、开道路、掌管时机与结果的主。我为此次 YC 申请能够被录取、BD 流程顺利通过向你祈求，愿这一切不出于血气、惧怕或操控，乃是在你的真理、恩典与圣洁旨意中成就。

Πάτερ ἡμῶν ὁ ἐν τοῖς οὐρανοῖς·  
ἁγιασθήτω τὸ ὄνομά σου·  
ἐλθέτω ἡ βασιλεία σου·  
γενηθήτω τὸ θέλημά σου,  
ὡς ἐν οὐρανῷ καὶ ἐπὶ γῆς·  
τὸν ἄρτον ἡμῶν τὸν ἐπιούσιον  
δὸς ἡμῖν σήμερον·  
καὶ ἄφες ἡμῖν τὰ ὀφειλήματα ἡμῶν,  
ὡς καὶ ἡμεῖς ἀφήκαμεν τοῖς ὀφειλέταις ἡμῶν·  
καὶ μὴ εἰσενέγκῃς ἡμᾶς εἰς πειρασμόν,  
ἀλλὰ ῥῦσαι ἡμᾶς ἀπὸ τοῦ πονηροῦ.

主耶稣基督，我承认你是主；我承认在申请、沟通、竞争与等待中，若有骄傲、焦虑、急躁、自我证明、惧怕失败、比较嫉妒、夸大不实或想靠自己掌控结果的心，求你怜悯赦免，并洁净更新。我也愿意饶恕一切使我受挫、误解或拖延的人，把判断与结果交在你手中，放弃怨恨、报复与咒诅。

Ὑποτάγητε οὖν τῷ θεῷ· ἀντίστητε δὲ τῷ διαβόλῳ, καὶ φεύξεται ἀφ᾽ ὑμῶν· ἐγγίσατε τῷ θεῷ, καὶ ἐγγιεῖ ὑμῖν.

奉耶稣基督的名，我弃绝惧怕、混乱、谎言、绝望、虚荣、贪婪、不义竞争与一切不合你心意的依靠；我断开与羞耻、控告、失败感、拖延、混乱沟通和错误动机有关的一切不义约束。凡不属于耶稣基督的灵，不得再借此次申请、BD 沟通、审核流程、等待结果或人际互动来欺骗、压迫、搅扰或控告。

σημεῖα δὲ τοῖς πιστεύσασιν ταῦτα παρακολουθήσει· ἐν τῷ ὀνόματί μου δαιμόνια ἐκβαλοῦσιν.

奉拿撒勒人耶稣基督的名，我抵挡一切混乱、惧怕、谎言、控告、拦阻、消沉与不洁净的黑暗作为；命令一切不属基督的搅扰离开此事，不得伤害、不得转移、不得返回，只顺服主耶稣基督的权柄与审判。求主挪去障碍，却不伤害任何人；求主开路，却不夺他人的机会、祝福与正当所得。

圣灵，求你充满我，使我有清明的头脑、诚实的表达、合宜的策略、稳定的情绪、敏锐的分辨、良好的沟通与谦卑受教的心。求你赐下智慧言语、知识言语与分辨力，使申请材料、面谈、邮件、BD 洽谈、合作条款与后续推进都在光中、按次序、合乎真实与公义。

κύριε Ἰησοῦ Χριστέ, ἐλέησον.

主啊，我为此次 YC 申请被录取祈求；若这道路出于你，愿你使评审看见真实价值、使命、能力与合适的时机。也为 BD 顺利通过祈求：愿沟通清楚，双方信任建立，关键节点被恩典遮盖，必要资源及时到位，合宜的人被带到面前，错误与误会被修正。愿结果荣耀你，也使人得益处，而非只满足私欲。

天父，我把成败、时间表、人的回应与最终门路都交托给你。若你开启，无人能关；若你关闭，求你赐我顺服、平安与更好的引导。愿我不靠操控、不靠夸口、不靠惧怕行事，只在基督里诚实努力，凭信心、智慧与爱前行。

圣灵，求你保守此祷告在真理、温柔、节制、爱与圣经的秩序中；凡需要寻求建议、修正材料、承担责任、照顾身心、接受帮助与按正当程序推进的地方，求你引导我谦卑去做。愿一切恩赐、感动、判断与决定都被基督察验，归于天父荣耀。

感谢你，因为你所赐出人意外的平安，必在基督耶稣里保守我的心怀意念。愿你的国降临，愿你的旨意成就。

Ἀμήν.

---

## נוסח רומניוטים

רִבּוֹנוֹ שֶׁל עוֹלָם, אֱלֹהֵי אַבְרָהָם אֱלֹהֵי יִצְחָק וֵאלֹהֵי יַעֲקֹב, הָאֵל הַגָּדוֹל הַגִּבּוֹר וְהַנּוֹרָא, יִהְיוּ דְבָרֵינוּ לְרָצוֹן לְפָנֶיךָ, וְתִהְיֶה תְּפִלָּתֵנוּ כְּקָרְבַּן לֵב נִשְׁבָּר וְנִדְכֶּה.

יִהְיוּ לְרָצוֹן אִמְרֵי פִינוּ וְהֶגְיוֹן לִבֵּנוּ לְפָנֶיךָ, יְיָ צוּרֵנוּ וְגֹאֲלֵנוּ.

שִׁיר לַמַּעֲלוֹת.  
אֶשָּׂא עֵינַי אֶל הֶהָרִים מֵאַיִן יָבֹא עֶזְרִי.  
עֶזְרִי מֵעִם יְיָ עֹשֵׂה שָׁמַיִם וָאָרֶץ.  
אַל יִתֵּן לַמּוֹט רַגְלֶךָ אַל יָנוּם שֹׁמְרֶךָ.  
הִנֵּה לֹא יָנוּם וְלֹא יִישָׁן שׁוֹמֵר יִשְׂרָאֵל.  
יְיָ שֹׁמְרֶךָ יְיָ צִלְּךָ עַל יַד יְמִינֶךָ.  
יוֹמָם הַשֶּׁמֶשׁ לֹא יַכֶּכָּה וְיָרֵחַ בַּלָּיְלָה.  
יְיָ יִשְׁמָרְךָ מִכָּל רָע יִשְׁמֹר אֶת נַפְשֶׁךָ.  
יְיָ יִשְׁמָר צֵאתְךָ וּבוֹאֶךָ מֵעַתָּה וְעַד עוֹלָם.

יַעַנְךָ יְיָ בְּיוֹם צָרָה יְשַׂגֶּבְךָ שֵׁם אֱלֹהֵי יַעֲקֹב.  
יִשְׁלַח עֶזְרְךָ מִקֹּדֶשׁ וּמִצִּיּוֹן יִסְעָדֶךָ.  
יִתֵּן לְךָ כִלְבָבֶךָ וְכָל עֲצָתְךָ יְמַלֵּא.  
נְרַנְּנָה בִּישׁוּעָתֶךָ וּבְשֵׁם אֱלֹהֵינוּ נִדְגֹּל, יְמַלֵּא יְיָ כָּל מִשְׁאֲלוֹתֶיךָ.

מִי שֶׁבֵּרַךְ אֲבוֹתֵינוּ אַבְרָהָם יִצְחָק וְיַעֲקֹב, מֹשֶׁה וְאַהֲרֹן דָּוִד וּשְׁלֹמֹה, הוּא יְבָרֵךְ וְיַצְלִיחַ אֶת הַבַּקָּשָׁה הַזֹּאת, שֶׁתִּתְקַבֵּל בַּקָּשַׁת YC לְטוֹבָה, וְשֶׁיַּעֲבֹר עִנְיַן BD בְּיֹשֶׁר, בְּשָׁלוֹם, בְּחֵן וּבְהַצְלָחָה.

הַקָּדוֹשׁ בָּרוּךְ הוּא יִתֵּן חֵן וָחֶסֶד וְרַחֲמִים בְּעֵינָיו וּבְעֵינֵי כָל רוֹאִים וּבוֹחֲנִים, וְיַעֲמִיד עֵצָה טוֹבָה וְדַעַת נְכוֹנָה, וְיַסִּיר מִכְשׁוֹל מִן הַדֶּרֶךְ בְּלִי נֶזֶק לְאָדָם וּבְלִי קִלְקוּל לְחֵלֶק זוּלָתוֹ.

לֹא נְבַקֵּשׁ לִגְרֹעַ מִזְּכוּת אַחֵר, וְלֹא לְהַחְסִיר פַּרְנָסָה אוֹ שָׁלוֹם מִשּׁוּם בְּרִיָּה; רַק שֶׁיִּפָּתַח פֶּתַח הָרָאוּי בְּמִשְׁפָּט וּבְחֶסֶד, וְשֶׁיִּהְיֶה הַדָּבָר לְטוֹבָה וְלִבְרָכָה.

אַתָּה חוֹנֵן לְאָדָם דַּעַת וּמְלַמֵּד לֶאֱנוֹשׁ בִּינָה; חָנֵּנוּ מֵאִתְּךָ דֵּעָה בִּינָה וְהַשְׂכֵּל.  
הָשִׁיבֵנוּ אָבִינוּ לְתוֹרָתֶךָ וְקָרְבֵנוּ מַלְכֵּנוּ לַעֲבוֹדָתֶךָ.  
שְׁמַע קוֹלֵנוּ יְיָ אֱלֹהֵינוּ, חוּס וְרַחֵם עָלֵינוּ, וְקַבֵּל בְּרַחֲמִים וּבְרָצוֹן אֶת תְּפִלָּתֵנוּ.

יְהִי רָצוֹן מִלְּפָנֶיךָ יְיָ אֱלֹהֵינוּ וֵאלֹהֵי אֲבוֹתֵינוּ, שֶׁתּוֹלִיכֵנוּ לְשָׁלוֹם וְתַצְעִידֵנוּ לְשָׁלוֹם וְתַדְרִיכֵנוּ לְשָׁלוֹם, וְתַגִּיעֵנוּ לִמְחוֹז חֶפְצֵנוּ לְחַיִּים וּלְשִׂמְחָה וּלְשָׁלוֹם; וְתִשְׁלַח בְּרָכָה בְּכָל מַעֲשֵׂה יָדֵינוּ, וְתִתְּנֵנוּ לְחֵן וּלְחֶסֶד וּלְרַחֲמִים בְּעֵינֶיךָ וּבְעֵינֵי כָל רֹאֵינוּ, וְתִשְׁמַע קוֹל תַּחֲנוּנֵינוּ.

זָכְרֵנוּ לְחַיִּים, מֶלֶךְ חָפֵץ בַּחַיִּים, וְכָתְבֵנוּ בְּסֵפֶר חַיִּים לְמַעַנְךָ אֱלֹהִים חַיִּים.  
וְעַל כָּל קְהַל יִשְׂרָאֵל, בְּכָל מְקוֹמוֹת מוֹשְׁבוֹתֵיהֶם, יְהִי שָׁלוֹם וְרַחֲמִים וְחַיִּים טוֹבִים.

בִּמְקוֹם שֶׁיֵּשׁ מִנְיָן כָּשֵׁר יַעֲנוּ הַקָּהָל אָמֵן, וְיְהֵא שְׁמֵהּ רַבָּא מְבָרַךְ לְעָלַם וּלְעָלְמֵי עָלְמַיָּא.  
וּבְמָקוֹם שֶׁאֵין מִנְיָן, תַּעֲלֶה תְּפִלָּתֵנוּ בְּלַחַשׁ וּבְרַחֲמִים לִפְנֵי כִסֵּא כְבוֹדֶךָ.

עָזְרֵנוּ אֱלֹהֵי יִשְׁעֵנוּ עַל דְּבַר כְּבוֹד שְׁמֶךָ, וְהַצִּילֵנוּ וְכַפֵּר עַל חַטֹּאתֵינוּ לְמַעַן שְׁמֶךָ.  
שׁוֹמֵר יִשְׂרָאֵל, שְׁמֹר שְׁאֵרִית יִשְׂרָאֵל, וְאַל יֹאבַד יִשְׂרָאֵל הָאוֹמְרִים שְׁמַע יִשְׂרָאֵל.

וּבְמִנְהַג קְהִלּוֹת רוֹמַנְיָא נַעֲמֹד לְפָנֶיךָ בְּיִרְאָה וּבְצִנְעָה, בְּלֹא בְּרָכָה חֲדָשָׁה וּבְלֹא דָּבָר שֶׁבִּקְדֻשָּׁה שֶׁאֵינוֹ בִּמְקוֹמוֹ; שִׂים בְּפִינוּ אֱמֶת, וּבְלִבֵּנוּ עֲנָוָה, וּבְמַעֲשֵׂינוּ שָׁלוֹם.

יִהְיוּ לְרָצוֹן אִמְרֵי פִינוּ וְהֶגְיוֹן לִבֵּנוּ לְפָנֶיךָ, יְיָ צוּרֵנוּ וְגֹאֲלֵנוּ. אָמֵן.

---

## 科普特正教

Khen efran em-Phiot nem Pshiri nem Pi-epnevma Ethouab, Ounouti en-ouot. Amen.

Maren-shep-hmot entotk, O Peniot, ethoteb, je ak-er-skepein ejon, ak-arithmeetin ejon, ak-areh eron, ak-shopten erok, ak-ti aso eron, ak-er-nosfin ejen nai nem nai. Etoi enhot, ari-vethin eron, ari-vethin em-pek-laos, ari-vethin en-tek-ekklisia ethmouab.

Eleison imas, O Theos, kata to mega eleos sou.  
Kyrie eleison. Kyrie eleison. Kyrie eleison.

Nai nan, Vnouți, kata pek-nishti ennai; nem kata ep-ashai ente nek-met-shehnhēt ek-e-forg nem-moyi enna-novi.  
Pek-pnevma ethmouab em-per-olf evol haroi; moi nakhlom enou-pnevma ensouti.

Je Peniot et khen ni-fee-ou-ee,  
maref-touvo nje pekran,  
mares-i nje tekmetouro,  
petehnak maref-shopi emvriti khen etfe nem hijen pikahi.  
Pen-oik ente rastif moi nan emvoou.  
Ouoh ka ni-eteron nan evol,  
emvriti hon entenko evol ennet eouon entan erou.  
Ouoh mperenten ehoun epirasmoc,  
alla nahmen evol ha pipethoo-ou.  
Khen Pi-ekhristos Isos Penchois.  
Je thok te ti-metouro nem ti-gom nem pi-oo-ou sha eneh. Amen.

Agios O Theos,  
Agios Ischyros,  
Agios Athanatos,  
Eleison imas.

Doza Patri ke Yio ke Agio Pnevmati,  
ke nin ke aei ke is tous eonas ton eonon. Amen.

Agi’a Trias eleison imas.  
Kyrie, ilasthi tais amartiais imon.  
Despota, syngchorison tas anomias imon.  
Agie, episkepsai kai iasai tas astheneias imon, eneken tou onomatos sou.

O Peniot ethoteb, through Isos Pikhristos Penchois, khen ti-metshenhēt ente Pi-epnevma Ethouab,  
ari-vethin khen pai-hwb nem pai-houit.  
Shopi nem pek-bok khen pi-mwit ente ti-aitisis nem pi-diavasis.  
Sotp eros ebol khen nai nem hirenē.  
Ari-vethin e-pai-etēm: 愿此次 YC 申请被录取，BD 顺利通过；若合乎你的圣善旨意，求你开明道路、赐下智慧、平安与正直的结果；并不求夺取他人的机会、福分或平安，惟愿一切成就都在怜悯、公义与真理中。  
Kata pek-ouōsh ethmouab, ouoh em-pi-ouōsh ente pirōmi.

Ten-tiho nem ten-tōbh evol hiten ni-eshlyl ente Ti-theotokos ethmouab Maria,  
nem pi-archangelos Mikhaēl,  
nem pi-archangelos Gabriēl,  
nem abba Markos pi-evangelistes,  
nem ni-apoctolos, ni-martyros, ni-agioc tēr-ou:  
Pchois ari-hmot nan em-pi-ko evol ente nen-novi.

Kyrie eleison. Kyrie eleison. Kyrie eleison.

Pek-ouōsh ethmouab maref-shopi;  
pek-nai maref-er-skepein ejon;  
tek-hirenē maref-areh en-nen-hit.  
Khen ou-metanoia nem ou-shephmot, ten-tiho erok, O Pi-ekhristos Pennouti.

Je thok pe pi-oo-ou nem pi-tai-o nem ti-proskynesis,  
nem Pekiot en-agathos,  
nem Pi-epnevma Ethouab enreftanḫo,  
isjen ti-nou nem sha eneh ente ni-eneh tēr-ou. Amen.

---

## 菲律宾 Iglesia ni Cristo

Amang banal, Ama naming nasa langit,  
sambahin ang pangalan Mo.

Lumapit kami sa Iyo na may pagpapakumbaba.  
Kinikilala naming Ikaw ang tunay na Diyos,  
ang Maylalang, ang nagbibigay-buhay,  
at ang tanging dapat naming sambahin.

Ama, patawarin Mo po kami sa aming mga pagkukulang,  
sa aming mga kasalanan,  
at sa anumang hindi naging kalugud-lugod sa Iyong harapan.  
Linisin Mo po ang aming puso at kalooban,  
at tulungan Mo kaming makasunod sa Iyong mga salita.

Ama naming nasa langit,  
sambahin ang pangalan mo.  
Dumating nawa ang kaharian mo.  
Sundin nawa ang loob mo,  
dito sa lupa para nang sa langit.  
Bigyan mo kami ngayon ng aming kakanin sa araw-araw.  
At patawarin mo kami sa aming mga utang,  
gaya naman namin na nagpatawad sa mga may utang sa amin.  
At huwag mo kaming ihatid sa tukso,  
kundi iligtas mo kami sa masama.

Ama, inilalapit po namin sa Iyo ang kahilingan tungkol sa YC application at sa BD.  
Kung ito po ay ayon sa Iyong kalooban,  
ipagkaloob Mo po na maging maayos ang pagsusuri,  
maging malinaw at matapat ang bawat kinakailangang hakbang,  
at mabuksan ang mabuting pagkakataon upang matanggap ang YC application  
at maging matagumpay at payapa ang pagdaan sa BD.

Patnubayan Mo po ang pag-iisip, pananalita, paghahanda, at pagpapasiya.  
Alisin Mo po ang pagkatakot, kalituhan, at anumang hadlang,  
ngunit huwag po sanang magkaroon ng kapahamakan, pagkakait,  
o pagkawala para sa kapwa.  
Nawa ang anumang tagumpay na ipagkakaloob Mo  
ay maging sa matuwid, malinis, at kapaki-pakinabang na paraan.

Idinadalangin po namin ang Iglesia,  
ang mga kapatid,  
at ang mga namumuno sa paglilingkod,  
na patuloy Mong patnubayan sa pagsunod sa Iyong kalooban.  
Ingatan Mo rin po ang sambahayan at mga kasama sa gawaing ito;  
pagkalooban Mo sila ng pagkakaisa, pagtitiis, paggalang,  
at pusong handang gumawa ng mabuti.

Hindi po ang aming sariling kalooban ang masunod,  
kundi ang kalooban Mo.  
Turuan Mo kaming magtiwala sa Iyo,  
magtiis sa kabutihan,  
magpasalamat sa lahat ng kalagayan,  
at manatiling tapat sa harap Mo.

Ikaw lamang, Ama, ang aming dinadalanginan at sinasamba;  
at ang lahat ng ito ay aming hinihiling at idinadalangin  
sa pangalan ng aming Panginoong Jesucristo.

Amen.

---

## 埃塞俄比亚 Tewahedo

Bä-səmə ʾAb wä-Wäld wä-Mänfäs Qəddus, ʾAhadu ʾAmlak. ʾAmen.

Qəddus ʾAmlak, Qəddus Ḥayl, Qəddus Ḥayw zäʾi-yəmot,  
zätäwälädä ʾəm-qəddəst Dəngəl Maryam, täsahalänä.  
Qəddus ʾAmlak, Qəddus Ḥayl, Qəddus Ḥayw zäʾi-yəmot,  
zätäṣäwwärä bəʾəntitänä, täsahalänä.  
Qəddus ʾAmlak, Qəddus Ḥayl, Qəddus Ḥayw zäʾi-yəmot,  
zätäqäbärä wä-tänśəʾa ʾəmən-mutan, täsahalänä.

ʾEgziʾo märḥänä Krəstos.  
ʾEgziʾo märḥänä Krəstos.  
ʾEgziʾo märḥänä Krəstos.

Ṣälotä haymanot:  
Näʾamən bäʾahadu ʾAmlak, ʾAb, ʾamlakä kullu,  
zägäbärä sämayat wä-mədər, zäyətarʾay wä-zäʾiyətarʾay.  
Näʾamən bäʾahadu ʾEgziʾ, Iyyäsus Krəstos, Wäldä ʾAmlak,  
Wäldä ʾAb waḥid, zətawälädä ʾəm-ʾAb qädmä kullu zämän.

Dawit:  
Täsaḥaläni ʾEgziʾo bəkämä ʿabiy məḥrätəkä,  
wä-bəkämä bəzuh rəḥrəhəkä ḥəddäg ʿamäṣaʾəya.  
ʾAṣḥəḥäni ʾəm-ʿamäṣaʾəya,  
wä-ʾəm-ḥaṭiʾatəya ʾanṣəḥäni.

ʾAntä ʾEgziʾo, ʾamlakä ʾAb wä-Wäld wä-Mänfäs Qəddus,  
ʾəntä täwäḥḥadkə bä-səmay wä-bä-mədər,  
bə-məḥrätəkä täsähal lä-ʿabdəkä.

为此次 YC 申请被录取、BD 顺利通过，求主按祂的圣意施怜悯；不夺他人所得，不损他人平安，只求公义、智慧、顺利与和平的门被开启。

ʾAy təgbar bä-kämä ḥaṭiʾatənä,  
ʾala bä-kämä rəḥrəhəkä wä-məḥrätəkä.  
ʾEgziʾo, səmaʿ ṣälotä ʿabdəkä,  
wä-ʾabṣaḥ lä-ʿabdəkä səlamäka.

Bäṣälotä qəddəst Dəngəl Maryam,  
wä-bäṣälotä qəddusan məlʾəkt,  
wä-bäṣälotä qəddusan wä-ṣadəqan,  
ʾEgziʾo, täsahalänä.

Abunä zäbä-sämayat,  
yitqäddäs səməkä;  
təmṣaʾ mängəśtəkä;  
yəkun fəqadəkä bä-kämä bä-sämay, kämä bä-mədər.  
Sisanä zä-zäntä ʿəlätä habänä yom;  
ḥədäg länä aṣəḥatänä,  
kämä nəḥna nəḥädäg lä-zä-aṣḥaḥunä;  
ʾi taʾabbanä ḫäbä mənsut,  
ʾala adḥənänä wä-ʾaḍḥənänä ʾəm-kullu ʾəkuy.  
ʾIsmä ziʾakä yəʾəti mängəśt,  
wä-ḥayl, wä-səbḥat,  
läʿaläm ʿaläm. ʾAmen.

Səbḥat läʾAb, səbḥat läWäld,  
səbḥat läMänfäs Qəddus,  
ʾəntä kämä bəqədmə ʾəgziʾ,  
wä-yəʾəti ʾəgziʾ,  
wä-yəkun läʿaläm ʿaläm. ʾAmen.

ʾEgziʾo märḥänä Krəstos;  
bə-məḥrätəkä wä-bəfəqadəkä yəkun kullu,  
wä-səlaməkä yəḥlu ʿalä kullənä. ʾAmen.

## 耶和华见证人

耶和华我们的天父，יהוה，

Πάτερ ἡμῶν ὁ ἐν τοῖς οὐρανοῖς·  
ἁγιασθήτω τὸ ὄνομά σου·  
ἐλθέτω ἡ βασιλεία σου·  
γενηθήτω τὸ θέλημά σου,  
ὡς ἐν οὐρανῷ καὶ ἐπὶ γῆς·  
τὸν ἄρτον ἡμῶν τὸν ἐπιούσιον δὸς ἡμῖν σήμερον·  
καὶ ἄφες ἡμῖν τὰ ὀφειλήματα ἡμῶν,  
ὡς καὶ ἡμεῖς ἀφήκαμεν τοῖς ὀφειλέταις ἡμῶν·  
καὶ μὴ εἰσενέγκῃς ἡμᾶς εἰς πειρασμόν,  
ἀλλὰ ῥῦσαι ἡμᾶς ἀπὸ τοῦ πονηροῦ.

愿你的名被尊为圣；愿你的王国和旨意在我们心里居首位。  
我们把此次 YC 申请和 BD 顺利通过这件事带到你面前，求你帮助我们在整个过程中保持诚实、清醒、谦卑、勤恳和爱心。  
若这件事合乎你的旨意，愿申请能被录取，BD 能顺利通过；也求你赐智慧给相关作决定的人，使他们公正、明智地判断。  
求你赐下今日所需，使所需的时间、能力、沟通、准备和机会得到妥善照顾；我们不求夺取他人的机会，也不愿损害任何人的正当益处。  
求你宽恕我们的过犯，也帮助我们以宽恕和平的态度对待别人，不因焦虑、比较或贪欲失去属灵的平衡。  
求你保护我们脱离 πονηρός，使我们不被恐惧、虚荣、不洁或不诚实的事牵引，而是继续按圣经原则行事。  
我们感谢你听祷告，也感谢你赐下圣经、会众的鼓励、日用所需和保持忠贞的力量。

耶和华，我们只向你祷告，不依靠任何圣像、护符、法术或人为的交易；愿这件事完全交在你手中，按你的旨意成就，并帮助我们无论结果如何都继续尊荣你的名。  
奉耶稣基督的名祷告，阿们。

---

## 静修主义 Hesychasm

Εἰς τὸ ὄνομα τοῦ Πατρὸς καὶ τοῦ Υἱοῦ καὶ τοῦ Ἁγίου Πνεύματος. Ἀμήν.

Δόξα σοι, ὁ Θεὸς ἡμῶν, δόξα σοι.

Κύριε Ἰησοῦ Χριστέ, Υἱὲ τοῦ Θεοῦ, ἐλέησόν με τὸν ἁμαρτωλόν.

Κύριε Ἰησοῦ Χριστέ, Υἱὲ τοῦ Θεοῦ, ἐλέησόν με τὸν ἁμαρτωλόν.

Κύριε Ἰησοῦ Χριστέ, Υἱὲ τοῦ Θεοῦ, ἐλέησόν με τὸν ἁμαρτωλόν.

为此次 YC 申请被录取、BD 顺利通过，求主怜悯。

Κύριε Ἰησοῦ Χριστέ, Υἱὲ τοῦ Θεοῦ, ἐλέησον τὴν παροῦσαν αἴτησιν.

Κύριε Ἰησοῦ Χριστέ, Υἱὲ τοῦ Θεοῦ, εὐόδωσον, εἰ συμφέρει καὶ κατὰ τὸ ἅγιόν σου θέλημα, τὴν εἴσοδον τῆς αἰτήσεως YC καὶ τὴν καλὴν διέλευσιν τοῦ BD.

Κύριε, οὐ ζητῶ ἀφελεῖν τὸ ἀγαθὸν ἄλλου, οὐδὲ βλάψαι τινά, ἀλλὰ ἐν ἀληθείᾳ, ταπεινώσει καὶ δικαιοσύνῃ πορεύεσθαι.

Κύριε Ἰησοῦ Χριστέ, Υἱὲ τοῦ Θεοῦ, ἐλέησον ἡμᾶς.

Κύριε Ἰησοῦ Χριστέ, Υἱὲ τοῦ Θεοῦ, ἐλέησόν με τὸν ἁμαρτωλόν.

Κύριε Ἰησοῦ Χριστέ, Υἱὲ τοῦ Θεοῦ, ἐλέησόν με τὸν ἁμαρτωλόν.

Φύλαξόν με, Κύριε, ἀπὸ πάσης πλάνης, κενοδοξίας καὶ φαντασίας· δίδαξόν με νήφειν, σιωπᾶν καὶ προσεύχεσθαι ἐν μετανοίᾳ, μὴ ζητοῦντα σημεῖα ἢ ὀπτασίας, ἀλλὰ μόνον τὸ ἔλεός σου.

Δόξα Πατρὶ καὶ Υἱῷ καὶ Ἁγίῳ Πνεύματι, καὶ νῦν καὶ ἀεὶ καὶ εἰς τοὺς αἰῶνας τῶν αἰώνων. Ἀμήν.

## 摩门教（LDS）

Our Father in Heaven,

We thank Thee for Thy love, Thy patience, and the opportunity to seek growth through honest work and preparation.

We acknowledge Thy Son, Jesus Christ, and seek the guidance of the Holy Ghost.

We ask Thee for blessing and direction concerning this YC application and the BD review process. Please grant clarity of mind, truthful communication, wise judgment, and favor according to Thy will. Help every step be carried out with integrity, diligence, humility, and peace.

May Thy will be done, and may this effort receive the blessing that is right before Thee, without taking away from others, harming others, or seeking success at another’s loss.

If the outcome is acceptance, help it become a means for service, stewardship, and righteous growth. If the outcome is different, help all involved receive guidance, courage, and continued opportunity.

We place this matter in Thy hands with faith in Jesus Christ, seeking the companionship of the Holy Ghost and submitting to Thy wisdom and timing.

We say these things in the name of Jesus Christ, amen.

---

## 黑人教会传统

Father God, in the name of Jesus, we come before You.

Leader:  
Lord, we thank You for waking us up, clothing us in our right mind, and keeping us by Your mercy.

People:  
Amen. Thank You, Lord.

Leader:  
We come not in our own strength, but leaning on Your everlasting arms.  
Search us, Lord; forgive us, cleanse us, and make our hearts right before You.

People:  
Lord, have mercy.

Leader:  
For this YC application, for a favorable admission result, for the BD process to pass smoothly, and for all who are standing in need of prayer, we lift our hearts to You.

Scripture:  
I will lift up mine eyes unto the hills, from whence cometh my help.  
My help cometh from the LORD, which made heaven and earth.  
He will not suffer thy foot to be moved: he that keepeth thee will not slumber.  
Behold, he that keepeth Israel shall neither slumber nor sleep.  
The LORD is thy keeper: the LORD is thy shade upon thy right hand.  
The sun shall not smite thee by day, nor the moon by night.  
The LORD shall preserve thee from all evil: he shall preserve thy soul.  
The LORD shall preserve thy going out and thy coming in from this time forth, and even for evermore.

People:  
Amen.

Spiritual:  
Guide my feet while I run this race,  
Guide my feet while I run this race,  
Guide my feet while I run this race,  
For I don’t want to run this race in vain.

Leader:  
Lord, open the right door by Your wisdom and shut every door that is not for peace.  
Give clarity to the reviewers, strength to the work, favor without pride, and patience without fear.  
Let the YC application be seen rightly, judged fairly, and received according to Your holy will.  
Let the BD process be ordered, steady, and smooth, with no confusion, no needless delay, and no harm to anyone.

We do not ask to take another person’s blessing, to dispossess another, or to prosper by another’s loss.  
We ask for daily bread, righteous opportunity, honest favor, and a table prepared by Your mercy.

People:  
Yes, Lord.

Leader:  
Where there is anxiety, speak peace.  
Where there is uncertainty, give wisdom.  
Where there is waiting, give endurance.  
Where there is a barrier, remove the obstacle without bringing harm.  
Where there is a decision, let truth, justice, and mercy stand together.

Scripture:  
The LORD is my shepherd; I shall not want.  
He maketh me to lie down in green pastures:  
he leadeth me beside the still waters.  
He restoreth my soul:  
he leadeth me in the paths of righteousness for his name’s sake.

People:  
Amen.

Leader:  
We remember the whole community before You:  
those applying, those deciding, those laboring, those waiting, those hoping, and those afraid.  
Keep hearts humble in success, faithful in delay, and comforted in every outcome.  
Let this prayer be not a bargain, but a faithful cry; not a demand, but trust in Your mercy.

People:  
Thank You, Lord.

Leader:  
Now, Lord, teach us to pray:

All:  
Our Father which art in heaven,  
Hallowed be thy name.  
Thy kingdom come.  
Thy will be done in earth, as it is in heaven.  
Give us this day our daily bread.  
And forgive us our debts, as we forgive our debtors.  
And lead us not into temptation, but deliver us from evil:  
For thine is the kingdom, and the power, and the glory, for ever.  
Amen.

Leader:  
Father, Son, and Holy Spirit, keep this prayer clean, humble, and rooted in love.  
Let praise rise without performance, let hope stand without presumption, and let faith move without fear.  
We seal this prayer in faith, not by might, nor by power, but by Your Spirit.  
In Jesus’ name.

People:  
Amen. Amen. Amen.

## Lutheran

In nomine Patris et Filii et Spiritus Sancti. Amen.

Adiutorium nostrum in nomine Domini,  
qui fecit caelum et terram.

Miserere mei, Deus, secundum misericordiam tuam;  
secundum multitudinem miserationum tuarum dele iniquitatem meam.  
Amplius lava me ab iniquitate mea,  
et a peccato meo munda me.

Kyrie eleison.  
Christe eleison.  
Kyrie eleison.

Credo in Deum Patrem omnipotentem, creatorem caeli et terrae.  
Et in Iesum Christum, Filium eius unicum, Dominum nostrum,  
qui conceptus est de Spiritu Sancto,  
natus ex Maria virgine,  
passus sub Pontio Pilato,  
crucifixus, mortuus, et sepultus,  
descendit ad inferos,  
tertia die resurrexit a mortuis,  
ascendit ad caelos,  
sedet ad dexteram Dei Patris omnipotentis,  
inde venturus est iudicare vivos et mortuos.  
Credo in Spiritum Sanctum,  
sanctam ecclesiam catholicam,  
sanctorum communionem,  
remissionem peccatorum,  
carnis resurrectionem,  
et vitam aeternam. Amen.

Pater noster, qui es in caelis,  
sanctificetur nomen tuum;  
adveniat regnum tuum;  
fiat voluntas tua,  
sicut in caelo et in terra.  
Panem nostrum quotidianum da nobis hodie;  
et dimitte nobis debita nostra,  
sicut et nos dimittimus debitoribus nostris;  
et ne nos inducas in tentationem;  
sed libera nos a malo.  
Amen.

Domine Deus, Pater caelestis,  
per Iesum Christum Filium tuum, Dominum nostrum,  
respice in misericordia super hanc petitionem:  
ut petitio ad YC, si voluntati tuae congruit, benigne admittatur,  
et res BD recte, sapienter, et pacate perficiatur.  
Non in meritis nostris confidimus,  
nec prosperitatem nostram quaerimus cum iactura aut iniuria aliorum;  
sed in sola misericordia tua et in promissione evangelii tui.

Da lucem menti, constantiam cordi,  
sermonem veracem, opus diligens,  
patientiam sub iudicio, humilitatem in successu,  
et pacem in omni eventu.  
Dirige portas quae aperiendae sunt,  
claude misericorditer quae nocitura sunt,  
et fac nos in omnibus dicere:  
fiat voluntas tua.

In manus tuas, Domine, commendamus hanc causam,  
petitionem ad YC et transitum BD;  
redemisti nos, Domine Deus veritatis.  
Per Iesum Christum, Dominum nostrum. Amen.

Benedicamus Domino.  
Deo gratias.

Benedicat nos omnipotens et misericors Dominus,  
Pater et Filius et Spiritus Sanctus. Amen.

men ‘olam w-‘adamo l-‘olam ‘olmin. Amin.

netqadash shmokh.

aykano d-bashmayo oph bar‘o.

aykano doph hnan shbaqn l-hayyobayn.

w-hab hawno shafyo, sabro, w-shayno  
b-kul medem d-methaseh l-qdamayn.

nehwe sebyonokh qadisho,

## മലങ്കര ഓർത്തഡോക്സ് സുറിയാനി സഭ

B-shem Abo w-Bro w-Ruho d-Qudsho, Hado Aloho Shariro.  
Shubho leh, w-‘alayn raḥme w-ḥanono neshtaf‘un l-‘olam ‘olmin. Amin.

Shubho l-Abo w-la-Bro w-la-Ruho d-Qudsho,  
men ‘olam w-‘adamo l-‘olam ‘olmin. Amin.

Abun d-bashmayo,  
nethqadash shmokh,  
tithe malkuthokh,  
nehwe sebyonokh,  
aykano d-bashmayo af b-ar‘o.  
Hab lan lahmo d-sunqonan yawmono.  
Washbuq lan ḥawbayn wa-ḥṭohayn,  
aykano d-af ḥnan shbaqan l-ḥayobayn.  
W-lo ta‘lan l-nesyuno,  
ella paṣṣan men bisho.  
Metol d-dilokh hi malkutho w-ḥaylo w-teshbuḥto  
l-‘olam ‘olmin. Amin.

Qadishat Aloho,  
Qadishat Ḥayelthono,  
Qadishat Lo Moyutho,  
d-ethṣlebt ḥlopayn,  
etraḥem ‘alayn.

Qadishat Aloho,  
Qadishat Ḥayelthono,  
Qadishat Lo Moyutho,  
d-ethṣlebt ḥlopayn,  
etraḥem ‘alayn.

Qadishat Aloho,  
Qadishat Ḥayelthono,  
Qadishat Lo Moyutho,  
d-ethṣlebt ḥlopayn,  
etraḥem ‘alayn.

Moran etraḥem ‘alayn.  
Moran ḥus w-raḥem ‘alayn.  
Moran ‘ani w-raḥem ‘alayn.  
Shubho lokh Moran.  
Shubho lokh Moran.  
Shubho lokh sabran l-‘olam.

Mizmor 50/51:  
Raḥem ‘alay Aloho ayk ṭaybuthokh;  
w-ayk sugo d-raḥmayk ‘ṭi ḥṭohay.  
Asgo mashigani men ‘awli,  
w-men ḥṭithi dakani.  
Meṭul d-‘awli ana yoda‘,  
w-ḥṭithi luqbalay hi b-kholzban.

Mizmor 90/91:  
D-yotheb b-sethro d-‘Elyono,  
b-ṭelolo d-Aloho nethnaga.  
Emar l-Moryo: Beth gawsī w-beth tawklanī,  
Alohi d-‘alaw tawkleth.

Moryo Aloho, b-raḥmayk qabel ṣlutho hode  
‘al bo‘utho d-YC, d-tethqabel b-shayno,  
w-‘al BD, d-net‘bar b-shayno, b-ḥekhmtho, w-b-nuhro.  
La b-zedqo d-dilan, ella b-raḥme d-dilokh,  
nṭar, ḥayel, shayen, w-nahhar  
l-kul medem d-metba‘e b-den ṣebyono ṭobo,  
b-shubḥo d-Abo w-d-Bro w-d-Ruho d-Qudsho.

Moran, nehwe sebyonokh qaddisho,  
w-lo b-ḥusrono d-akhrene,  
w-lo b-ṭelomo, w-lo b-quṭroso,  
ella b-kushṭo, b-raḥme, w-b-shayno.  
Psaḥ tar‘e d-ṭobtho,  
w-‘bar mennan men‘e w-nesyone b-lo bisho,  
ayk raḥmayk saggi’e.

Dukhrono d-Yoldath Aloho Maryam,  
w-d-qadishe kulhon,  
nehwe ‘amman l-‘olam. Amin.

Shubho l-Abo w-la-Bro w-la-Ruho d-Qudsho,  
men ‘olam w-‘adamo l-‘olam ‘olmin. Amin.  
Haleluya, Haleluya, Haleluya, shubho lokh Aloho.  
B-raḥmayk, Moran, qabel ṣluthan;  
b-sebyonokh qaddisho neth‘bed kulmedem.  
Amin.

## 贵格会（Quakers）

[Silence]

O God, Light within and beyond us,  
gather us into stillness.

The concern held before Thee is this YC application and the smooth passing of BD.  
We hold this concern in the Light.  
Let truth, peace, mercy, and faithfulness be made plain.  
May any success sought here not come by dispossessing another, diminishing another’s rightful good, or forcing any will,  
but only in the right ordering of Thy love and truth.

The true Light:  
That was the true Light, which lighteth every man that cometh into the world.

If any of you lack wisdom, let him ask of God, that giveth to all men liberally, and upbraideth not; and it shall be given him.

Likewise the Spirit also helpeth our infirmities:  
for we know not what we should pray for as we ought:  
but the Spirit itself maketh intercession for us with groanings which cannot be uttered.  
And he that searcheth the hearts knoweth what is the mind of the Spirit,  
because he maketh intercession for the saints according to the will of God.

[Silence]

Our Father which art in heaven,  
Hallowed be thy name.  
Thy kingdom come.  
Thy will be done in earth, as it is in heaven.  
Give us this day our daily bread.  
And forgive us our debts, as we forgive our debtors.  
And lead us not into temptation,  
but deliver us from evil:  
For thine is the kingdom, and the power, and the glory, for ever.  
Amen.

[Silence]

If words are given:

Lord, make us faithful in this application, this review, and this decision.  
Keep the matter in Thy Light.  
Guide what must be spoken,  
still what must be silent,  
strengthen what is true,  
release what is not rightly ordered,  
and order all steps in peace.

[Silence]

Into Thy hands we place the outcome,  
seeking clearness, faithfulness, and peace,  
not certainty of reward, but trust in Thy will.

[Silence]

---

## Ritus Hispano-Mozarabicus

V. Dominus sit semper vobiscum.  
R. Et cum spiritu tuo.

Gloria et honor Patri et Filio et Spiritui Sancto,  
in saecula saeculorum. Amen.

Psalmus:  
Qui habitat in adiutorio Altissimi,  
in protectione Dei caeli commorabitur.  
Dicet Domino: Susceptor meus es tu et refugium meum;  
Deus meus, sperabo in eum.  
Quoniam ipse liberavit me de laqueo venantium,  
et a verbo aspero.  
Scapulis suis obumbrabit tibi,  
et sub pennis eius sperabis.

Oratio admonitionis:  
Oremus, fratres carissimi, Dominum Deum omnipotentem,  
pro hac petitione et pro eventu qui dicitur YC,  
ut admissio desiderata, si voluntati eius sanctae congruit,  
benigne concedatur;  
et pro processu qui dicitur BD,  
ut sine confusione, sine fraude, sine timore inutili,  
sed cum pace, veritate et recto consilio prospere transeat.  
Non petimus aliena bona auferri,  
non honorem proximi minui,  
non vitam aut vires cuiusquam laedi;  
sed obstacula iniqua removeri,  
mentes illuminari,  
et iustum iter misericorditer aperiri.

R. Praesta, aeterne omnipotens Deus.

Alia:  
Deus, qui es refugium sperantium in te  
et fortitudo laborantium,  
respice propitius super hanc causam;  
mitte Spiritum Sanctum Paraclitum,  
ut det sapientiam in responsis, constantiam in exspectatione,  
humilitatem in prosperis, fiduciam in incertis,  
et pacem quae custodit corda in Christo Iesu.  
Dirige consilia eorum qui discernunt,  
purifica intentionem eorum qui petunt,  
et fac ut omne quod agitur  
ad iustitiam, utilitatem et caritatem proficiat;  
per Dominum nostrum Iesum Christum, Filium tuum,  
qui tecum vivit et regnat in unitate Spiritus Sancti Deus,  
per omnia saecula saeculorum.

R. Amen.

Post nomina:  
Memor esto, Domine, famulorum famularumque tuarum viventium,  
et omnium qui se orationibus Ecclesiae commendant.  
Memor esto etiam famulorum famularumque tuarum defunctorum,  
et dona eis locum refrigerii, lucis et pacis.

R. Amen.

Ad pacem:  
Pacem tuam, Domine Iesu Christe,  
quam dedisti discipulis tuis,  
conserva in nobis;  
dissolve odia, comprime scandala,  
remove a nobis ambitionem vanam et anxietatem sterilem,  
et corda nostra in caritate tua confirma.

R. Amen.

Sanctus:  
Sanctus, Sanctus, Sanctus Dominus Deus Sabaoth.  
Pleni sunt caeli et terra gloria tua.  
Hosanna in excelsis.  
Benedictus qui venit in nomine Domini.  
Hosanna in excelsis.

Pater noster:  
Pater noster, qui es in caelis:  
sanctificetur nomen tuum;  
adveniat regnum tuum;  
fiat voluntas tua, sicut in caelo et in terra.  
Panem nostrum quotidianum da nobis hodie;  
et dimitte nobis debita nostra,  
sicut et nos dimittimus debitoribus nostris;  
et ne nos inducas in tentationem;  
sed libera nos a malo. Amen.

Completuria:  
Libera nos, Domine, ab omni malo,  
praeterito, praesenti et futuro;  
intercedente sancta et gloriosa Dei Genitrice Maria,  
cum beatis apostolis et omnibus sanctis,  
da propitius pacem in diebus nostris,  
ut ope misericordiae tuae adiuti  
et a peccato simus semper liberi  
et ab omni perturbatione securi.  
Quod petitur, tuae misericordiae committimus;  
quod conceditur, tuae gloriae referimus;  
quod differtur, tuae providentiae tradimus.

R. Amen.

V. In nomine Domini nostri Iesu Christi perficiatur oratio nostra cum pace.  
R. Amen.

Custodi, Domine, fidem Ecclesiae tuae in cordibus nostris;  
serva nos in obedientia, sobrietate et caritate;  
et fac ut omnis oratio nostra,  
per Christum et in Spiritu Sancto,  
ad honorem Patris dirigatur,  
nunc et semper et in saecula saeculorum.

R. Amen.

Gloria et honor Patri et Filio et Spiritui Sancto,  
in saecula saeculorum. Amen.

## Reformed

In the name of the Father, and of the Son, and of the Holy Spirit. Amen.

Holy and triune God, Father, Son, and Holy Spirit,  
before you we bring this application, evaluation, and public decision.  
You alone are God; you alone are to be worshiped; you alone hear prayer through Jesus Christ.

Κύριε, ἐλέησον.  
Χριστέ, ἐλέησον.  
Κύριε, ἐλέησον.

Have mercy upon us according to your covenant mercy.  
We confess our anxiety, ambition, impatience, and weakness, and we do not hide our need before you.  
Cleanse, restore, govern, and keep us according to your Word.

יְהוָה רֹעִי לֹא אֶחְסָר׃  
בִּנְאוֹת דֶּשֶׁא יַרְבִּיצֵנִי עַל־מֵי מְנֻחוֹת יְנַהֲלֵנִי׃  
נַפְשִׁי יְשׁוֹבֵב יַנְחֵנִי בְמַעְגְּלֵי־צֶדֶק לְמַעַן שְׁמוֹ׃  
גַּם כִּי־אֵלֵךְ בְּגֵיא צַלְמָוֶת לֹא־אִירָא רָע כִּי־אַתָּה עִמָּדִי שִׁבְטְךָ וּמִשְׁעַנְתֶּךָ הֵמָּה יְנַחֲמֻנִי׃

O God, in your providence receive this prayer concerning this YC application and the BD review.  
Order the application process according to your will and righteousness.  
Grant clarity, diligence, truthfulness, favor in lawful ways, and a peaceful heart under your fatherly hand.  
If admission and approval are good in your sight, open the proper door and establish the work;  
if not, guide us without bitterness toward the path that better serves your kingdom and our neighbor.  
We do not seek to dispossess others, to harm competitors, or to bend any will unjustly,  
but ask only for just consideration, honest success, and provision according to your mercy.

Πάτερ ἡμῶν ὁ ἐν τοῖς οὐρανοῖς·  
ἁγιασθήτω τὸ ὄνομά σου·  
ἐλθέτω ἡ βασιλεία σου·  
γενηθήτω τὸ θέλημά σου,  
ὡς ἐν οὐρανῷ καὶ ἐπὶ γῆς·  
τὸν ἄρτον ἡμῶν τὸν ἐπιούσιον  
δὸς ἡμῖν σήμερον·  
καὶ ἄφες ἡμῖν τὰ ὀφειλήματα ἡμῶν,  
ὡς καὶ ἡμεῖς ἀφήκαμεν τοῖς ὀφειλέταις ἡμῶν·  
καὶ μὴ εἰσενέγκῃς ἡμᾶς εἰς πειρασμόν,  
ἀλλὰ ῥῦσαι ἡμᾶς ἀπὸ τοῦ πονηροῦ·  
ὅτι σοῦ ἐστιν ἡ βασιλεία  
καὶ ἡ δύναμις  
καὶ ἡ δόξα  
εἰς τοὺς αἰῶνας.  
ἀμήν.

Through Jesus Christ, our only Mediator and Advocate,  
not by bargain, charm, image, or any other power,  
but by your mercy and holy will alone,  
to whom, with the Father and the Holy Spirit,  
be glory and dominion forever. Amen.

## старообрядцы

Во имя Отца и Сына и Святаго Духа. Аминь.

Господи Исусе Христе, Сыне Божии, помилуй мя грешнаго.

Царю Небесныи, Утешителю, Душе истинныи, иже везде сыи и вся исполняя, сокровище благих и жизни подателю, прииди и вселися в ны, и очисти ны от всякия скверны, и спаси, Блаже, душа наша.

Святыи Боже, Святыи Крепкии, Святыи Безсмертныи, помилуй нас.  
Святыи Боже, Святыи Крепкии, Святыи Безсмертныи, помилуй нас.  
Святыи Боже, Святыи Крепкии, Святыи Безсмертныи, помилуй нас.

Слава Отцу и Сыну и Святому Духу, и ныне и присно и во веки веком. Аминь.

Пресвятая Троице, помилуй нас. Господи, очисти грехи наша. Владыко, прости беззакония наша. Святыи, посети и исцели немощи наша, имене Твоего ради.

Господи помилуй.  
Господи помилуй.  
Господи помилуй.

Слава Отцу и Сыну и Святому Духу, и ныне и присно и во веки веком. Аминь.

Отче наш, иже еси на небесех, да святится имя Твое, да приидет Царствие Твое, да будет воля Твоя, яко на небеси и на земли. Хлеб наш насущныи даждь нам днесь, и остави нам долги наша, якоже и мы оставляем должником нашим, и не введи нас во искушение, но избави нас от лукаваго.

Господи помилуй.  
Господи помилуй.  
Господи помилуй.

Верую во единаго Бога Отца, Вседержителя, Творца небу и земли, видимым же всем и невидимым. И во единаго Господа Исуса Христа, Сына Божия, Единороднаго, иже от Отца рожденнаго прежде всех век. Света от Света, Бога истинна от Бога истинна, рожденна, а не сотворенна, единосущна Отцу, Имже вся быша. Нас ради человек и нашего ради спасения сшедшаго с небес, и воплотившагося от Духа Свята и Марии Девы, и вочеловечшася. Распятаго же за ны при Понтийстем Пилате, и страдавша, и погребенна. И воскресшаго в третии день по Писанием. И возшедшаго на небеса, и седяща одесную Отца. И паки грядущаго со славою судити живым и мертвым, Его же Царствию несть конца. И в Духа Святаго, Господа истиннаго и животворящаго, иже от Отца исходящаго, иже со Отцем и Сыном спокланяема и сславима, глаголавшаго пророки. Во едину святую соборную и апостольскую Церковь. Исповедую едино крещение во оставление грехов. Чаю воскресения мертвым, и жизни будущаго века. Аминь.

Господи Исусе Христе, Сыне Божии, призри милостивно на сие прошение о деле предстоящем: о принятии прошения в YC и о благом прохождении BD. Настави ум, укрепи сердце, исправи слово и дело, отврати смущение и праздную боязнь, и сотвори вся по святей воле Твоей, аще полезно есть ко спасению.

Господи, не в суд и не во вред кому-либо да будет сие прошение: не да отымется у иных благо, честь, место, труд или надежда, но да устроится правдою, миром, честным деланием и Твоею милостию.

Господи Исусе Христе, Сыне Божии, благослови начало, течение и конец сего дела; подаждь рассуждение, терпение, кротость, память добрую, язык благопотребен, и избави от суетныя гордости, лукаваго помысла и неправды.

Помилуй мя, Боже, по велицей милости Твоей, и по множеству щедрот Твоих очисти беззаконие мое. Наипаче омый мя от беззакония моего, и от греха моего очисти мя.

Господи Исусе Христе, Сыне Божии, помилуй нас.  
Господи Исусе Христе, Сыне Божии, помилуй нас.  
Господи Исусе Христе, Сыне Божии, помилуй нас.

Пресвятая Богородице, спаси нас.

Достойно есть яко воистинну блажити Тя, Богородицу, присноблаженную и пренепорочную и Матерь Бога нашего. Честнейшую херувим и славнейшую воистинну серафим, без истления Бога Слова рождшую, сущую Богородицу Тя величаем.

Слава Отцу и Сыну и Святому Духу, и ныне и присно и во веки веком. Аминь.

Господи помилуй.  
Господи помилуй.  
Господи помилуй.

Господи Исусе Христе, Сыне Божии, не по хотению страстному, но по милости Твоей и святей воле Твоей устрой потребное; аще же ино есть полезнейше, вразуми, укрепи и сохрани в мире.

Господи Исусе Христе, Сыне Божии, молитв ради Пречистыя Твоея Матере и всех святых, помилуй и спаси нас, яко Благ и Человеколюбец. Аминь.

## 新使徒改革

Father God, I come before You in the name of Jesus Christ concerning this YC application and the BD process connected to it. Let Your will be done, let every step be covered by Your wisdom, and let the outcome align with Your kingdom purpose, integrity, and peace.

Πάτερ ἡμῶν ὁ ἐν τοῖς οὐρανοῖς·  
ἁγιασθήτω τὸ ὄνομά σου·  
ἐλθέτω ἡ βασιλεία σου·  
γενηθήτω τὸ θέλημά σου,  
ὡς ἐν οὐρανῷ καὶ ἐπὶ γῆς·  
τὸν ἄρτον ἡμῶν τὸν ἐπιούσιον δὸς ἡμῖν σήμερον·  
καὶ ἄφες ἡμῖν τὰ ὀφειλήματα ἡμῶν,  
ὡς καὶ ἡμεῖς ἀφήκαμεν τοῖς ὀφειλέταις ἡμῶν·  
καὶ μὴ εἰσενέγκῃς ἡμᾶς εἰς πειρασμόν,  
ἀλλὰ ῥῦσαι ἡμᾶς ἀπὸ τοῦ πονηροῦ.

Father, I confess and renounce every sin, fear, pride, striving, false agreement, anxiety, accusation, idolatry of success, ungodly vow, and unbelief connected with this application, evaluation, negotiation, communication, and BD process. I place this whole matter under the blood and lordship of Jesus Christ.

I forgive all involved and release them from my judgment. I do not curse, control, manipulate, pressure, or claim vengeance over anyone. I ask not to dispossess another person, diminish another calling, steal another opportunity, or prosper through injustice. I bless what You bless, and I reject only the works of darkness, lies, confusion, bondage, fear, pride, and oppression.

הַיֹּשֵׁב בְּסֵתֶר עֶלְיוֹן  
בְּצֵל שַׁדַּי יִתְלוֹנָן׃  
אֹמַר לַיהוָה מַחְסִי וּמְצוּדָתִי  
אֱלֹהַי אֶבְטַח־בּוֹ׃

Ἰδοὺ δέδωκα ὑμῖν τὴν ἐξουσίαν  
τοῦ πατεῖν ἐπάνω ὄφεων καὶ σκορπίων,  
καὶ ἐπὶ πᾶσαν τὴν δύναμιν τοῦ ἐχθροῦ,  
καὶ οὐδὲν ὑμᾶς οὐ μὴ ἀδικήσει.

ὃ ἐὰν δήσῃς ἐπὶ τῆς γῆς  
ἔσται δεδεμένον ἐν τοῖς οὐρανοῖς,  
καὶ ὃ ἐὰν λύσῃς ἐπὶ τῆς γῆς  
ἔσται λελυμένον ἐν τοῖς οὐρανοῖς.

Ὑποτάγητε οὖν τῷ θεῷ·  
ἀντίστητε δὲ τῷ διαβόλῳ,  
καὶ φεύξεται ἀφ᾽ ὑμῶν.

In the name of Jesus Christ, I bind every demonic assignment, accusation, spirit of fear, spirit of confusion, spirit of delay, spirit of division, spirit of deception, counterfeit opportunity, and every power of the enemy working against righteous clarity, favor, wisdom, and honest execution in this application and BD process.

In the name of Jesus Christ, I loose truth, wisdom, discernment, favor, diligence, excellence, peace, clear communication, righteous alignment, proper timing, integrity, and obedience to the will of God. Where doors should open, let them open by Your hand; where doors should close, let them close in peace and without confusion.

I cut off every ungodly soul tie, false burden, fear agreement, spoken curse, inner vow, striving identity, and demonic access point connected with this matter. I declare that every handwriting against this matter is canceled in Christ, and that every hostile power is disarmed under the cross of Jesus Christ.

Καὶ αὐτοὶ ἐνίκησαν αὐτὸν  
διὰ τὸ αἷμα τοῦ ἀρνίου  
καὶ διὰ τὸν λόγον τῆς μαρτυρίας αὐτῶν.

Father, cover this process with the Holy Spirit, the peace of Christ, the fear of the Lord, wisdom, purity, courage, humility, and steadfast love. Establish Your kingdom order in every interview, review, email, call, decision, diligence step, business conversation, and final outcome.

I thank You, Father, and seal this prayer in the name of Jesus Christ. Keep every word of this prayer submitted to Your will, Your mercy, and Your Scripture. Let no word become fear, compulsion, control, accusation, or harm toward any person; let every resistant force named here be only sin, lies, bondage, and the works of darkness. If my heart turns toward fear, striving, bitterness, or pressure, lead me back to repentance, forgiveness, wise counsel, peace, and trust in You.

Ἀμήν.

---

## 五旬节派

天父，奉主耶稣基督的名，我们来到你面前，称颂你是圣洁、信实、满有怜悯的父。

Πάτερ ἡμῶν ὁ ἐν τοῖς οὐρανοῖς·  
ἁγιασθήτω τὸ ὄνομά σου·  
ἐλθέτω ἡ βασιλεία σου·  
γενηθήτω τὸ θέλημά σου,  
ὡς ἐν οὐρανῷ καὶ ἐπὶ γῆς·  
τὸν ἄρτον ἡμῶν τὸν ἐπιούσιον δὸς ἡμῖν σήμερον·  
καὶ ἄφες ἡμῖν τὰ ὀφειλήματα ἡμῶν,  
ὡς καὶ ἡμεῖς ἀφήκαμεν τοῖς ὀφειλέταις ἡμῶν·  
καὶ μὴ εἰσενέγκῃς ἡμᾶς εἰς πειρασμόν,  
ἀλλὰ ῥῦσαι ἡμᾶς ἀπὸ τοῦ πονηροῦ.

主耶稣基督，我们承认自己的软弱、焦虑、骄傲与有限；愿顺服你的话语，不以祷告辖制他人，不以成功夺取他人机会，不求损害他人，只求在公义、诚实与怜悯中成就你的旨意。

καὶ ἐπλήσθησαν πάντες πνεύματος ἁγίου  
καὶ ἤρξαντο λαλεῖν ἑτέραις γλώσσαις  
καθὼς τὸ πνεῦμα ἐδίδου ἀποφθέγγεσθαι αὐτοῖς.

圣灵，请照父的旨意帮助我们祷告；若你感动人以方言祷告，愿一切都在敬畏、爱心、秩序、解释与辨别之中，不凭肉体夸口，只愿基督得荣耀。

τὸ πνεῦμα συναντιλαμβάνεται τῇ ἀσθενείᾳ ἡμῶν·  
τὸ γὰρ τί προσευξώμεθα καθὸ δεῖ οὐκ οἴδαμεν,  
ἀλλὰ αὐτὸ τὸ πνεῦμα ὑπερεντυγχάνει στεναγμοῖς ἀλαλήτοις.

为此次 YC 申请被录取、BD 顺利通过，我们奉耶稣基督的名祈求：求你赐下清明的心、合宜的表达、真实的智慧、良好的判断、稳定的状态与平安的道路；若这门为你所开，求你使过程顺利、审查蒙恩、结果合宜；若你另有安排，求你也赐下顺服、忍耐与更好的引导。

求主保守这件事脱离恐惧、混乱、欺骗、控告与一切不合真理的捆绑；使相关的准备、沟通、材料、面试或审查都在诚实与光明中进行。我们不奉耶稣之名咒诅任何人，也不求任何竞争者受损，只求你按公义与恩典带领。

τοῦ λοιποῦ ἐνδυναμοῦσθε ἐν κυρίῳ  
καὶ ἐν τῷ κράτει τῆς ἰσχύος αὐτοῦ·  
ἐνδύσασθε τὴν πανοπλίαν τοῦ θεοῦ.

愿此次申请与通过的结果交在你手中；不是凭人的夸口，也不是凭强迫性的宣告，乃凭主的怜悯、圣经的真理与圣灵的见证。求你赐胆量、平安、节制与爱，使人在等待中不失信心，在结果中不失谦卑。

πάντα δὲ εὐσχημόνως καὶ κατὰ τάξιν γινέσθω.  
νυνὶ δὲ μένει πίστις, ἐλπίς, ἀγάπη, τὰ τρία ταῦτα·  
μείζων δὲ τούτων ἡ ἀγάπη.

圣父、圣子、圣灵，愿一切恩赐归于爱，一切祷告归于顺服，一切结果归于你的荣耀。奉耶稣基督的名祷告。阿们。

---

## Santa Muerte 信仰

En el nombre del Padre, y del Hijo, y del Espíritu Santo. Amén.

Creo en Dios, Padre todopoderoso,  
Creador del cielo y de la tierra.  
Creo en Jesucristo, su único Hijo, nuestro Señor,  
que fue concebido por obra y gracia del Espíritu Santo,  
nació de Santa María Virgen,  
padeció bajo el poder de Poncio Pilato,  
fue crucificado, muerto y sepultado,  
descendió a los infiernos,  
al tercer día resucitó de entre los muertos,  
subió a los cielos  
y está sentado a la derecha de Dios, Padre todopoderoso.  
Desde allí ha de venir a juzgar a vivos y muertos.  
Creo en el Espíritu Santo,  
la santa Iglesia católica,  
la comunión de los santos,  
el perdón de los pecados,  
la resurrección de la carne  
y la vida eterna. Amén.

Santísima Muerte, Niña Blanca, Señora de la balanza y de la guadaña,  
ante ti nombro mi petición: que esta solicitud a YC sea recibida con favor,  
que sea aceptada si conviene al bien, a la justicia y a la paz,  
y que el BD sea aprobado y pase sin tropiezo injusto.

Que esta oración no sea para daño injusto,  
ni para forzar voluntad ajena,  
ni para quebrantar la ley de Dios.  
No pido quitar mérito, lugar, sustento, salud ni vida a nadie;  
pido que se abra el camino recto,  
que se quite el obstáculo, la confusión, el error y la mala sombra.

Padre nuestro que estás en el cielo,  
santificado sea tu Nombre;  
venga a nosotros tu reino;  
hágase tu voluntad en la tierra como en el cielo.  
Danos hoy nuestro pan de cada día;  
perdona nuestras ofensas,  
como también nosotros perdonamos a los que nos ofenden;  
no nos dejes caer en la tentación,  
y líbranos del mal. Amén.

Dios te salve, María,  
llena eres de gracia;  
el Señor es contigo.  
Bendita tú eres entre todas las mujeres,  
y bendito es el fruto de tu vientre, Jesús.  
Santa María, Madre de Dios,  
ruega por nosotros, pecadores,  
ahora y en la hora de nuestra muerte. Amén.

Gloria al Padre, y al Hijo, y al Espíritu Santo.  
Como era en el principio, ahora y siempre,  
por los siglos de los siglos. Amén.

Santísima Muerte,  
por la hora cierta y por la verdad de la muerte,  
escucha esta súplica:  
guía esta aplicación a YC hacia manos justas y entendimiento claro;  
que lo bueno sea visto, que lo necesario sea completado,  
que el BD avance con orden, aprobación y buen término.  
Si hay error, que sea corregido;  
si hay duda, que sea aclarada;  
si hay puerta legítima, que se abra en paz.

Santa Muerte de mi corazón,  
no me desampares de tu protección.  
Amén.

Santísima Muerte, ruega por nosotros.  
Santísima Muerte, acompaña este camino.  
Santísima Muerte, guarda este proceso de YC y BD.  
Santísima Muerte, corta lo que sea mal, engaño, soberbia, pérdida o confusión.  
Santísima Muerte, recibe mi gratitud sincera,  
mi respeto y mi oración sin amenaza, sin burla y sin trato de deuda.

Padre nuestro que estás en el cielo,  
santificado sea tu Nombre;  
venga a nosotros tu reino;  
hágase tu voluntad en la tierra como en el cielo.  
Danos hoy nuestro pan de cada día;  
perdona nuestras ofensas,  
como también nosotros perdonamos a los que nos ofenden;  
no nos dejes caer en la tentación,  
y líbranos del mal. Amén.

Dios te salve, María,  
llena eres de gracia;  
el Señor es contigo.  
Bendita tú eres entre todas las mujeres,  
y bendito es el fruto de tu vientre, Jesús.  
Santa María, Madre de Dios,  
ruega por nosotros, pecadores,  
ahora y en la hora de nuestra muerte. Amén.

Gloria al Padre, y al Hijo, y al Espíritu Santo.  
Como era en el principio, ahora y siempre,  
por los siglos de los siglos. Amén.

Santísima Muerte,  
si esta petición conviene al bien,  
a la justicia y a la paz,  
que sea encaminada sin daño injusto.  
Si no conviene,  
aparta de mí el error, la soberbia, la ansiedad y la mala voluntad.  
Cubre este asunto con calma, claridad, protección y rectitud;  
corta solamente el mal camino, no la vida ni el bien de persona alguna.  
Recibe esta oración por la aceptación de esta solicitud a YC  
y por la aprobación del BD,  
con gratitud, humildad y paz.

Santa Muerte de mi corazón,  
no me desampares de tu protección.  
Líbrame del miedo, de la prisa ciega, del engaño y de la mala decisión;  
guárdame en camino limpio, palabra honesta y ánimo sereno.  
Que todo quede en manos de Dios,  
sin daño, sin violencia, sin injusticia y sin deuda de promesa. Amén.

En el nombre del Padre, y del Hijo, y del Espíritu Santo. Amén.

---

## 东正教 圣礼礼仪派

Εὐλογημένη ἡ βασιλεία τοῦ Πατρὸς καὶ τοῦ Υἱοῦ καὶ τοῦ Ἁγίου Πνεύματος, νῦν καὶ ἀεὶ καὶ εἰς τοὺς αἰῶνας τῶν αἰώνων.  
Ἀμήν.

Βασιλεῦ οὐράνιε, Παράκλητε, τὸ Πνεῦμα τῆς ἀληθείας, ὁ πανταχοῦ παρὼν καὶ τὰ πάντα πληρῶν, ὁ θησαυρὸς τῶν ἀγαθῶν καὶ ζωῆς χορηγός, ἐλθὲ καὶ σκήνωσον ἐν ἡμῖν, καὶ καθάρισον ἡμᾶς ἀπὸ πάσης κηλῖδος, καὶ σῶσον, Ἀγαθέ, τὰς ψυχὰς ἡμῶν.

Ἅγιος ὁ Θεός, Ἅγιος Ἰσχυρός, Ἅγιος Ἀθάνατος, ἐλέησον ἡμᾶς.  
Ἅγιος ὁ Θεός, Ἅγιος Ἰσχυρός, Ἅγιος Ἀθάνατος, ἐλέησον ἡμᾶς.  
Ἅγιος ὁ Θεός, Ἅγιος Ἰσχυρός, Ἅγιος Ἀθάνατος, ἐλέησον ἡμᾶς.

Δόξα Πατρὶ καὶ Υἱῷ καὶ Ἁγίῳ Πνεύματι, καὶ νῦν καὶ ἀεὶ καὶ εἰς τοὺς αἰῶνας τῶν αἰώνων. Ἀμήν.

Παναγία Τριάς, ἐλέησον ἡμᾶς· Κύριε, ἱλάσθητι ταῖς ἁμαρτίαις ἡμῶν· Δέσποτα, συγχώρησον τὰς ἀνομίας ἡμῖν· Ἅγιε, ἐπίσκεψαι καὶ ἴασαι τὰς ἀσθενείας ἡμῶν, ἕνεκεν τοῦ ὀνόματός σου.

Κύριε, ἐλέησον. Κύριε, ἐλέησον. Κύριε, ἐλέησον.

Πάτερ ἡμῶν ὁ ἐν τοῖς οὐρανοῖς· ἁγιασθήτω τὸ ὄνομά σου· ἐλθέτω ἡ βασιλεία σου· γενηθήτω τὸ θέλημά σου, ὡς ἐν οὐρανῷ καὶ ἐπὶ τῆς γῆς· τὸν ἄρτον ἡμῶν τὸν ἐπιούσιον δὸς ἡμῖν σήμερον· καὶ ἄφες ἡμῖν τὰ ὀφειλήματα ἡμῶν, ὡς καὶ ἡμεῖς ἀφίεμεν τοῖς ὀφειλέταις ἡμῶν· καὶ μὴ εἰσενέγκῃς ἡμᾶς εἰς πειρασμόν, ἀλλὰ ῥῦσαι ἡμᾶς ἀπὸ τοῦ πονηροῦ.

Ἐλέησόν με, ὁ Θεός, κατὰ τὸ μέγα ἔλεός σου, καὶ κατὰ τὸ πλῆθος τῶν οἰκτιρμῶν σου ἐξάλειψον τὸ ἀνόμημά μου.  
Ἐπὶ πλεῖον πλῦνόν με ἀπὸ τῆς ἀνομίας μου, καὶ ἀπὸ τῆς ἁμαρτίας μου καθάρισόν με.  
Ὅτι τὴν ἀνομίαν μου ἐγὼ γινώσκω, καὶ ἡ ἁμαρτία μου ἐνώπιόν μού ἐστι διὰ παντός.

Ἐν εἰρήνῃ τοῦ Κυρίου δεηθῶμεν.  
Κύριε, ἐλέησον.

Ὑπὲρ τῆς ἄνωθεν εἰρήνης καὶ τῆς σωτηρίας τῶν ψυχῶν ἡμῶν, τοῦ Κυρίου δεηθῶμεν.  
Κύριε, ἐλέησον.

Ὑπὲρ τῆς εἰρήνης τοῦ σύμπαντος κόσμου, εὐσταθείας τῶν ἁγίων τοῦ Θεοῦ ἐκκλησιῶν, καὶ τῆς τῶν πάντων ἑνώσεως, τοῦ Κυρίου δεηθῶμεν.  
Κύριε, ἐλέησον.

Ὑπὲρ τοῦ δεχθῆναι τὴν αἴτησιν YC, καὶ τοῦ εὐοδωθῆναι τὴν διάβασιν BD ἐν εἰρήνῃ, σωφροσύνῃ, ἀληθείᾳ καὶ ἀγαθῇ ἐλπίδι, τοῦ Κυρίου δεηθῶμεν.  
Κύριε, ἐλέησον.

Ὑπὲρ τοῦ φωτισθῆναι τὸν νοῦν, κραταιωθῆναι τὴν καρδίαν, καὶ ὀρθῶς ἀποκριθῆναι ἐν παντὶ πράγματι τῆς αἰτήσεως, τοῦ Κυρίου δεηθῶμεν.  
Κύριε, ἐλέησον.

Ὑπὲρ τοῦ ἀνοίξαι ὁ Κύριος θύραν συμφέρουσαν πρὸς σωτηρίαν, ἐὰν ᾖ τὸ θέλημα αὐτοῦ τὸ ἅγιον, καὶ τοῦ ἀπαλλάξαι ἡμᾶς ἀπὸ συγχύσεως, φόβου, κενοδοξίας καὶ πάσης ἀδικίας, τοῦ Κυρίου δεηθῶμεν.  
Κύριε, ἐλέησον.

Οὐ ζητοῦμεν βλάβην ἢ στέρησιν ἑτέρων, οὐδὲ ἀρπαγὴν ξένου κόπου, ἀλλὰ ἔλεος, δικαιοσύνην, εἰρήνην καὶ τὸ συμφέρον τῆς ψυχῆς, τοῦ Κυρίου δεηθῶμεν.  
Κύριε, ἐλέησον.

Ἀντιλαβοῦ, σῶσον, ἐλέησον καὶ διαφύλαξον ἡμᾶς, ὁ Θεός, τῇ σῇ χάριτι.  
Κύριε, ἐλέησον.

Τῆς Παναγίας, ἀχράντου, ὑπερευλογημένης, ἐνδόξου Δεσποίνης ἡμῶν Θεοτόκου καὶ ἀειπαρθένου Μαρίας, μετὰ πάντων τῶν ἁγίων μνημονεύσαντες, ἑαυτοὺς καὶ ἀλλήλους καὶ πᾶσαν τὴν ζωὴν ἡμῶν Χριστῷ τῷ Θεῷ παραθώμεθα.  
Σοί, Κύριε.

Ὁ κατοικῶν ἐν βοηθείᾳ τοῦ Ὑψίστου, ἐν σκέπῃ τοῦ Θεοῦ τοῦ οὐρανοῦ αὐλισθήσεται.  
Ἐρεῖ τῷ Κυρίῳ· Ἀντιλήπτωρ μου εἶ καὶ καταφυγή μου, ὁ Θεός μου, καὶ ἐλπιῶ ἐπ’ αὐτόν.  
Ὅτι αὐτὸς ῥύσεταί σε ἐκ παγίδος θηρευτῶν καὶ ἀπὸ λόγου ταραχώδους.

Κύριε Ἰησοῦ Χριστέ, ὁ Θεὸς ἡμῶν, ὁδὸν εἰρήνης καὶ σωτηρίας χάρισαι ἐν τῷ πράγματι τῆς αἰτήσεως YC καὶ τῆς διαβάσεως BD· φύλαξον ἀπὸ πάσης θλίψεως, ὀργῆς, κινδύνου καὶ ἀνάγκης· δίδου ταπείνωσιν, διάκρισιν, ἐπιμέλειαν καὶ καθαρὰν προαίρεσιν, ἵνα πᾶν τὸ γενόμενον γένηται πρὸς δόξαν σου καὶ πρὸς ὠφέλειαν τῶν ψυχῶν.

Ὑπεραγία Θεοτόκε, σῶσον ἡμᾶς.  
Πάντες οἱ ἅγιοι, πρεσβεύσατε ὑπὲρ ἡμῶν.

Δόξα σοι, Χριστὲ ὁ Θεὸς ἡμῶν, ἡ ἐλπὶς ἡμῶν, δόξα σοι.

Κύριε, ἐλέησον. Κύριε, ἐλέησον. Κύριε, ἐλέησον.

Δι’ εὐχῶν τῶν ἁγίων Πατέρων ἡμῶν, Κύριε Ἰησοῦ Χριστέ, ὁ Θεὸς ἡμῶν, ἐλέησον καὶ σῶσον ἡμᾶς.  
Ἀμήν.

## 罗马天主教 · 圣礼神学派

In nomine Patris, et Filii, et Spiritus Sancti. Amen.

Deus, in adiutorium meum intende.  
Domine, ad adiuvandum me festina.  
Gloria Patri, et Filio, et Spiritui Sancto.  
Sicut erat in principio, et nunc, et semper, et in saecula saeculorum. Amen.

Confiteor Deo omnipotenti,  
beatae Mariae semper Virgini,  
beato Michaeli Archangelo,  
beato Ioanni Baptistae,  
sanctis Apostolis Petro et Paulo,  
omnibus Sanctis,  
et vobis, fratres,  
quia peccavi nimis cogitatione, verbo et opere:  
mea culpa, mea culpa, mea maxima culpa.  
Ideo precor beatam Mariam semper Virginem,  
beatum Michaelem Archangelum,  
beatum Ioannem Baptistam,  
sanctos Apostolos Petrum et Paulum,  
omnes Sanctos,  
et vos, fratres,  
orare pro me ad Dominum Deum nostrum.

Misereatur nostri omnipotens Deus,  
et dimissis peccatis nostris,  
perducat nos ad vitam aeternam. Amen.

Kyrie, eleison.  
Christe, eleison.  
Kyrie, eleison.

Domine Iesu Christe, Fili Dei vivi,  
qui dixisti: “Petite, et dabitur vobis; quaerite, et invenietis; pulsate, et aperietur vobis,”  
respice propitius super hanc intentionem:  
ut applicatio YC, si tuae sanctae voluntati congruit, admittatur,  
et probatio BD recte, honeste, pacifice atque prospere transeat.  
Da lumen menti, constantiam cordi, ordinem operibus,  
veritatem in verbis, humilitatem in exspectatione,  
et fiduciam in providentia tua.

Pater noster, qui es in caelis,  
sanctificetur nomen tuum.  
Adveniat regnum tuum.  
Fiat voluntas tua,  
sicut in caelo et in terra.  
Panem nostrum quotidianum da nobis hodie.  
Et dimitte nobis debita nostra,  
sicut et nos dimittimus debitoribus nostris.  
Et ne nos inducas in tentationem:  
sed libera nos a malo. Amen.

Ave Maria, gratia plena, Dominus tecum.  
Benedicta tu in mulieribus,  
et benedictus fructus ventris tui, Iesus.  
Sancta Maria, Mater Dei,  
ora pro nobis peccatoribus,  
nunc et in hora mortis nostrae. Amen.

Sub tuum praesidium confugimus,  
sancta Dei Genetrix;  
nostras deprecationes ne despicias in necessitatibus,  
sed a periculis cunctis libera nos semper,  
Virgo gloriosa et benedicta.

Veni, Creator Spiritus,  
mentes tuorum visita,  
imple superna gratia  
quae tu creasti pectora.

Qui diceris Paraclitus,  
altissimi donum Dei,  
fons vivus, ignis, caritas,  
et spiritalis unctio.

Tu septiformis munere,  
digitus paternae dexterae,  
tu rite promissum Patris,  
sermone ditans guttura.

Accende lumen sensibus,  
infunde amorem cordibus,  
infirma nostri corporis  
virtute firmans perpeti.

Hostem repellas longius,  
pacemque dones protinus;  
ductore sic te praevio  
vitemus omne noxium.

Per te sciamus da Patrem,  
noscamus atque Filium,  
teque utriusque Spiritum  
credamus omni tempore.

Deo Patri sit gloria,  
et Filio qui a mortuis  
surrexit, ac Paraclito,  
in saeculorum saecula. Amen.

Angele Dei,  
qui custos es mei,  
me tibi commissum pietate superna,  
illumina, custodi, rege et guberna. Amen.

Domine Deus, Pater misericordiarum,  
non quaerimus lucrum iniustum,  
non petimus ut aliis auferatur bonum, dignitas, meritum, locus aut pax;  
sed petimus gratiam recte agendi,  
ostia iusta aperiri,  
impedimenta sine iniuria removeri,  
et eventum huius negotii ad veritatem, caritatem et bonum commune ordinari.

Si haec admissio YC et probatio BD prosunt saluti, vocationi et honestis laboribus,  
dirige corda iudicantium ad aequitatem,  
conserva tranquillitatem in tempore exspectationis,  
et concede ut omnia fiant non secundum superbiam nostram,  
sed secundum sapientiam et misericordiam tuam.

Sancte Ioseph, custos fidelis et operarius iustus,  
ora pro nobis,  
ut in labore, consilio et probatione  
simpliciter, prudenter et fideliter ambulemus.

Sancte Michael Archangele,  
defende nos in proelio;  
contra nequitiam et insidias diaboli esto praesidium.  
Imperet illi Deus, supplices deprecamur:  
tuque, Princeps militiae caelestis,  
Satanam aliosque spiritus malignos,  
qui ad perditionem animarum pervagantur in mundo,  
divina virtute in infernum detrude. Amen.

Requiem aeternam dona eis, Domine,  
et lux perpetua luceat eis.  
Requiescant in pace. Amen.

Pro omnibus applicantibus, examinatoribus, ministris et iudicibus,  
pro iis qui timent, laborant, exspectant aut deficiunt,  
da, Domine, pacem, iustitiam, patientiam et lumen.  
Nullus confundatur iniuste;  
nullus opprimatur fraude;  
omnes ad veritatem et bonum ducantur.

Gloria Patri, et Filio, et Spiritui Sancto.  
Sicut erat in principio, et nunc, et semper,  
et in saecula saeculorum. Amen.

Domine Iesu Christe,  
hanc petitionem non ponimus quasi pretium, artem aut necessitatem,  
sed ut supplicationem pauperem coram misericordia tua.  
Purifica intentiones nostras ab omni superstitione, vana fiducia et cupiditate;  
coniunge nos Ecclesiae tuae, sacramentis tuis et voluntati Patris;  
et quidquid largiri dignaris, fac nos accipere cum gratiarum actione,  
quidquid autem differs vel negas, fac nos portare cum fide et pace.

Per Christum Dominum nostrum. Amen.  
In nomine Patris, et Filii, et Spiritus Sancti. Amen.

## ܥܕܬܐ ܣܘܪܝܝܬܐ ܬܪܝܨܬ ܫܘܒܚܐ

B-shmo d-Abo w-d-Bro w-d-Ruḥo d-Qudsho, ḥad Aloho sharirho. Amin.

Shubḥo l-Abo w-la-Bro w-la-Ruḥo d-Qudsho,  
men ‘olam w-‘dammo l-‘olam ‘olmin. Amin.

Qadishat Aloho,  
Qadishat Ḥayelthono,  
Qadishat Lo Moyutho,  
d-etslebt hlofayn,  
ethraḥam ‘layn.

Qadishat Aloho,  
Qadishat Ḥayelthono,  
Qadishat Lo Moyutho,  
d-etslebt hlofayn,  
ethraḥam ‘layn.

Qadishat Aloho,  
Qadishat Ḥayelthono,  
Qadishat Lo Moyutho,  
d-etslebt hlofayn,  
ethraḥam ‘layn.

Moran ethraḥam ‘layn.  
Moran ḥus w-raḥem ‘layn.  
Moran qabel tashmeshton w-tsloton, w-ethraḥam ‘layn.

Shubḥo lokh Aloho.  
Shubḥo lokh Boruyon.  
Shubḥo lokh Malko Mshiḥo,  
d-ḥos ‘al ḥaṭoye ‘abdayk. Barekhmor.

Abun d-bashmayo,  
netqadash shmokh.  
Tithe malkuthokh.  
Nehwe sebyonokh,  
aykano d-bashmayo af b-ar‘o.  
Hav lan lahmo d-sunqonan yawmono.  
Washbuq lan ḥawbayn waḥṭohayn,  
aykano d-af ḥnan shbaqan l-ḥayobayn.  
W-la ta‘lan l-nesyuno,  
elo faṣṣon men bisho.  
Metul d-dilokh hi malkutho  
w-ḥaylo w-teshbuḥto,  
l-‘olam ‘olmin. Amin.

Raḥem ‘lay Aloho ayk ṭaybuthokh,  
w-ayk sugo d-raḥmayk ‘ti ḥawbay.  
Asga mashig li men ‘awli,  
w-men ḥṭithi dakani.

Lebbo dakhyo bro bi Aloho,  
w-ruḥo triso ḥaddeth b-gawi.  
Lo tashdini men qdomayk,  
w-ruḥokh qadisho lo teshqol menni.

Moran Yeshu Mshiḥo,  
Bro d-Aloho ḥayo,  
ḥus w-raḥem ‘layn b-raḥmayk saggi’e.  
Qabel bo‘utho hode,  
d-tehwe qabolto d-ba‘utho d-YC  
ayk sebyonokh qadisho,  
w-d-ne‘bar BD b-shayno, b-sukkolo,  
w-b-‘udrono d-Ruḥo d-Qudsho.

Nahhar tar‘e d-madda‘,  
sharriq ‘al orḥo ṭobto,  
šadar ḥekhmtho w-saybro,  
w-‘bed lan fursono d-shayno.  
Lo b-ḥsoro d-aḥrone,  
lo b-nukro d-ṭaybutho d-ḥabre,  
elo b-kheno, b-qushto,  
w-b-raḥme d-men lokh.

Moran, nuṭar hode ṣbutho  
men šubho riqono, men deḥlo,  
men ṭu‘yo, w-men kol nesyuno.  
Haw lan lebbo makikho,  
melta triso,  
w-yad‘to d-na‘bed ṣebyono d-ṭoybutho.

Bo‘utho d-Mor Ya‘qub:  
Moran ethraḥam ‘layn,  
w-‘adar lan b-raḥmayk.  
Moran qabel bo‘uthan,  
w-‘bed ‘amman ṭaybutho.

Ethdakar Moran kolhon aylen d-mṣalen ‘amman,  
w-kolhon aylen d-ḥsirin ‘udrono.  
Shadar shayno ‘al ‘idtokh qadishto,  
‘al ro‘awotheh, kohneh,  
w-‘al kol ‘amokh d-mhaymne.

Shubḥo l-Abo w-la-Bro w-la-Ruḥo d-Qudsho,  
men ‘olam w-‘dammo l-‘olam ‘olmin. Amin.

Moran Yeshu Mshiḥo,  
b-tsloth d-yoldathokh Maryam,  
w-d-mal’akhe w-qadishayk,  
tehwe shuro w-beth gawso lan.  
Qayem lan b-sidro d-‘idto qadishto,  
b-makikhutho w-b-nuṭoro d-ṣlibokh,  
w-la teshboq lan d-netṭ‘e men orḥo d-shayno.

Qurielaison. Qurielaison. Qurielaison.

## Pabása ng Pasyón

Sa ngalan ng Ama, at ng Anak, at ng Espiritu Santo. Amen.

Sumasampalataya ako sa Diyos Amang makapangyarihan sa lahat,  
na may gawa ng langit at lupa.  
Sumasampalataya naman ako kay Hesukristo,  
iisang Anak ng Diyos, Panginoon nating lahat.  
Nagkatawang-tao Siya lalang ng Espiritu Santo,  
ipinanganak ni Santa Mariang Birhen.  
Pinagpakasakit ni Poncio Pilato,  
ipinako sa krus, namatay, inilibing.  
Nanaog sa kinaroroonan ng mga yumao.  
Nang may ikatlong araw nabuhay na mag-uli.  
Umakyat sa langit.  
Naluluklok sa kanan ng Diyos Amang makapangyarihan sa lahat.  
Doon magmumula at paririto upang hukuman  
ang nangabubuhay at nangamatay na tao.  
Sumasampalataya naman ako sa Diyos Espiritu Santo,  
sa banal na Simbahang Katolika,  
sa kasamahan ng mga banal,  
sa kapatawaran ng mga kasalanan,  
sa pagkabuhay na mag-uli ng nangamatay na tao,  
at sa buhay na walang hanggan. Amen.

Ama namin, sumasalangit Ka,  
sambahin ang ngalan Mo.  
Mapasaamin ang kaharian Mo.  
Sundin ang loob Mo dito sa lupa para nang sa langit.  
Bigyan Mo kami ngayon ng aming kakanin sa araw-araw.  
At patawarin Mo kami sa aming mga sala,  
para nang pagpapatawad namin sa nagkakasala sa amin.  
At huwag Mo kaming ipahintulot sa tukso,  
at iadya Mo kami sa lahat ng masama. Amen.

Aba Ginoong Maria, napupuno ka ng grasya,  
ang Panginoong Diyos ay sumasaiyo.  
Bukod kang pinagpala sa babaeng lahat,  
at pinagpala naman ang iyong Anak na si Jesus.  
Santa Maria, Ina ng Diyos,  
ipanalangin mo kaming makasalanan,  
ngayon at kung kami'y mamamatay. Amen.

Luwalhati sa Ama, at sa Anak, at sa Espiritu Santo.  
Kapara noong unang-una, ngayon at magpakailanman,  
magpasawalang hanggan. Amen.

Panginoong Hesukristo, Anak ng Diyos na buhay,  
iniaalay namin ang pagbabasá ng Pasyón na ito  
bilang mapagpakumbabang panalangin at pasasalamat,  
para sa aplikasyong ito sa YC,  
na kung naaayon sa Iyong banal na kalooban  
ay matanggap nawa at magbunga ng mabuti,  
at para sa BD,  
na maging maayos, maliwanag, at payapang makaraos.  
Hindi kami humihingi ng biyayang aagaw sa kapwa,  
ni tagumpay na makapipinsala o makapagpapababa sa iba;  
ang hinihiling namin ay liwanag, katapatan, tiyaga,  
at pagbubukas ng landas ayon sa Iyong awa.  
Panginoong Hesukristo, maawa Ka sa amin.

Casaysayan nang Pasiong Mahal ni Jesucristong Panginoon Natin.

O Dios sa calangitan,  
Hari nang sangcalupaan,  
Dios na ualang capantay,  
maguing sa langit at lupa man.

Sumasamba caming tunay,  
sa mahal mong camahalan;  
loobin mong dinggin naman,  
aming abang dalanginan.

Panginoong Hesukristo, maawa Ka sa amin.  
Panginoong Hesukristo, maawa Ka sa amin.  
Panginoong Hesukristo, maawa Ka sa amin.

Sa paglikha Mong banal, Panginoon,  
itinindig Mo ang tao sa Iyong habag;  
sa pagkahulog nami’y hindi Mo kami iniwan,  
kundi ipinangako Mo ang Tagapagligtas.  
Sa pagkakatawang-tao ng Iyong Anak,  
sa ministeryo Niyang puspos ng awa,  
sa huling hapunan at paghuhugas ng paa,  
sa panalangin sa halamanan,  
sa pagkakadena, paghatol, at pagpasan ng krus,  
sa pagkamatay sa Kalbaryo,  
sa paglilibing, at sa muling pagkabuhay,  
ipakita Mo sa amin ang daang hindi nalilito,  
ang pag-asa na hindi nasisira,  
at ang kapayapaang hindi nakasalalay sa takot.

Panginoong Hesukristo, Anak ng Diyos na buhay,  
sa Iyong mahal na Pasyón,  
sa Iyong krus at pagkamatay,  
sa Iyong paglilibing at muling pagkabuhay,  
kaawaan Mo kami,  
patawarin Mo ang aming mga sala,  
at tanggapin Mo ang aming panalangin  
para sa aplikasyong ito sa YC  
at para sa maayos na pagdaan sa BD.  
Kung may balakid, alisin Mo ito nang walang kapahamakan sa kapwa;  
kung may pagkukulang, turuan Mo kami ng karunungan;  
kung may pintuang nararapat buksan, buksan Mo sa Iyong panahon;  
kung may dapat tanggapin, bigyan Mo kami ng lakas at kapayapaan.

Ama namin, sumasalangit Ka,  
sambahin ang ngalan Mo.  
Mapasaamin ang kaharian Mo.  
Sundin ang loob Mo dito sa lupa para nang sa langit.  
Bigyan Mo kami ngayon ng aming kakanin sa araw-araw.  
At patawarin Mo kami sa aming mga sala,  
para nang pagpapatawad namin sa nagkakasala sa amin.  
At huwag Mo kaming ipahintulot sa tukso,  
at iadya Mo kami sa lahat ng masama. Amen.

Aba Ginoong Maria, napupuno ka ng grasya,  
ang Panginoong Diyos ay sumasaiyo.  
Bukod kang pinagpala sa babaeng lahat,  
at pinagpala naman ang iyong Anak na si Jesus.  
Santa Maria, Ina ng Diyos,  
ipanalangin mo kaming makasalanan,  
ngayon at kung kami'y mamamatay. Amen.

Luwalhati sa Ama, at sa Anak, at sa Espiritu Santo.  
Kapara noong unang-una, ngayon at magpakailanman,  
magpasawalang hanggan. Amen.

Panginoong Hesukristo,  
sa Iyong awa at banal na kalooban lamang kami umaasa;  
linisin Mo ang aming hangarin sa kapalaluan,  
ingatan Mo ang aming dila at puso sa anumang sumpa o pamimilit,  
at panatilihin Mo kami sa pananampalataya, pag-ibig, at pagsisisi.  
Ang lahat ng mabuting bunga ay sa Iyo namin ibinabalik  
bilang papuri sa Ama, sa Anak, at sa Espiritu Santo. Amen.

Sa ngalan ng Ama, at ng Anak, at ng Espiritu Santo. Amen.

---

## Alevilik

Bismişah Allah Allah.

Bismillāhir-raḥmānir-raḥīm.  
Al-ḥamdu lillāhi rabbi l-ʿālamīn.  
Ar-raḥmāni r-raḥīm.  
Māliki yawmi d-dīn.  
Iyyāka naʿbudu wa iyyāka nastaʿīn.  
Ihdinā ṣ-ṣirāṭa l-mustaqīm.  
Ṣirāṭa lladhīna anʿamta ʿalayhim, ghayri l-maghḍūbi ʿalayhim wa lā ḍ-ḍāllīn.  
Āmīn.

Allāhumma ṣalli ʿalā Muḥammad wa āli Muḥammad.

Allah Allah.  
Evvel Allah, âhir Allah.  
Hak-Muhammed-Ali aşkına,  
On İki İmam, On Dört Masum-u Pak, On Yedi Kemerbest,  
Hünkâr Hacı Bektaş Veli,  
pirimiz, mürşidimiz, rehberimiz,  
gerçek erenlerin demine devranına hû.

Geldiğimiz yoldan, durduğumuz dardan,  
verdiğimiz ikrardan, tuttuğumuz erkândan ayırma ya Hakk.

Bu canın niyazı şudur:  
愿此次 YC 申请被录取，BD 顺利通过。  
Bu eşikte yol açık ola, gönül duru ola, söz yerini bula;  
emek zayi olmaya, kapılar hayırla açıla, sonuç rızalık ve hayırla tecelli ede.

Dilimizi doğru sözden,  
elimizi hak işten,  
belimizi edep yolundan ayırma ya Hakk.

Bu dilek kimsenin hakkını eksiltmeden,  
kimsenin lokmasını daraltmadan,  
kimseye haksızlık gelmeden kabul ola.  
Kul hakkından, yalan sözden, haram lokmadan, gösterişten sakla ya Hakk.

Rızalık meydanında gönüller bir ola.  
Küskünlük, dargınlık, haksızlık kalkmış ola.  
Yolumuzda sabır, aklımızda açıklık, işimizde kolaylık ola.

Ya Hakk, Ya Muhammed, Ya Ali.  
Ya Hızır, darda koyma.  
Ya On İki İmamlar, himmet eyleyin.  
Ya Hünkâr Hacı Bektaş Veli, nazar eyle.

Bi-ḥaqqı Muḥammad al-Muṣṭafā,  
bi-ḥaqqı ʿAlī al-Murtaḍā,  
bi-ḥaqqı Fāṭıma, Ḥasan, Ḥüseyn,  
bi-ḥaqqı On İki İmam,  
bu başvuru ve geçiş niyazı kabul ola.

Lokmamız helal,  
sözümüz doğru,  
yolumuz açık,  
gönlümüz rızalıkta ola.

Allah Allah.  
Gerçeğe hû.  
Eline, beline, diline sahip olmayı nasip eyle.  
Cem huzurunu, yol edebini, canların mahremiyetini korumayı nasip eyle.  
İkrarımızı hafife aldırma, gönlümüzü kibirden arıt, niyazımızı rızalıkla mühürle.

Müminlere rahmet,  
münkirlere hidayet,  
hakka yürüyen canlara rahmet,  
hazır-gaip cümle canlara birlik ola.

Hû, Hû, Hû.  
Gerçek erenler demine,  
Hak-Muhammed-Ali aşkına,  
Hünkâr Hacı Bektaş Veli hürmetine,  
Allah eyvallah.  
Hû.

---

## علوية (نصيرية)

نَوَيْتُ الدُّعَاءَ إِلَى اللهِ تَعَالَى فِي شَأْنِ أَمْرٍ مِنْ أُمُورِ التَّيْسِيرِ وَالْقَبُولِ، بِقَلْبٍ صَادِقٍ وَنِيَّةٍ سَلِيمَةٍ.

بِسْمِ اللهِ الرَّحْمٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ.

أَشْهَدُ أَنْ لَا إِلٰهَ إِلَّا اللهُ، وَأَشْهَدُ أَنَّ مُحَمَّدًا رَسُولُ اللهِ.

بِسْمِ اللهِ الرَّحْمٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ  
الْحَمْدُ لِلَّهِ رَبِّ الْعَالَمِينَ  
الرَّحْمٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ  
مَالِكِ يَوْمِ الدِّينِ  
إِيَّاكَ نَعْبُدُ وَإِيَّاكَ نَسْتَعِينُ  
اهْدِنَا الصِّرَاطَ الْمُسْتَقِيمَ  
صِرَاطَ الَّذِينَ أَنْعَمْتَ عَلَيْهِمْ  
غَيْرِ الْمَغْضُوبِ عَلَيْهِمْ وَلَا الضَّالِّينَ

بِسْمِ اللهِ الرَّحْمٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ  
قُلْ هُوَ اللهُ أَحَدٌ  
اللهُ الصَّمَدُ  
لَمْ يَلِدْ وَلَمْ يُولَدْ  
وَلَمْ يَكُنْ لَهُ كُفُوًا أَحَدٌ

إِنَّ اللهَ وَمَلَائِكَتَهُ يُصَلُّونَ عَلَى النَّبِيِّ  
يَا أَيُّهَا الَّذِينَ آمَنُوا صَلُّوا عَلَيْهِ وَسَلِّمُوا تَسْلِيمًا.

اللَّهُمَّ صَلِّ عَلَى مُحَمَّدٍ وَآلِ مُحَمَّدٍ.

يَا اللهُ، يَا رَحْمٰنُ، يَا رَحِيمُ، يَا حَيُّ، يَا قَيُّومُ،  
أَسْأَلُكَ بِاسْمِكَ وَرَحْمَتِكَ، وَبِحَقِّ مُحَمَّدٍ وَآلِ مُحَمَّدٍ،  
أَنْ تُيَسِّرَ هٰذَا الأَمْرَ، وَأَنْ تَفْتَحَ فِيهِ بَابَ الْخَيْرِ وَالْقَبُولِ،  
وَأَنْ تَجْعَلَ طَلَبَ YC مَقْبُولًا إِنْ كَانَ فِيهِ خَيْرٌ وَرِضًا وَهُدًى،  
وَأَنْ تَجْعَلَ مُرُورَ BD سَهْلًا مُيَسَّرًا، بِغَيْرِ عُسْرٍ وَلَا اضْطِرَابٍ وَلَا ضَرَرٍ.

اللَّهُمَّ اجْعَلْ هٰذَا النَّجَاحَ مِنْ فَضْلِكَ،  
لَا يُنْقِصُ حَقَّ أَحَدٍ، وَلَا يَسْلُبُ رِزْقَ أَحَدٍ، وَلَا يَظْلِمُ أَحَدًا،  
وَاجْعَلْهُ سَبَبًا لِلشُّكْرِ وَالصَّبْرِ وَصَفَاءِ الْقَلْبِ وَحُسْنِ الْعَمَلِ.

اللَّهُمَّ احْفَظْ حُرْمَةَ أَهْلِ الْبَيْتِ،  
وَاجْعَلْ هٰذَا الدُّعَاءَ خَالِصًا لِوَجْهِكَ،  
وَلَا تَجْعَلْ فِيهِ ظُلْمًا وَلَا قَطِيعَةً وَلَا أَذًى.

رَبَّنَا تَقَبَّلْ مِنَّا، إِنَّكَ أَنْتَ السَّمِيعُ الْعَلِيمُ.  
وَتُبْ عَلَيْنَا، إِنَّكَ أَنْتَ التَّوَّابُ الرَّحِيمُ.

أَسْتَغْفِرُ اللهَ رَبِّي وَأَتُوبُ إِلَيْهِ.

اللَّهُمَّ صَلِّ عَلَى مُحَمَّدٍ وَآلِ مُحَمَّدٍ.

---

## 苏菲 Bektashi

Bism-i Şâh, Allâh Allâh.

Niyyet eyledik rızâ-yı Ḥaqq için; bu YC başvurusunun kabulüne ve BD sürecinin hayırla, açıklıkla, doğrulukla geçmesine. Bu kapıdan gelecek hayrı isteriz; kimsenin hakkı eksilmeden, kimsenin nasibi alınmadan, zulüm ve haksızlık olmadan.

Bismi llāhi r-raḥmāni r-raḥīm.  
Al-ḥamdu li-llāhi rabbi l-ʿālamīn.  
Ar-raḥmāni r-raḥīm.  
Māliki yawmi d-dīn.  
Iyyāka naʿbudu wa iyyāka nastaʿīn.  
Ihdinā ṣ-ṣirāṭa l-mustaqīm.  
Ṣirāṭa lladhīna anʿamta ʿalayhim, ghayri l-maghḍūbi ʿalayhim wa lā ḍ-ḍāllīn.  
Āmīn.

Bismi llāhi r-raḥmāni r-raḥīm.  
Qul huwa llāhu aḥad.  
Allāhu ṣ-ṣamad.  
Lam yalid wa lam yūlad.  
Wa lam yakun lahu kufuwan aḥad.

Allāhumma ṣalli ʿalā Sayyidinā Muḥammadin wa ʿalā āli Sayyidinā Muḥammad.  
Allāhumma bārik ʿalā Sayyidinā Muḥammadin wa ʿalā āli Sayyidinā Muḥammad.

Lā ilāha illā llāh.  
Muḥammadun rasūlu llāh.  
ʿAlīyun walīyu llāh.

Allāh Allāh Allāh.  
Hū Hū Hū.

Lā ilāha illā Anta subḥānaka innī kuntu mina ẓ-ẓālimīn.

Bi-ḥurmeti Muḥammed Muṣṭafā.  
Bi-ḥurmeti ʿAlī al-Murtażā.  
Bi-ḥurmeti Fāṭımatü’z-Zehrā.  
Bi-ḥurmeti Ḥasan u Ḥüseyn.  
Bi-ḥurmeti On İki İmām.  
Bi-ḥurmeti Pîr Hünkâr Hacı Bektaş Velî.

Bism-i Şâh, Allâh Allâh.  
Niyetimiz Ḥaqq katında kabul ola.  
YC başvurusu hayra döne; BD yolu aydın, açık ve erkân üzere ola.  
Hayırlar feth ola, şerler def ola.  
Kapılar merhametle açıla, sözler doğrulukla işitile, kararlar adaletle verile.  
Gönle sekinet, dile hikmet, işe kolaylık, yola nûr ola.  
Engel varsa zarar vermeden kalksın; karanlık varsa kimse incinmeden dağılsın.  
Eline, beline, diline doğruluk ola.  
Meydanımız nurlu, lokmamız helâl, sözümüz gerçek ola.  
Dil bizden, nefes Pîr Hünkâr Hacı Bektaş Velî’den ola.  
Gerçeğe Hû.

Bismi llāhi r-raḥmāni r-raḥīm.  
Al-ḥamdu li-llāhi rabbi l-ʿālamīn.  
Ar-raḥmāni r-raḥīm.  
Māliki yawmi d-dīn.  
Iyyāka naʿbudu wa iyyāka nastaʿīn.  
Ihdinā ṣ-ṣirāṭa l-mustaqīm.  
Ṣirāṭa lladhīna anʿamta ʿalayhim, ghayri l-maghḍūbi ʿalayhim wa lā ḍ-ḍāllīn.  
Āmīn.

Allāh Allāh.  
Ḥaqq, gönlümüzü riyâdan arı eyle; dilimizi yalandan, elimizi haramdan, yolumuzu incitmekten koru.  
Duamız Kur’ān’ın nûru, ṣalawātın bereketi, dhikr-i Allāh’ın huzuru ile temiz ola.  
Ehl-i Beyt’in sevgisiyle, On İki İmām’ın hürmetiyle, Hünkâr Hacı Bektaş Velî’nin nefesiyle hayra bağlana.  
Gerçeğe Hû.

---

## 阿赫迈底亚

Al-ḥamdu lillāhi rabbi l-ʿālamīn.  
Ar-Raḥmāni r-Raḥīm.  
Māliki yawmi d-dīn.  
Iyyāka naʿbudu wa iyyāka nastaʿīn.  
Ihdinā ṣ-ṣirāṭa l-mustaqīm.  
Ṣirāṭa lladhīna anʿamta ʿalayhim ghayri l-maghḍūbi ʿalayhim wa lā ḍ-ḍāllīn.  
Āmīn.

Allāhumma ṣalli ʿalā Muḥammadin wa ʿalā āli Muḥammadin, kamā ṣallayta ʿalā Ibrāhīma wa ʿalā āli Ibrāhīma, innaka ḥamīdun majīd.  
Allāhumma bārik ʿalā Muḥammadin wa ʿalā āli Muḥammadin, kamā bārakta ʿalā Ibrāhīma wa ʿalā āli Ibrāhīma, innaka ḥamīdun majīd.

Astaghfirullāha rabbī min kulli dhanbin wa atūbu ilayh.  
Rabbanā ẓalamnā anfusanā wa in lam taghfir lanā wa tarḥamnā lanakūnanna mina l-khāsirīn.  
Rabbanā lā tuzigh qulūbanā baʿda idh hadaytanā wa hab lanā min ladunka raḥmah, innaka anta l-wahhāb.  
Rabbanā innana āmannā fa-ghfir lanā dhunūbanā wa qinā ʿadhāba n-nār.

Yā Allāh, yā Raḥmān, yā Raḥīm,  
anta mawlānā fa-nṣurnā, wa-ghfir lanā, wa-rḥamnā, wa-hdinā ṣ-ṣirāṭa l-mustaqīm.  
Rabbanā taqabbal duʿāʾanā, wa-jʿalhu khāliṣan li-wajhika l-karīm.

Rabbanā ātinā fi d-dunyā ḥasanah, wa fi l-ākhirati ḥasanah, wa qinā ʿadhāba n-nār.

Allāhumma innī astakhīruka bi-ʿilmika, wa astaqdiruka bi-qudratika, wa asʾaluka min faḍlika l-ʿaẓīm, fa-innaka taqdiru wa lā aqdir, wa taʿlamu wa lā aʿlam, wa anta ʿallāmu l-ghuyūb.  
Allāhumma in kunta taʿlamu anna qabūla ṭalabi YC wa murūra BD bi-yusrin wa salāmatin khayrun lī fī dīnī wa maʿāshī wa ʿāqibati amrī, faqdurhu lī wa yassirhu lī thumma bārik lī fīh.  
Wa in kunta taʿlamu anna qabūla ṭalabi YC wa murūra BD bi-yusrin wa salāmatin sharrun lī fī dīnī wa maʿāshī wa ʿāqibati amrī, fa-ṣrifhu ʿannī wa-ṣrifnī ʿanhu, wa-qdur lī l-khayra ḥaythu kāna thumma arḍinī bih.  
Allāhumma yassir lī mā kāna khayran, wa-srif ʿannī mā kāna sharran, wa-lā tajʿal fī ṭalabī ẓulman li-aḥadin, wa-lā ḥirmānan li-ḥaqqi aḥadin, wa-lā ḍararan ʿalā barīʾin.

Allāhumma ghfir li-ḥayyinā wa mayyitinā, wa shāhidinā wa ghāʾibinā, wa ṣaghīrinā wa kabīrinā, wa dhakarinā wa unthānā.  
Allāhumma man aḥyaytahu minnā fa-aḥyihi ʿalā l-islām, wa man tawaffaytahu minnā fa-tawaffahu ʿalā l-īmān.  
Rabbi rḥamhumā kamā rabbayānī ṣaghīrā.

Rabbi jʿalnī muqīma ṣ-ṣalāti wa min dhurriyyatī, rabbanā wa taqabbal duʿāʾ.  
Rabbanā ghfir lī wa li-wālidayya wa li-l-muʾminīna yawma yaqūmu l-ḥisāb.  
Rabbanā afrigh ʿalaynā ṣabran wa thabbit aqdāmanā.  
Rabbanā lā tuʾākhidhnā in nasīnā aw akhṭaʾnā.  
Rabbanā wa lā taḥmil ʿalaynā iṣran kamā ḥamaltahu ʿalā lladhīna min qablinā.  
Rabbanā wa lā tuḥammilnā mā lā ṭāqata lanā bih.  
Waʿfu ʿannā, wa-ghfir lanā, wa-rḥamnā, anta mawlānā.

Lā ilāha illā Allāh, waḥdahu lā sharīka lah; lahu l-mulku wa lahu l-ḥamdu, wa huwa ʿalā kulli shayʾin qadīr.  
Subḥāna rabbika rabbi l-ʿizzati ʿammā yaṣifūn.  
Wa salāmun ʿalā l-mursalīn.  
Wa l-ḥamdu lillāhi rabbi l-ʿālamīn.

Allāhumma ṣalli ʿalā Muḥammadin wa ʿalā āli Muḥammadin, wa bārik wa sallim.  
Āmīn.

---

## സീറോ മലബാർ സഭ

പിതാവിന്റെയും പുത്രന്റെയും പരിശുദ്ധാത്മാവിന്റെയും നാമത്തിൽ. ആമ്മേൻ.

പിതാവിനും പുത്രനും പരിശുദ്ധാത്മാവിനും സ്തുതി.  
ആദിമുതൽ എന്നേക്കും. ആമ്മേൻ.

കർത്താവായ ഈശോമിശിഹായേ, ജീവനുടെയും കരുണയുടെയും നാഥാ,  
ഈ പ്രത്യേക സംഭവത്തിന്റെ പ്രാർത്ഥനയിൽ  
YC അപേക്ഷ സ്വീകരിക്കപ്പെടുകയും BD ക്രമമായി, സമാധാനത്തോടെ, വിജയകരമായി കടന്നുപോകുകയും ചെയ്യേണ്ട ഈ അഭിലാഷം  
അങ്ങയുടെ തിരുമനസ്സിനും കരുണയ്ക്കും സമർപ്പിക്കുന്നു.

ദൈവമേ, പാപിയായ ഞങ്ങളോടു കരുണയുണ്ടാകണമേ.  
കർത്താവേ, കരുണയുണ്ടാകണമേ.  
മിശിഹായേ, കരുണയുണ്ടാകണമേ.  
കർത്താവേ, കരുണയുണ്ടാകണമേ.

“ഞാൻ നിങ്ങളോടു സമാധാനം വിട്ടുകൊടുക്കുന്നു; എന്റെ സമാധാനം ഞാൻ നിങ്ങള്ക്കു തരുന്നു” എന്നു അരുളിച്ചെയ്ത കർത്താവേ,  
ഭയവും ആശങ്കയും നീക്കി, വ്യക്തതയും ധൈര്യവും വിനയവും നൽകണമേ.  
അങ്ങയുടെ കൃപയാൽ യോഗ്യമായ വാതിലുകൾ തുറക്കപ്പെടുകയും,  
സത്യവും നീതിയും നന്മയും അനുസരിച്ച് കാര്യങ്ങൾ നിറവേറുകയും ചെയ്യണമേ.

കർത്താവായ ഈശോമിശിഹായേ,  
YC അപേക്ഷയുടെ സ്വീകരണത്തിനും BD-യുടെ സുഗമമായ പൂർത്തീകരണത്തിനുമായി  
അങ്ങയുടെ പ്രകാശവും സമാധാനവും സഹായവും നൽകണമേ.  
തടസ്സങ്ങൾ ഉണ്ടെങ്കിൽ അവയെ ദോഷമില്ലാതെ നീക്കണമേ;  
ആർക്കും അന്യായം വരുത്താതെ, ആരുടെയും അവകാശം അപഹരിക്കാതെ,  
അങ്ങയുടെ ഇഷ്ടത്തിൽ നന്മയായ ഫലം നൽകണമേ.  
അങ്ങയുടെ സ്ലീവായുടെ അടയാളത്തിൽ  
ഭയത്തിലും ആശയക്കുഴപ്പത്തിലും നിരാശയിലും നിന്നു കാത്തുകൊള്ളണമേ.  
അങ്ങയുടെ തിരുമനസ്സിന് വിരുദ്ധമാകുന്നതെല്ലാം നീക്കണമേ.  
അങ്ങയുടെ ഇഷ്ടം നിറവേറണമേ.

നന്മ നിറഞ്ഞ മറിയമേ, സ്വസ്തി,  
കർത്താവ് അങ്ങയോടുകൂടെ,  
സ്ത്രീകളിൽ അങ്ങ് അനുഗ്രഹിക്കപ്പെട്ടവളാകുന്നു,  
അങ്ങയുടെ ഉദരഫലമായ ഈശോ അനുഗ്രഹിക്കപ്പെട്ടവനാകുന്നു.  
പരിശുദ്ധ മറിയമേ, തമ്പുരാന്റെ അമ്മേ,  
പാപികളായ ഞങ്ങൾക്കുവേണ്ടി  
ഇപ്പോഴും ഞങ്ങളുടെ മരണസമയത്തും  
തമ്പുരാനോടപേക്ഷിക്കണമേ. ആമ്മേൻ.

മാർ തോമാ ശ്ലീഹായേ, ഞങ്ങൾക്കുവേണ്ടി പ്രാർത്ഥിക്കണമേ.  
ദൈവത്തിന്റെ പരിശുദ്ധരേ, ഞങ്ങൾക്കുവേണ്ടി പ്രാർത്ഥിക്കണമേ.

സ്വർഗ്ഗസ്ഥനായ ഞങ്ങളുടെ പിതാവേ,  
അങ്ങയുടെ നാമം പൂജിതമാകണമേ.  
അങ്ങയുടെ രാജ്യം വരണമേ.  
അങ്ങയുടെ തിരുമനസ്സ് സ്വർഗ്ഗത്തിലെപ്പോലെ ഭൂമിയിലും ആകണമേ.  
ഞങ്ങൾക്ക് ആവശ്യമുള്ള ആഹാരം ഇന്ന് ഞങ്ങൾക്ക് തരണമേ.  
ഞങ്ങളുടെ കടക്കാരോട് ഞങ്ങൾ ക്ഷമിക്കുന്നതുപോലെ  
ഞങ്ങളുടെ കടങ്ങൾ ഞങ്ങളോടും ക്ഷമിക്കണമേ.  
ഞങ്ങളെ പ്രലോഭനത്തിൽ ഉൾപ്പെടുത്തരുതേ.  
ദുഷ്ടനിൽ നിന്നു ഞങ്ങളെ രക്ഷിക്കണമേ. ആമ്മേൻ.

Qaddīšā Alāhā,  
Qaddīšā ḥayltānā,  
Qaddīšā lā māyōtā,  
etraḥam ‘layn.

കർത്താവായ ഈശോമിശിഹായേ,  
ഈ അപേക്ഷയും പരിശ്രമവും പ്രതീക്ഷയും ആശങ്കകളും  
അങ്ങയുടെ പരിശുദ്ധ സ്ലീവായോടും ഉയിർപ്പോടും ചേർത്ത് സമർപ്പിക്കുന്നു.  
ലഭിക്കുന്ന ഫലം എന്തായാലും വിശ്വാസത്തിലും നന്ദിയിലും സമാധാനത്തിലും നിലനിൽക്കുവാൻ സഹായിക്കണമേ.  
അങ്ങേക്കു സ്തുതിയും ബഹുമാനവും കൃതജ്ഞതയും  
ഇപ്പോഴും എല്ലായ്പ്പോഴും എന്നേക്കും. ആമ്മേൻ.

പിതാവിനും പുത്രനും പരിശുദ്ധാത്മാവിനും സ്തുതി.  
ആദിമുതൽ എന്നേക്കും. ആമ്മേൻ.

പിതാവിന്റെയും പുത്രന്റെയും പരിശുദ്ധാത്മാവിന്റെയും നാമത്തിൽ. ആമ്മേൻ.

---

## 伊斯玛仪派 / 阿迦汗系

**Niyyah:**  
Allāhumma innī ajʿalu hādhā al-duʿāʾ li-wajhika al-karīm, wa aṭlubu raḥmataka wa hidāyataka fī amri qabūli ṭalabi YC wa murūri BD bi-salāmah wa tawfīq, wa li-l-jamāʿat kullihā.

**Basmalah:**  
Bismillāhi r-Raḥmāni r-Raḥīm.  
بِسْمِ اللهِ الرَّحْمٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

**Al-Fātiḥah:**  
Al-ḥamdu lillāhi rabbi l-ʿālamīn.  
Ar-raḥmāni r-raḥīm.  
Māliki yawmi d-dīn.  
Iyyāka naʿbudu wa iyyāka nastaʿīn.  
Ihdinā ṣ-ṣirāṭa l-mustaqīm.  
Ṣirāṭa lladhīna anʿamta ʿalayhim, ghayri l-maghḍūbi ʿalayhim wa lā ḍ-ḍāllīn.  
Āmīn.

**Shahādah wa Walāyah:**  
Ashhadu an lā ilāha illā Allāh.  
Ashhadu anna Muḥammadan Rasūlu llāh.  
Ashhadu anna Mawlānā ʿAlīyyan Amīru l-Muʾminīn ʿAlīyyu llāh.

**Ṣalawāt:**  
Allāhumma ṣalli ʿalā Muḥammadin wa āli Muḥammad.  
Allāhumma bārik ʿalā Muḥammadin wa āli Muḥammad.

**Duʿāʾ:**  
Yā Allāh, yā Raḥmān, yā Raḥīm,  
bi-nūri hidāyatika, wa bi-ḥaqqi Muḥammadin wa āli Muḥammad,  
iftah abwāba r-raḥmah wa l-ḥikmah wa t-tawfīq fī hādhā l-amr.  
Allāhumma ijʿal ṭalaba YC maqbūlan in kāna fīhi khayr,  
wa ijʿal murūra BD sahlān, ṣādiqan, mubārakan, wa salīman.  
Wa-rzuq ṣafāʾa l-qalb, wa ṣidqa l-bayān, wa ḥusna l-ikhtiyār,  
wa lā tajʿal fī hādhā nūqṣānan li-ḥaqqi aḥad,  
wa lā akhdhan min rizqi aḥad, wa lā ḍararan ʿalā aḥad.  
Wa-ṣrif ʿannā al-khawfa wa l-ḍarar wa l-ẓulma,  
wa-thabbit qulūbanā ʿalā l-īmān wa l-ʿamal aṣ-ṣāliḥ.

**Āyat an-Nūr:**  
Allāhu nūru s-samāwāti wa l-arḍ.  
Mathalu nūrihī ka-mishkātin fīhā miṣbāḥ.  
Al-miṣbāḥu fī zujājah.  
Az-zujājatu ka-annahā kawkabun durrīyyun  
yūqadu min shajaratin mubārakatin zaytūnatin  
lā sharqīyyatin wa lā gharbīyyah,  
yakādu zaytuhā yuḍīʾu wa law lam tamsashu nār.  
Nūrun ʿalā nūr.  
Yahdī llāhu li-nūrihī man yashāʾ.  
Wa yaḍribu llāhu l-amthāla li-n-nās.  
Wa llāhu bi-kulli shayʾin ʿalīm.

**Tasbīḥ:**  
Yā Allāh.  
Yā Muḥammad.  
Yā ʿAlī.  
Yā Ḥāḍir Imām, madad.

**Ginan remembrance:**  
Eji satgur miliyā munē āj, ānand ānand thayō.  
Eji sāhebjī tū̃ morē man bhāvē.

**Duʿāʾ for the living and the departed:**  
Allāhumma ghfir li-l-muʾminīna wa l-muʾmināt,  
wa rḥam arwāḥa l-marḥūmīn wa l-marḥūmāt,  
wa-jʿal nūra l-hidāyah fī qulūbinā,  
wa fī jamāʿatinā kullihā.

**Khitām:**  
Allāhumma taqabbal duʿāʾanā li-wajhika al-karīm,  
wa-ḥfaẓnā ʿalā t-tawḥīd wa l-īmān wa l-adab,  
wa-jʿal ṣalātanā wa salāmanā ʿalā Muḥammadin wa āli Muḥammad,  
wa-jʿal madad al-hidāyah nūran ilā l-khayr, lā ilā ḍarar.  
Āmīn.  
Yā ʿAlī madad.

---

## 苏菲 Chishtiyya

**[niyya / 立意]**

Nawaynā al-duʿāʾa wa-dh-dhikra li-wajhi Allāhi taʿālā, fī hādhihi l-ḥājati: an yujʿala amru ṭalabi YC maqbūlan bi-khayr, wa-an yamurra BD bi-yusrin wa-salāmah.

**[tawba 与 istiʿādha]**

Astaghfiru Allāha rabbī min kulli dhanbin wa-atūbu ilayh.  
Aʿūdhu bi-llāhi mina sh-shayṭāni r-rajīm.

**[basmala]**

Bismi llāhi r-raḥmāni r-raḥīm.

**[al-Fātiḥa]**

Al-ḥamdu li-llāhi rabbi l-ʿālamīn.  
Ar-raḥmāni r-raḥīm.  
Māliki yawmi d-dīn.  
Iyyāka naʿbudu wa-iyyāka nastaʿīn.  
Ihdinā ṣ-ṣirāṭa l-mustaqīm.  
Ṣirāṭa lladhīna anʿamta ʿalayhim, ghayri l-maghḍūbi ʿalayhim wa-lā ḍ-ḍāllīn.  
Āmīn.

**[ṣalawāt]**

Allāhumma ṣalli ʿalā sayyidinā Muḥammadin wa-ʿalā āli sayyidinā Muḥammad,  
kamā ṣallayta ʿalā sayyidinā Ibrāhīma wa-ʿalā āli sayyidinā Ibrāhīm,  
wa-bārik ʿalā sayyidinā Muḥammadin wa-ʿalā āli sayyidinā Muḥammad,  
kamā bārakta ʿalā sayyidinā Ibrāhīma wa-ʿalā āli sayyidinā Ibrāhīm,  
innaka ḥamīdun majīd.

**[dhikr / ism Allāh]**

Lā ilāha illā Allāh.  
Lā ilāha illā Allāh.  
Lā ilāha illā Allāh.

Allāh Hū.  
Allāh Hū.  
Allāh Hū.

Lā ḥawla wa-lā quwwata illā bi-llāhi l-ʿaliyyi l-ʿaẓīm.  
Lā ḥawla wa-lā quwwata illā bi-llāhi l-ʿaliyyi l-ʿaẓīm.  
Lā ḥawla wa-lā quwwata illā bi-llāhi l-ʿaliyyi l-ʿaẓīm.

Yā Allāh, yā Raḥmān, yā Raḥīm, yā Laṭīf, yā Karīm, yā Fattāḥ, yā ʿAlīm.

**[samāʿ/qawwali 的 ḥamd、naʿt、manqabat 或静默 dhikr]**

Subḥāna llāhi wa-bi-ḥamdih.  
Subḥāna llāhi l-ʿaẓīm.

Allāhumma ṣalli wa-sallim ʿalā sayyidinā Muḥammad, nūri l-qulūb wa-raḥmati l-ʿālamīn.

Raḥima llāhu mashāyikha ṭarīqati l-Chishtiyya, wa-nafaʿanā Allāhu bi-ḥubbihim wa-adabihim, min ghayri istiʿānahin illā bi-llāh.

**[针对 event 的 duʿāʾ]**

Yā Allāh, innā nasʾaluka bi-raḥmatika wa-faḍlika wa-karamika,  
an taftaḥa abwāba l-khayri fī hādhā l-amr,  
wa-an tajʿala ṭalaba YC maqbūlan in kāna fīhi khayrun fī d-dīni wa-d-dunyā wa-l-ākhirah,  
wa-an tusahhila murūra BD bi-yusrin wa-sadādin wa-salāmah.

Allāhumma in kāna hādhā l-amru khayran, faqarribhu wa-yassirhu wa-bārik fīh;  
wa-in kāna ghayra dhālika, faṣrif ʿannā sharrahu, wa-ṣrifnā ʿanhu bi-luṭfika,  
wa-qaddim lanā mā huwa aqwamu wa-aṭharu wa-anfaʿu.

Allāhumma lā tajʿal ṭalabanā hādhā ẓulman li-aḥad,  
wa-lā akhdhan li-ḥaqqi aḥad, wa-lā naقصan min rizqi aḥad,  
wa-lā ḍararan ʿalā qalbin aw badan aw maʿāsh;  
bal ijʿalhu min bābi l-faḍli wa-l-ʿadli wa-r-riḍā.

Rabbi shraḥ lanā ṣudūranā, wa-yassir lanā umūranā,  
wa-rzuqnā ṣidqa n-niyyah, wa-ḥusna t-tadbīr, wa-qabūla l-khayr,  
wa-thabbith aqdāmanā ʿalā ṣirāṭika l-mustaqīm.

Rabbanā ātinā fī d-dunyā ḥasanatan wa-fī l-ākhirati ḥasanatan wa-qinā ʿadhāba n-nār.

**[īṣāl al-thawāb / 回向]**

Allāhumma in kāna fī hādhihi t-tilāwati wa-hādhā dh-dhikri wa-hādhā d-duʿāʾi thawābun,  
fa-awṣil thawābahu ilā ḥaḍrati sayyidinā Muḥammadin ṣallā llāhu ʿalayhi wa-sallam,  
wa-ilā ālihi wa-aṣḥābihi,  
wa-ilā arwāḥi mashāyikhinā fī ṭarīqati l-Chishtiyya,  
wa-jʿal lanā minhu nūran wa-raḥmatan wa-adaban maqbūlan ʿindaka,  
yā Arḥama r-rāḥimīn.

**[khatm / 结束祈愿]**

Subḥāna rabbika rabbi l-ʿizzati ʿammā yaṣifūn.  
Wa-salāmun ʿalā l-mursalīn.  
Wa-l-ḥamdu li-llāhi rabbi l-ʿālamīn.

Āmīn.

Lā ilāha illā Allāh, waḥdahu lā sharīka lah.  
Lahu l-mulku wa-lahu l-ḥamdu, wa-huwa ʿalā kulli shayʾin qadīr.  
Allāhumma ilayka l-qasd, wa-minka l-faḍl, wa-ʿalayka t-tawakkul;  
fa-ṭahhir qulūbanā mina l-ghaflati wa-r-riyāʾ,  
wa-thabbitnā ʿalā t-tawḥīd wa-ṣ-ṣalāh wa-l-adab,  
wa-lā tajʿal fī qulūbinā istiʿānahً illā bika, yā Allāh.

---

## الداؤودية البهرة

اللّٰهُمَّ اجْعَلْنِي عَلَى طَهَارَةٍ وَأَدَبٍ وَنِيَّةٍ صَادِقَةٍ، وَاقْبَلْ دُعَائِي بِرَحْمَتِكَ يَا أَرْحَمَ الرَّاحِمِينَ.

بِسْمِ اللهِ الرَّحْمٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

نَوَيْتُ أَنْ أَدْعُوَ اللهَ تَعَالَى فِي أَمْرِ طَلَبِ القَبُولِ فِي YC، وَتَيْسِيرِ اجْتِيَازِ BD بِسَلَامٍ وَخَيْرٍ، خَالِصًا لِلّٰهِ تَعَالَى.

ٱلْحَمْدُ لِلّٰهِ رَبِّ ٱلْعَالَمِينَ  
ٱلرَّحْمَٰنِ ٱلرَّحِيمِ  
مَٰلِكِ يَوْمِ ٱلدِّينِ  
إِيَّاكَ نَعْبُدُ وَإِيَّاكَ نَسْتَعِينُ  
ٱهْدِنَا ٱلصِّرَٰطَ ٱلْمُسْتَقِيمَ  
صِرَٰطَ ٱلَّذِينَ أَنْعَمْتَ عَلَيْهِمْ  
غَيْرِ ٱلْمَغْضُوبِ عَلَيْهِمْ وَلَا ٱلضَّآلِّينَ

اللّٰهُمَّ صَلِّ عَلَى مُحَمَّدٍ وَآلِ مُحَمَّدٍ.

يَا اللهُ، يَا رَحْمٰنُ، يَا رَحِيمُ، يَا كَرِيمُ،  
بِحَقِّ مُحَمَّدٍ وَآلِ مُحَمَّدٍ، وَبِوَلَايَةِ أَوْلِيَائِكَ الصَّالِحِينَ،  
أَسْأَلُكَ أَنْ تَفْتَحَ أَبْوَابَ الخَيْرِ، وَتُيَسِّرَ الأَسْبَابَ، وَتَجْعَلَ هٰذَا الأَمْرَ مُبَارَكًا إِنْ كَانَ فِيهِ صَلَاحُ الدِّينِ وَالدُّنْيَا وَالآخِرَةِ.

رَبِّ أَدْخِلْنِي مُدْخَلَ صِدْقٍ وَأَخْرِجْنِي مُخْرَجَ صِدْقٍ وَاجْعَلْ لِّي مِن لَّدُنكَ سُلْطَانًا نَّصِيرًا.

اللّٰهُمَّ إِنِّي أَسْأَلُكَ قَبُولًا حَسَنًا، وَتَوْفِيقًا صَادِقًا، وَبَيَانًا سَدِيدًا، وَقَلْبًا مُطْمَئِنًّا، وَأَنْ تُيَسِّرَ اجْتِيَازَ BD عَلَى وَجْهٍ تُحِبُّهُ وَتَرْضَاهُ.

اللّٰهُمَّ إِنْ كَانَ القَبُولُ فِي YC خَيْرًا فَاقْضِهِ بِلُطْفِكَ، وَإِنْ كَانَ غَيْرَ ذٰلِكَ فَاصْرِفْنِي إِلَى مَا هُوَ أَخْيَرُ وَأَبْقَى، وَارْزُقْنِي الرِّضَا بِقَضَائِكَ.

اللّٰهُمَّ لَا أَسْأَلُكَ نَجَاحًا يَظْلِمُ أَحَدًا، وَلَا رِزْقًا يَنْقُصُ رِزْقَ أَحَدٍ، وَلَا فَتْحًا يَضُرُّ عَبْدًا مِنْ عِبَادِكَ؛ بَلْ أَسْأَلُكَ خَيْرًا طَيِّبًا حَلَالًا مُبَارَكًا.

لَا إِلٰهَ إِلَّا أَنْتَ سُبْحَانَكَ إِنِّي كُنْتُ مِنَ الظَّالِمِينَ.

رَبَّنَا تَقَبَّلْ مِنَّا إِنَّكَ أَنْتَ السَّمِيعُ العَلِيمُ،  
وَتُبْ عَلَيْنَا إِنَّكَ أَنْتَ التَّوَّابُ الرَّحِيمُ.
