## 神智学协会

In the name of the One Life, and for the good of the whole human family, this prayer is held concerning this event: may the YC application be received with favor, and may BD pass smoothly, within right human relations and the Plan of Love and Light.

From the point of Light within the Mind of God  
Let light stream forth into the minds of men.  
Let Light descend on Earth.

From the point of Love within the Heart of God  
Let love stream forth into the hearts of men.  
May Christ return to Earth.

From the centre where the Will of God is known  
Let purpose guide the little wills of men—  
The purpose which the Masters know and serve.

From the centre which we call the race of men  
Let the Plan of Love and Light work out  
And may it seal the door where evil dwells.

Let Light and Love and Power restore the Plan on Earth.

May this application, this review, and this passing-through be held in clear light, honest merit, right opportunity, and serviceable purpose. May success come without coercing any will, without depriving another of rightful good, and without harm, rivalry, or return of injury.

May every obstacle be illumined, every decision be guided by fairness, and every outcome serve not private gain alone, but a wider usefulness within the human family.

Let Light and Love and Power restore the Plan on Earth.  
May this wish be purified into goodwill, harmlessness, and right human relations; may it stand only insofar as it accords with the Plan of Love and Light, and may the benefit be shared with all beings.

---

## 赫密士主义当代社团

[净化与定向]  
In silentio, pietate et mente clara hic sto;  
non ad nocendum, non ad cogendum, non ad fallendum, non ad rapiendum.  
Oratio haec referatur ad τὸ ἕν, ad νοῦς, ad λόγος,  
et ad ordinem divinum qui omnia sapienter gubernat.

[向一者与 Nous 发愿]  
Ad Unum et ad Nous me converto;  
cesset confusio, dirigatur voluntas, purgetur sermo,  
et mens fiat simplex, temperata, vigilans.

[赫密士感恩祷正行：Asclepius 41]  
Tibi gratias agimus, summe et excellentissime,  
cuius numine solo gubernamur;  
et gratias agimus tibi, qui nos tanto lumine cognitionis inlustrasti.

Sanctum est nomen tuum et honorabile,  
nomen unum, quo solus Deus benedicendus est religione paterna,  
quoniam omnibus paternam pietatem, religionem, amorem  
et quaecumque sunt dulcioris affectus praestare dignatus es.

[陈明所愿]  
愿此次 YC 申请被录取，BD 顺利通过；愿其中一切沟通、判断、时机与执行，合于明智、节制、诚实与正当秩序。  
不以此愿夺他人机会、损他人福分、侵他人自由，亦不以欺诈、胁迫或不义取得成功。  
若此事合于善与正序，愿门径开启，障碍化解，言辞清明，结果稳妥。

[感恩]  
Non impero sacro; supplico, audio, et corrigor.  
Quod claritatis, concordiae, tutelae et sapientiae ex hac prece oritur,  
ad bonum, ad ordinem, ad pacem referatur.  
Gratias ago pro lumine cognitionis; gratias ago pro via recta.

[回向与静默]  
Purificetur intentio; solvatur aviditas; servetur libertas omnium.  
Si timor, adhaesio aut inordinatio oriatur,  
revocetur vox mea ad simplicem gratiarum actionem  
et quiescat omnis invocatio in pace.

Sigē. Nous. Logos. Hen.

## 玛丁主义（Martinism）

In nomine Patris, et Filii, et Spiritus Sancti. Amen.

Seigneur, Dieu éternel, source de toute lumière, de toute justice et de toute miséricorde,  
que notre pensée, notre parole et notre acte soient redressés devant Toi.  
Seigneur Jésus-Christ, Réparateur, que ta paix descende sur cette intention droite nommée devant Toi :  
ut petitio ad YC benigne recipiatur, et probatio BD ordinate ac feliciter transeat,  
non auferendo bonum alterius, non minuendo vitam alterius,  
sed secundum justitiam, veritatem, charitatem, et voluntatem Patris.

Miserere mei, Deus, secundum magnam misericordiam tuam.  
Et secundum multitudinem miserationum tuarum, dele iniquitatem meam.  
Amplius lava me ab iniquitate mea,  
et a peccato meo munda me.  
Cor mundum crea in me, Deus,  
et spiritum rectum innova in visceribus meis.  
Ne proicias me a facie tua,  
et Spiritum sanctum tuum ne auferas a me.  
Redde mihi laetitiam salutaris tui,  
et spiritu principali confirma me.

Asperges me, Domine, hyssopo, et mundabor;  
lavabis me, et super nivem dealbabor.

Pater noster, qui es in caelis,  
sanctificetur nomen tuum.  
Adveniat regnum tuum.  
Fiat voluntas tua, sicut in caelo et in terra.  
Panem nostrum quotidianum da nobis hodie.  
Et dimitte nobis debita nostra,  
sicut et nos dimittimus debitoribus nostris.  
Et ne nos inducas in tentationem,  
sed libera nos a malo. Amen.

In principio erat Verbum,  
et Verbum erat apud Deum,  
et Deus erat Verbum.  
Hoc erat in principio apud Deum.  
Omnia per ipsum facta sunt:  
et sine ipso factum est nihil, quod factum est.  
In ipso vita erat,  
et vita erat lux hominum:  
et lux in tenebris lucet,  
et tenebrae eam non comprehenderunt.

Veni, Creator Spiritus,  
mentes tuorum visita,  
imple superna gratia  
quae tu creasti pectora.

Providentia divina, quae omnia in numero, pondere et mensura disponis,  
aperi viam rectam, si haec via est in lumine tuo.  
Confirma intellectum, memoriam, sermonem et cor;  
remove impedimenta non per vim, sed per pacem;  
ordina tempus, responsum et judicium secundum misericordiam tuam.  
Fiat voluntas tua.

Seigneur Jésus-Christ, Réparateur,  
ramène toute inquiétude au silence de l’intérieur sanctuaire;  
que la lumière divine éclaire ce qui doit être accompli,  
que la paix garde ce qui doit être attendu,  
et que l’âme demeure humble dans la réintégration vers Dieu.

Gloria Patri, et Filio, et Spiritui Sancto.  
Sicut erat in principio, et nunc, et semper,  
et in saecula saeculorum. Amen.

Miserere mei, Deus, secundum magnam misericordiam tuam;  
cor mundum crea in me, Deus,  
et spiritum rectum innova in visceribus meis.

Pater noster, qui es in caelis,  
sanctificetur nomen tuum.  
Adveniat regnum tuum.  
Fiat voluntas tua, sicut in caelo et in terra.  
Et ne nos inducas in tentationem,  
sed libera nos a malo. Amen.

In nomine Patris, et Filii, et Spiritus Sancti. Amen.

---

## Spiritism · Kardecism（凯德克派）

Dieu tout-puissant, souverainement juste et bon,  
nous élevons vers toi notre pensée avec sincérité,  
sans orgueil, sans esprit de domination,  
et sans vouloir contraindre aucune créature visible ou invisible.

Que ta volonté soit faite et non la nôtre.  
Si la demande que nous formons est utile au progrès de l’âme,  
conforme à ta loi, à la justice et à la charité,  
daigne l’accueillir.

Notre Père qui êtes aux cieux,  
que votre nom soit sanctifié;  
que votre règne arrive;  
que votre volonté soit faite sur la terre comme au ciel.  
Donnez-nous aujourd'hui notre pain de chaque jour;  
pardonnez-nous nos offenses,  
comme nous pardonnons à ceux qui nous ont offensés;  
ne nous laissez pas succomber à la tentation,  
mais délivrez-nous du mal.  
Ainsi soit-il.

Bons Esprits qui êtes les ministres de Dieu,  
assistez-nous dans l’épreuve présente.  
Anges gardiens, Esprits protecteurs,  
éclairez la pensée, soutenez le courage,  
écartez les pensées mauvaises,  
et inspirez ce qui est juste, charitable et conforme à la loi de Dieu.

Seigneur,  
nous te prions au sujet de cette candidature à YC  
et du passage de BD.  
Inspirez la meilleure résolution,  
la parole juste, le discernement clair,  
la préparation loyale et le calme intérieur.  
Si cette admission et cette réussite peuvent servir au bien,  
au travail honnête, au progrès moral et à l’utilité commune,  
permets qu’elles s’accomplissent selon ta volonté.

Que cette réussite ne soit pas cherchée au détriment d’autrui;  
qu’elle ne ravisse à personne son bien légitime,  
sa paix, sa dignité, sa chance ni son mérite.  
Que tout obstacle soit écarté sans haine,  
et que chacun reçoive ce qui convient le mieux  
à son avancement devant Dieu.

Nous prions aussi pour toutes les personnes vivantes liées à cette décision:  
qu’elles soient éclairées avec justice, bienveillance et vérité.  
Nous prions pour les Esprits souffrants qui pourraient s’approcher de cette situation:  
que les bons Esprits leur portent des pensées fraternelles,  
que la lumière se fasse pour eux,  
et qu’ils trouvent le chemin du repentir, de la paix et du progrès.

Seigneur,  
ne permets pas que cette prière serve l’orgueil,  
l’intérêt égoïste, la curiosité frivole,  
ni la domination d’aucun esprit.  
Qu’elle soit seulement un acte de foi,  
de charité, de repentir et de soumission à ta volonté.

Aide à corriger les défauts,  
à réparer ce qui doit être réparé,  
à pardonner sincèrement,  
à travailler avec droiture,  
et à accepter avec confiance ce que ta sagesse permettra.

À Dieu, souverainement juste et bon,  
soient rendus la confiance, la reconnaissance et l’amour.  
Ainsi soit-il.

---

## Spiritualism / NSAC

Infinite Intelligence, God of love, law, and life,  
I come in reverence, in sincerity, and in personal responsibility,  
holding this YC application and BD review before Thee.

Our Father which art in heaven,  
Hallowed be thy name.  
Thy kingdom come.  
Thy will be done in earth, as it is in heaven.  
Give us this day our daily bread.  
And forgive us our debts, as we forgive our debtors.  
And lead us not into temptation,  
but deliver us from evil:  
For thine is the kingdom, and the power, and the glory, for ever.  
Amen.

I affirm:  
We believe in Infinite Intelligence.  
We believe that the phenomena of Nature, both physical and spiritual,  
are the expression of Infinite Intelligence.  
We affirm that true religion is living in obedience to Nature’s Laws.  
We affirm that the existence and personal identity of the individual  
continue after the change called death.  
We affirm that communication with the so-called dead is a fact,  
scientifically proven by the phenomena of Spiritualism.  
We affirm the highest morality contained in the Golden Rule:  
Therefore all things whatsoever ye would that men should do to you,  
do ye even so to them.  
We affirm moral responsibility, and that each soul makes its own happiness  
or unhappiness as it obeys or disobeys Nature’s physical and spiritual laws.  
We affirm that the doorway to reformation is never closed  
against any soul here or hereafter.  
We affirm that the precepts of Prophecy and Healing are Divine attributes  
proven through Mediumship.

Infinite Intelligence,  
within Divine Law, truth, compassion, and the welfare of all concerned,  
let this YC application be held in light.  
May the materials already submitted be received with fairness, clarity, and right understanding.  
May the BD review proceed smoothly, in good order, with honest communication, sound judgment, and right timing.  
May courage, steadiness, preparation, and integrity be present in every step.  
May acceptance come if it is in harmony with Divine Law, moral responsibility, and the true good of all concerned.  
This prayer does not seek to dispossess another, to diminish another’s rightful opportunity, or to gain by unfairness;  
let the way open only through truth, merit, service, and the Golden Rule.

Let the words of my mouth, and the meditation of my heart,  
be acceptable in thy sight, O LORD, my strength, and my redeemer.

May no word spoken here replace conscience, responsibility, or truth.  
May no spirit, person, or influence be compelled.  
May all be governed by Infinite Intelligence, Divine Love, and Natural Law.

I now release anxious seeking after signs, messages, or certainty,  
and return to the Lord’s Prayer, to quietness, to personal responsibility,  
and to obedience to Nature’s physical and spiritual laws.  
Where practical, legal, financial, or professional judgment is needed,  
may I be guided toward proper qualified help and honest counsel.  
In stillness, may fear be softened, judgment be clear, and right action be done.

Amen.

---

## 威卡 Dianic

By earth and moon, by breath and flame,  
this place is made sacred.

I cast this circle as a boundary of truth,  
a circle of protection,  
a circle of blessing,  
a circle of the Goddess.

O Diana,  
Bright Lady of the Moon,  
Mother of the wild places,  
Keeper of women’s mysteries,  
be present in this circle.

I name the matter of this rite:  
may this YC application be accepted,  
and may BD pass smoothly, clearly, and in right order.

Let the path open where it may open in freedom.  
Let the right doors recognize the right work.  
Let preparation, speech, judgment, timing, and response  
move with clarity and good fortune.

O Diana,  
look upon this application, this process, and this passage.

Where there is fear, let there be steady breath.  
Where there is confusion, let there be inner knowing.  
Where there is delay, let there be patient strength.  
Where there is uncertainty, let there be clear signs.  
Where there is opportunity, let it unfold rightly.  
Where there is success, let it come without theft, coercion, or harm.

This blessing seeks not to dispossess another,  
not to diminish another’s portion,  
not to bend an unwilling will,  
but to strengthen what is true, prepared, and worthy.

All acts of love and pleasure are my rituals.

I place within this circle  
gratitude, focus, clean intention, and the light of the Moon.

By the waxing, full, and waning Moon,  
by the dark and returning Moon,  
may what is true be strengthened,  
may what is harmful be dissolved,  
may what belongs to this path come near,  
may what is not meant depart in peace.

For this YC application and the smooth passing of BD,  
I ask blessing, clarity, right timing, and right unfolding.

An it harm none, do what ye will.

O Diana,  
I thank you for your presence.  
Remain if you will,  
depart if you must,  
with blessing between us.

The circle is open,  
but unbroken.  
Merry meet,  
merry part,  
and merry meet again.

Let this working be clean, free, and harmless.  
Let it bind no unwilling heart.  
Let it cross no oath-bound door.  
Let all force return to balance,  
all excess fall away,  
and all blessing remain only where it may dwell in freedom.

## Dievturība（拉脱维亚）

Dievs, Dieviņ, labais devēj,  
stāv pie šī nodoma,  
stāv pie YC pieteikuma,  
stāv pie BD pārbaudes.

Dievs, dod man kalnā kāpt,  
Ne no kalna lejiņā;  
Dievs, dod man otram dot,  
Ne no otra mīļi lūgt.

Par šo YC pieteikumu un BD pārbaudi es saku taisnu vārdu:  
lai doma ir skaidra,  
lai darbs ir godīgs,  
lai ceļš ir taisns,  
lai lēmums nāk labā laikā un taisnā kārtā,  
lai uzņemšana izdodas, ja tā saskan ar godu, darbu un tikumu,  
lai BD pārbaude norit mierīgi, skaidri un sekmīgi,  
ne atņemot cita labumu, ne mazinot cita ceļu, ne darot pāri nevienam.

Dod, Dieviņi, otram dot,  
Ne no otra mīļi lūgt;  
Otram devu, sev palika,  
Savu mūžu dzīvojot.

Dievs, Dieviņ, labais devēj,  
pieņem šo vārdu par šo nodomu,  
pieņem šo dainu par YC pieteikumu un BD pārbaudi.

Dievs, dod man kalnā kāpt,  
Ne no kalna lejiņā.

Lai vārds paliek dainā,  
lai darbs paliek tikumā,  
lai sirds paliek mierā,  
lai viss top bez ļauna, bez piespiešanas, bez sveša zaudējuma.

Lai top.

---

## 巴斯克 Sorginak 复兴

Ni naiz bidearen eskatzailea.  
Hitz hau nire ahoan, arnasa nire bularrean, lurra nire oinen azpian.

Agur, Mari Anbotoko Dama.  
Agur, Lurraren bihotzeko andrea.  
Entzun nire hitza, entzun nire arnasa.

Sasi guztien gainetik eta laino guztien azpitik.  
Gezurra behera, egia gora.  
Iluna behera, argia gora.

Nire eskaria hau da:  
YC eskaera onartua izan dadila;  
BD bidea garbi, zuzen eta ongi gainditua izan dadila;  
ate egokiak ireki daitezela,  
hitza bere lekuan gera dadila,  
eta gertakari hau argitasunez eta bakez bete dadila.

Gertakari honen inguruan,  
lotura gaiztoa askatu dadila,  
bidea garbi ager dadila,  
hitza zuzen gera dadila.

Eguzki amandrea, argitu bidea.  
Ilargi amandrea, gorde isila.  
Lurra, hartu mina.  
Haizea, eraman beldurra.  
Ura, garbitu aztarna.  
Sua, piztu indarra.

Ez dut inoren zoria kendu nahi.  
Ez dut inoren bizi-indarra laburtu nahi.  
Ez dut kalterik nahi.  
Ez dut inor behartu nahi.  
Ez dut gezurrik zin egiten.  
Ez dut sorgin izena gaizki erabiltzen.

Mari Anbotoko Dama,  
nire hitza entzuna izan dadila,  
nire muga gordea izan dadila,  
nire bidea argitua izan dadila.

Arnasa garbi itzul dadila bularrera.  
Oinak lasai gera daitezela lurrean.  
Eskuak hutsik eta bihotza zuzen gera daitezela.  
Kalterik gabe, behartzerik gabe, gezurrik gabe.

Sasi guztien gainetik eta laino guztien azpitik.  
Gezurra behera, egia gora.  
Iluna behera, argia gora.  
Hala bedi.

---

## 威卡 Alexandrian

I stand within the Circle, in perfect love and perfect trust.  
Let all within this rite be bounded by the Rede:  
An it harm none, do what ye will.

By Air, by Fire, by Water, by Earth,  
this Circle is cast and sealed.  
Between the worlds, and in the presence of the Mighty Ones,  
let this rite be held for the acceptance of this YC application and the smooth passing of BD.

Ye Lords of the Watchtowers of the East,  
powers of Air,  
I do summon, stir, and call you up,  
to witness and guard this rite.

Ye Lords of the Watchtowers of the South,  
powers of Fire,  
I do summon, stir, and call you up,  
to witness and guard this rite.

Ye Lords of the Watchtowers of the West,  
powers of Water,  
I do summon, stir, and call you up,  
to witness and guard this rite.

Ye Lords of the Watchtowers of the North,  
powers of Earth,  
I do summon, stir, and call you up,  
to witness and guard this rite.

O Great Mother, Lady of the Moon,  
source of wisdom, grace, and right unfolding,  
receive this prayer for the YC application to be accepted,  
and for BD to pass smoothly in truth, clarity, and good order.

O Horned One, Lord of the Greenwood,  
guardian of life, death, and return,  
receive this prayer for strength, timing, courage, and rightful success,  
that every necessary path may open without harm.

Eko Eko Azarak,  
Eko Eko Zomelak,  
Eko Eko Azarak,  
Eko Eko Zomelak.

For this YC application,  
for BD and all due review, decision, and passage,  
for acceptance, smooth progress, and a clear favorable outcome,  
within right will, right boundary, and harm to none,  
let the prayer be shaped in truth.

Let this success seek not to dispossess another,  
nor to diminish another’s rightful chance, fortune, health, or life.  
Let obstacles be removed by just and harmless means;  
let confusion be clarified, delays be eased, and merit be seen.

So mote it be.

Ye Lords of the Watchtowers of the North,  
powers of Earth,  
I thank you for witnessing and guarding this rite.  
Hail and farewell.

Ye Lords of the Watchtowers of the West,  
powers of Water,  
I thank you for witnessing and guarding this rite.  
Hail and farewell.

Ye Lords of the Watchtowers of the South,  
powers of Fire,  
I thank you for witnessing and guarding this rite.  
Hail and farewell.

Ye Lords of the Watchtowers of the East,  
powers of Air,  
I thank you for witnessing and guarding this rite.  
Hail and farewell.

The Circle is open, but unbroken.  
Merry meet, merry part, and merry meet again.

If any word has strayed beyond right will,  
let it fall away now and return to Earth as harmless dust.  
By breath, by body, by ground beneath, this rite is closed and made clean.  
An it harm none, do what ye will.

Blessed be.

---

## 威卡 Gardnerian

In this place, in this hour, I stand between the worlds,  
with clean hands, clear speech, and a will held in Perfect Love and Perfect Trust.

I conjure thee, O Circle of Power,  
that thou beest a boundary between the world of men and the realms of the Mighty Ones,  
a guardian and a meeting-place for the working of this event:  
that the YC application be received favorably,  
and that the BD process pass smoothly, lawfully, and in right measure.

Lady of the Moon, Great Mother, Bright One, Queen of the secret place,  
hear the words spoken within this circle.

Whenever ye have need of anything,  
once in the month, and better it be when the moon is full,  
then shall ye assemble in some desert place,  
or in a forest all together join  
to adore the potent spirit of your queen.

Horned One, Lord of the wildwood, keeper of life and death,  
stand apart in thy own power and witness this working.

Before the Lady I speak the need:  
May the path of this YC application be opened with clarity, merit, right timing, and good reception;  
may the BD review, decision, and passage proceed without confusion, obstruction, or needless delay.

Before the Lord I speak the boundary:  
Let this prayer harm none, bind none, coerce none, and deceive none;  
let it seek no one’s loss, no one’s dispossession, no shortening of another’s fortune, life, or rightful opportunity.

Let this prayer be for acceptance, smooth passage, honest success, and good alignment,  
harming none, binding none against the true will,  
and turning aside falsehood, fear, and ill-wrought force.

Eko, Eko, Azarak,  
Eko, Eko, Zomelak.

By earth, let this intention take lawful root.  
By air, let this intention be known in clarity.  
By fire, let this intention be quickened without harm.  
By water, let this intention flow in peace.

Lady of the Moon, receive this prayer.  
Horned One, witness this prayer.  
Mighty Ones of the circle, keep it within right measure.

As the cup and the bread are blessed in fellowship,  
so may the work be whole:  
for the YC application, for the BD passage,  
according to freedom, consent, truth, and right outcome.

What is not rightful, let it fall away cleanly.  
What is fearful, let it be washed from the heart.  
What is oathbound, let it remain untouched.  
What is public, simple, and sincere, let it stand in peace.

The circle is open, yet unbroken.  
Merry meet, and merry part, and merry meet again.

---

## 威卡 Eclectic

I stand within the circle between the worlds,  
in perfect love and perfect trust,  
for this event: the YC application being accepted and BD passing smoothly.

By earth and sea and sky,  
let this circle be cast and sealed.  
What enters here shall enter in truth;  
what leaves here shall leave in peace.

Guardians of the Watchtowers of the East, powers of Air,  
I do summon, stir, and call you up,  
to witness this rite for the YC application and BD review.

Guardians of the Watchtowers of the South, powers of Fire,  
I do summon, stir, and call you up,  
to witness this rite for the YC application and BD review.

Guardians of the Watchtowers of the West, powers of Water,  
I do summon, stir, and call you up,  
to witness this rite for the YC application and BD review.

Guardians of the Watchtowers of the North, powers of Earth,  
I do summon, stir, and call you up,  
to witness this rite for the YC application and BD review.

Great Mother,  
Listen to the words of the Great Mother,  
who of old was called Artemis, Astarte, Dione, Melusine,  
Aphrodite, Cerridwen, Diana, Arionrhod, Brigid, and by many other names.  
All acts of love and pleasure are my rituals.  
Be present to this prayer for the YC application and BD review.

Horned One,  
Lord of the wildwood, keeper of life, death, and return,  
be present to this prayer for the YC application and BD review.

An it harm none, do what ye will.

Therefore I speak only within willing, rightful, and harmless bounds:  
May this YC application be received with clarity, merit, and favorable regard;  
may BD pass smoothly through every fitting review, meeting, and decision;  
may the right doors open at the right time, without force, deceit, or coercion.  
I do not seek to take another’s rightful place, diminish another’s path, or dispossess any being of their good.  
Let no will be bound.  
Let no heart be compelled.  
Let no life be diminished.  
Let what is not mine return to its own place.  
Let what is mine stand clear in truth.

Eko Eko Azarak,  
Eko Eko Zomelak,  
Eko Eko Azarak,  
Eko Eko Zomelak.

For the YC application and BD review,  
may the crooked be made clear,  
may the harmful be made harmless,  
may the hidden be known in right measure,  
may the needed path open without coercion.

If any word of this rite has exceeded rightful boundary,  
I withdraw it now.  
If any force has been called beyond consent,  
I release it now.  
If any bond has been made against true will,  
I unmake it now.  
Peace to all beings touched by this prayer.

Great Mother, I thank you and release you.  
Go if you must, stay if you will.  
Hail and farewell.

Horned One, I thank you and release you.  
Go if you must, stay if you will.  
Hail and farewell.

Guardians of the Watchtowers of the North, powers of Earth,  
I thank you and release you.  
Hail and farewell.

Guardians of the Watchtowers of the West, powers of Water,  
I thank you and release you.  
Hail and farewell.

Guardians of the Watchtowers of the South, powers of Fire,  
I thank you and release you.  
Hail and farewell.

Guardians of the Watchtowers of the East, powers of Air,  
I thank you and release you.  
Hail and farewell.

The circle is open, but unbroken.  
Merry meet, merry part, and merry meet again.  
So mote it be.

---

## Finnish Suomenusko

Alku aina, alku aina,  
sana synty, virsi nousi.

Minä sanani sanon,  
hiljaisesta mielestä,  
selvästä sydämestä,  
tämän hetken kynnyksellä.

Oi Ukko, ylijumala,  
taivahallinen jumala,  
kuule sanat suustani,  
ota virsi viereltäni.

Mieleni minun tekevi,  
aivoni ajattelevi,  
lähteäni laulamahan,  
saa’ani sanelemahan.

Sanat suustani sulavat,  
puhe’et putoelevat,  
kielelleni kerkiävät,  
hampahilleni hajoovat.

Synty syvä, synty vanha,  
tien synty ja portin alku,  
tule tietä myöten tähän,  
näytä juuri, näytä alku,  
näytä oikea omasi.

Ei pahaksi, ei panoksi,  
ei kateeksi, ei kiroukseksi,  
ei toisen onnen ottamiseksi,  
ei kenenkään osan lyhentämiseksi,  
vaan oikeaksi avuksi  
tämän YC-hakemuksen hyväksymisen  
ja BD-vaiheen suotuisan läpimenon asiassa.

Oi Ukko, ylijumala,  
taivahallinen jumala,  
avaa tie oikea,  
selvennä sana suora,  
vahvista hyvä vastaus,  
anna rauha päätökseen,  
anna suoja kulkemiseen,  
anna onni omalle kohdalle  
ilman vahinkoa toisille.

Tie, joka on oikea, auetkoon;  
ovi, joka on sovelias, avautukoon;  
sana, joka on tosi, kuulukoon;  
työ, joka on hyvä, kantakoon.

Mikä on väärin lausuttu,  
se takaisin peräytyköön.  
Mikä on pahoin pantu,  
se omaan sijaansa palatkoon.  
Mikä on oikein sanottu,  
se paikalleen asettukoon.

Jos sana väärin kulki,  
se nyt seisatkoot.  
Jos tahto väärin nousi,  
se nyt taittukoot.  
En käske pahaan, en kiroa,  
en murra toisen tahtoa,  
vaan pyydän apua oikeaan.

Mene väki sijallesi,  
mene voima kohdallesi,  
mene sana synnyllesi,  
mene rauha rinnalleni.

Ukko ylinen, kuule lempeästi;  
haltijat hyvät, pysykää rauhassa;  
väet vanhat, palatkaa omillenne.  
Anteeksi, jos sana horjui;  
anteeksi, jos mieli hairahti.  
Rauha maahan, rauha mieleen,  
valo päälle, tie etehen.

Näin sanon, näin sidon,  
sanan suuhun, työn teloille,  
rauhan maahan, valon päälle,  
hyvän osaksi, pahan poissa.

---

## 匈牙利 Ősmagyar Vallás

Istenem, Magyarok Istene,  
hallgasd meg e tiszta kérést.

Őseim, apáim és anyáim,  
kik előttem jártatok,  
álljatok mögöttem tiszta emlékezettel,  
ne ártással, ne haraggal,  
hanem áldással.

Áldjon meg az Isten,  
őrizzen meg az Isten,  
fordítsa jóra a YC-jelentkezés dolgát,  
hogy felvételt nyerjen,  
és a BD ügye rendben, békével, akadály nélkül átmenjen.

Adjon Isten jó utat ennek az eseménynek.  
Legyen előtte nyitott kapu,  
mögötte békesség,  
mellette jó társ,  
felette tiszta ég.

Adjon Isten világosságot a döntők elméjébe,  
jó mértéket a szóba,  
erős tartást a cselekedetbe,  
tiszta szerencsét az útra,  
és igaz rendet minden lépésbe.

Nem kérek más kárából nyereséget,  
nem kérek más kenyerének elvételét,  
nem kérek más életének rövidülését.  
Ami jön, igaz úton jöjjön,  
ami megnyílik, tiszta rend szerint nyíljon meg.

Ami ártó szó,  
ami rossz kötés,  
ami zavar vagy akadály e dolog köré tapad,  
az oldódjék el,  
menjen vissza a semmibe,  
ne bántson senkit,  
ne térjen ártással.

Köszönöm az eget fölöttem,  
a földet alattam,  
a tüzet, mely tisztán világít,  
a vizet, mely békén folyik,  
a kenyeret, mely életet tart,  
és az ősök emlékezetét, mely jó útra int.

Nem mondok hamis esküt,  
nem kérek ártást,  
nem gyalázom az ősöket,  
nem töröm meg a kenyeret haraggal,  
nem szennyezem a tüzet rossz szóval,  
nem lépem át a küszöböt tisztelet nélkül.  
Alázattal szólok, nem táltosként, nem regösként,  
hanem tiszta szívű kérőként.

Áldás legyen ezen az úton,  
áldás legyen a YC-jelentkezésen,  
áldás legyen a BD rendes átmenetelén,  
áldás legyen azon, ami igaz és tiszta.

Úgy legyen.  
Áldás, békesség.

---

## Maausk（爱沙尼亚）

Tere, püha hiis.  
Tere, püha maa.  
Tere, Maaema.

Mina, paluja,  
seisan siin,  
puhta meelega ja rahuliku sõnaga.

Tere, esivanemad.  
Tere, isade-isade hinged.  
Tere, emade-emade hinged.  
Mäletan teid nimega ja nimeta,  
lähedalt ja kaugelt,  
vere, kodu ja maa kaudu.

Maaema,  
hoia seda ettevõtmist.  
Püha hiis,  
hoia seda teed.  
Esivanemad,  
andke selge meel,  
andke õiged sõnad,  
andke tugev süda.

Tulgu hea tee ja õige aeg:  
et YC taotlus leiaks vastuvõtmise,  
et BD kulgeks selgelt ja sujuvalt,  
et õiged uksed avaneksid õigel ajal,  
et töö, sõna ja tegu oleksid kooskõlas.

Ärgu see õnn võtku teise õnne.  
Ärgu see tee sulgegu teise teed.  
Ärgu see edu sündigu kahju, pettuse ega sundimise läbi.

Taara avita.  
Taara avita.  
Taara avita.

Katkegu kuri sõna.  
Vaibugu halb tahe.  
Lahkugu võõras vari.  
Jäägu süda kindlaks,  
mõte selgeks,  
samm õigeks.

Maa all rahu.  
Maa peal rahu.  
Taeva all rahu.  
Kodus rahu.  
Südames rahu.

Mis on antud, olgu puhas.  
Mis on öeldud, olgu aus.  
Mis on palutud, olgu kooskõlas maa, vee, tule ja tuulega.

Olgu hea osa maale.  
Olgu hea osa kodule.  
Olgu hea osa suguvõsale.  
Olgu hea osa kõigile elavatele.

Kui mu sõna on eksinud,  
palun andeks, püha paik.  
Kui mu meel on olnud hooletu,  
palun andeks, Maaema.  
Kui mu tegu on olnud kohatu,  
palun andeks, esivanemad.

Jäägu paik puhtaks.  
Jäägu maa puhtaks.  
Jäägu süda puhtaks.  
Jäägu tänu, mitte kaup.  
Jäägu au, mitte uhkus.

Tänu, püha hiis.  
Tänu, Maaema.  
Tänu, esivanemad.

Taara avita.  
Nõnda olgu.

---

## Rodnovery（斯拉夫）

Чур, чур, чур.  
Межа чиста, слово право, сердце крепко.

Аз есмь молящийся.  
Стаю пред огнем, землею и небом.  
Не во зло, не во кривду, но во правду.

Слава Роду.  
Слава Предкам.  
Предки благие, слышите слово мое.  
Помяните добром путь живых.

Слава тебе, Дажьбоже.  
Гой, Дажьбоже, гой.  
Приди на глас мой.  
Прими требу чистую: хлеб, соль и чистую воду — во славу, не в торг.

За это дело слово мое:  
да будет заявка в YC принята благим образом,  
да пройдет BD ровно, ясно и успешно,  
да откроется верная дорога, крепкое слово и добрая встреча.

Не кляну ложно.  
Не прошу кривды.  
Не беру чужой воли.  
Не отнимаю чужой доли, чужого счастья и чужого срока.  
Да уйдут преграды без вреда для людей.  
Да будет по Прави, по чести, по мере.

Слава Дажьбогу.  
Слава Роду.  
Слава Предкам.

Треба чиста, слово мирно, сердце прямо.  
За принятое — благодарение; за непринятое — разумение.  
Тако бысть, тако еси, тако буди.  
Чур.

---

## 凯尔特德鲁伊（OBOD / ADF / AODA）

[净化与定界]  
Â dŵr glân, ag anadl dawel, a chylch o heddwch:  
Awen, Awen, Awen.

[向土地与三界致敬]  
Anrhydedd i’r ddaear sydd yn ein cynnal,  
i’r dŵr sydd yn llifo,  
i’r gwynt sydd yn symud,  
i’r tân sydd yn goleuo.  

Anrhydedd i’r Uwchfyd, i’r Byd hwn, ac i’r Isfyd.  
Anrhydedd i ysbrydion y lle,  
ac i bob bod sy’n cadw cytgord y tir.

[陈明目的]  
Pwrpas y weddi hon yw:  
boed i’r cais YC gael ei dderbyn,  
a boed i BD basio’n rhwydd ac yn gyfiawn.  

Na cheisir niwed i neb,  
na gorfodaeth ar ewyllys neb,  
na llwyddiant drwy amddifadu eraill,  
na budd drwy dorri cytgord y ddaear, y gymuned, na’r holl fodau.

[分别致敬土地灵、祖灵、Awen]  
Ysbrydion y lle, derbyniwch y cyfarchiad hwn mewn parch.  
Hynafiaid anrhydeddus, rhai a fu o’n blaenau, tystiwch i’r weddi hon.  
Awen sanctaidd, llifa fel goleuni, doethineb, a nerth tawel.

Awen, Awen, Awen.  
Awen, Awen, Awen.  
Awen, Awen, Awen.

[正行：Gweddi'r Derwydd / The Druid's Prayer]  
Dyro, Dduw, dy nawdd;  
Ac yn nawdd, nerth;  
Ac yn nerth, deall;  
Ac yn neall, gwybod;  
Ac yngwybod, gwybod y cyfiawn;  
Ac yngwybod y cyfiawn, ei garu;  
Ac o garu, caru pob hanfod;  
Ac ymhob hanfod, caru Duw;  
Duw a phob daioni.

[供献与请求]  
Boed nawdd dros y cais YC.  
Boed nerth dros BD yn y prawf a’r broses.  
Boed deall yn clirio pob dryswch.  
Boed gwybod y cyfiawn yn arwain pob penderfyniad.  
Boed caru pob hanfod yn cadw’r canlyniad mewn tegwch, parch, a heddwch.  

Cyflwynir yr offrwm glân hwn—dŵr, anadl, a diolchgarwch—  
i’r ddaear ac i’r rhai anrhydeddus,  
nid fel cyfnewid, ond fel mawl a diolch.

[静默承接]  
Awen, Awen, Awen.

[感谢诸灵]  
Diolch i’r ddaear.  
Diolch i ysbrydion y lle.  
Diolch i’r hynafiaid anrhydeddus.  
Diolch i Awen.  
Boed i bob un ddychwelyd mewn heddwch,  
a boed i’r weddi hon weithio yn unig drwy ffyrdd cyfiawn.

[关闭与回归]  
Mae’r geiriau wedi eu llefaru;  
boed iddynt wreiddio mewn gwirionedd da.  
Awen, Awen, Awen.

---

## Heathenry / Ásatrú

Friðr sé hér.  
Helga ek þenna stað til fríðar ok sannra orða.

Ek kalla á Óðinn,  
Hangatýr, Farmatýr, Fimbultýr,  
heyr orð mín.

Heill dagr, heilir dags synir,  
heil nótt ok nipt!  
Óreiðum augum lítið okkr þinig,  
ok gefið sitjendum sigr.

Heilir æsir, heilar ásynjur,  
heil sjá in fjölnýta fold!  
Mál ok manvit gefið okkr mærum tveim,  
ok læknishendr, meðan lifum.

Ek ber fram orð, hug ok þökk.  
Ek bið um at YC-umsókn verði viðtekin,  
ok at BD gangi greiðliga í gegn.  
Lát þetta mál standa í friði,  
með heilum hug, heilum orðum, heilum verkum.

Brimrúnar skaltu kunna,  
ef þú vilt borgit hafa  
á sundi seglmörum.

Gef leið yfir brim þessa atburðar,  
gef sigr án níðs,  
gef greiða ferð án skaða.  
Ek bið eigi at taka gæfu annarra,  
né skerða líf, hlut eða heill annarra.

Ek geri eigi níð.  
Ek bind eigi vilja annars.  
Ek sver eigi ósannan eið.  
Orð mín standi innan friðar.

Óðinn, tak við orðum mínum.  
Gef þessu máli sigr, ef þat er rétt, heilt ok innan friðar.

Svá sé.  
Friðr með oss.

---

## Romuva（立陶宛）

Ugnie šventa, Gabija,  
būk rami, būk gera,  
būk soti ant savo vietos.

Gabija, sukurta, pakurta,  
neužgauk, negesk,  
saugok kelią, žodį ir širdies darną.

Vėlelės mūsų,  
ateikit, pasivaišinkit,  
prisiminkit gerąsias giminės šaknis,  
palaiminkit dorą žingsnį ir aiškų protą.

Saulele motule, šviesioji,  
kilk per rasą, kilk per lauką,  
apšviesk mintį, sutvirtink žodį,  
tegu akys mato tiesų kelią,  
tegu rankos atlieka, kas pradėta,  
tegu durys atsiveria be prievartos ir be skriaudos.

Priimkite tyrą duoną, medaus lašą, švarų vandenį,  
ne kaip mainą, bet kaip pagarbą,  
kaip dainą prie ugnies,  
kaip ramų atminimą žemei ir protėviams.

Tegu ši YC paraiška būna priimta,  
tegu BD praeina sklandžiai,  
tegu geri žodžiai randa gerą klausą,  
tegu kliūtys išsisklaido kaip migla prie saulės.  
Neprašome atimti kito dalios,  
neprašome trumpinti kito kelio,  
tik prašome teisingos vietos, darnaus sprendimo  
ir palaimos tam, kas dera su tiesa.

Žemynėle žiedkelėle,  
žydėk rugiais, kviečiais,  
miežiais ir visais javais.  
Laikyk darną žemėje,  
laikyk darną darbuose,  
laikyk darną širdyje.

Darna tegu būna širdyje,  
darna tegu būna namuose,  
darna tegu būna žemėje.

Ugnie šventa, Gabija,  
ačiū už šviesą,  
ačiū už šilumą,  
lik rami, lik gera.

Tegu ši malda nieko neverčia, nieko nekeikia, nieko nežemina;  
tegu ji eina tik su švaria ugnimi, švariu žodžiu ir švaria dovana.  
Tegu daina grįžta į tylą,  
tegu protėviai grįžta į ramybę,  
tegu darna pasilieka.

---

## Kemetism

ỉw=ỉ r ḏd mdw m mꜣꜥt.  
ỉb=ỉ wꜥb, r=ỉ mꜣꜥ, ḏrt=ỉ wꜥbt.  
n ỉnk ỉr ỉsft.  
n ỉnk ḥḏ ḥtpw nṯrw.  
n ỉnk šd mꜣꜥt.

dwꜣ Rꜥ.  
dwꜣ Rꜥ m wbn=f m ꜣḫt.  
ỉꜣw n=k, Rꜥ, nb pt, nb ꜣḫt, nb wbnw.  
di=k mꜣꜥt r st=s, di=k ḥtp r ỉb n dwꜣw pn.

ḥtp dỉ nsw Rꜥ nb pt.  
dỉ=f prt-ḫrw:  
t ḥnqt, kꜣw ꜣpdw, šs mnḫt,  
snṯr mrḥt, ḫt nb(t) nfr(t) wꜥb(t),  
n kꜣ n dwꜣw pn.

ỉb=ỉ n mwt=ỉ,  
ỉb=ỉ n ḫprw=ỉ,  
m ḏd r=ỉ m mꜣꜥty,  
m ỉr ḫft r=ỉ m-bꜣḥ nṯr ꜥꜣ.  
ỉb=ỉ n mwt=ỉ,  
m ḫsf r=ỉ m ḏꜣḏꜣt.

n ỉnk ỉr ỉsft.  
n ỉnk ḏd grg.  
n ỉnk ỉṯỉ ḫt n nṯr.  
n ỉnk ỉṯỉ ḫt n ꜣḫ.  
n ỉnk ḥtm rn.  
n ỉnk sḫm r ḏrt ḫft mꜣꜥt.  
n ỉnk ỉṯỉ šꜥw n ky.  
n ỉnk ḏr ꜥnḫ n ky.

愿此次 YC 申请被录取，BD 顺利通过；不夺他人福报，不损他人寿数，不以虚言取胜，不以损害成事，唯愿此事安置于 mꜣꜥt 之中。

di=k wp wꜣt nfrt.  
di=k sḏm mdw m mꜣꜥt.  
di=k šspw nfrw, wḏꜣ ḏꜣḏꜣt, ḥtp ỉb.  
di=k ḫpr spr nfr pn m mꜣꜥt, nn ỉsft ỉm=f.  
di=k wꜣḏ ỉb, snb ẖt, ḥtp pr, mꜣꜥ ḫrw.  
di=k wḏꜣ, snb, ꜥnḫ m mꜣꜥt.

dwꜣ Rꜥ.  
mꜣꜥt rꜥ nb.  
ḥtp n nṯrw, ḥtp n ꜣḫw.  
ḥtp n tꜣ, ḥtp n pt, ḥtp n ỉb.  
snṯr wꜥb, mw wꜥb, mdw mꜣꜥ.  
ỉsft ḫr, mꜣꜥt ḥr st=s.  
ḥtp n dwꜣw pn, mꜣꜥ ḫrw.

## Abakuá

Con licencia de los mayores y de los hermanos, en el corazón de la plaza.  
Saludo a Ékue y a Abasí, bajo mirada limpia y palabra contenida.  
Por esta petición: que la solicitud de YC sea aceptada y que BD pase con buen camino.  
Que el bien venga sin quitar el bien ajeno, sin cerrar camino de otro, sin dañar nombre ni vida.  
Honor a los ancestros, a los hermanos, y al fundamento guardado.  
Sin juramento, sin abrir secreto, sin tocar palabra reservada: cerramos con respeto y humildad.

---

## Sami Noaidi

Gula, gula, eatnama vuoiŋŋat.  
Gula, gula, dán báikki vuoiŋŋat.

Mii boahtit ráfis,  
namakeahttá ja čájeheami haga,  
dán eatnama alde.

Dán luođis mii namadat dáhpáhusa: YC-ohcan ja BD-geaidnu.  
Dán luođis mii muitalit áigumuša: čielggas bargu, rievttes sánit, buorre boađus.  
Ále boađe bahá daguin.  
Boađe ráfis, boađe čielggas.

Gula, YC-ohcan.  
Gula, BD-geaidnu.  
Dát YC-ohcan lihkostuvašii ja váldojuvvošii vuostá;  
BD mannášii čađa ráfis, čielgasit ja rievttes áiggis.

Luohti:  
lo lo lo, vuo-oi, vuo-oi,  
na na na, hei-ja, hei-ja,  
YC-ohcan, BD-geaidnu,  
vuo-oi, vuo-oi, na na na.

Doala ráfi.  
Doala čielggasvuođa.  
Doala duohtavuođa.  
Doala rievttes geainnu.  
Doala sániid mat leat duođalaččat,  
doala uvssaid mat leat rievttes rabas.

Ii váldde earáid oasi.  
Ii geahped earáid eallima.  
Ii rihko earáid vuoigatvuođa.  
Ii daga vahága geange geainnus.

Ii gearddu bahás.  
Ii gearddu gillámušas.  
Ii gearddu boastut sániin.  
Ii gearddu čiegus namain.

Dát sáhttá leat doarjjan,  
ii bággun,  
ii čatnan,  
ii vahágin.

Giitu, eatnama vuoiŋŋat.  
Giitu, dán báikki vuoiŋŋat.

Jus dát áigumuš lea boastut dahje menddo čavgat,  
de mii váldit dan ruovttoluotta.  
Jus mii leat gohččon maid ii galgga gohččot,  
de mii luoitit dan dál ráfis.  
Buot vuoiŋŋat mat gullet iežaset báikái,  
mannet ráfis iežaset báikái.  
Mana ráfis.  
Mana iežat báikái.  
Dát luohti lea giddejuvvon.  
Dát sátni lea giddejuvvon.

---

## Stregheria

Sto in questo luogo,  
con cuore fermo e parola chiara.  
Non chiedo dominio, non chiedo danno,  
ma via aperta, difesa giusta, e scioglimento del male.

Diana! Diana! Diana!  
Regina delle streghe!  
E della notte oscura,  
E di tutta la natura,  
Di tutti gli elementi,  
Dell'acqua e del fuoco,  
Della terra e dell'aria,  
Di tutte le stelle,  
Diana! Diana! Diana!

Per questo evento,  
io nomino davanti a te questa cosa:  
che questa domanda a YC sia accolta,  
e che BD passi con buon esito,  
secondo giustizia, chiarezza e via favorevole.

Non sia preso il bene d’altri,  
non sia tolta fortuna ad alcuno,  
non sia abbreviata vita né pace di nessuno.  
Ciò che è giusto venga vicino;  
ciò che è falso si separi;  
ciò che è nocivo perda presa.

Se vi è nodo, malocchio, paura, inganno, ritardo, confusione,  
o legame non giusto sopra questo cammino,  
sia sciolto senza vendetta.  
Se vi è strada chiusa,  
sia aperta senza violenza.  
Se vi è parola falsa,  
cada senza danno innocente.  
Se vi è ombra sopra questo evento,  
sia allontanata senza colpire chi non deve essere colpito.

Diana! Diana! Diana!  
Regina delle streghe!  
E della notte oscura,  
E di tutta la natura,  
Di tutti gli elementi,  
Dell'acqua e del fuoco,  
Della terra e dell'aria,  
Di tutte le stelle,  
Diana! Diana! Diana!

Per la notte, per la luna, per la terra e per l'aria,  
custodisci questo cammino di domanda, esame, giudizio e risposta.  
Rendi limpida la parola, saldo il cuore, favorevole l’incontro,  
aperta la porta che può aprirsi in modo giusto.

Io lego la mia parola a questo limite:  
non per costringere,  
non per ferire,  
non per rubare volontà,  
non per maleficio né dominio,  
ma per liberare, proteggere, chiarire.

Diana, ricevi questa voce.  
Diana, ascolta questa domanda.  
Diana, lascia che il cammino sia netto.

Ogni timore sia lavato via come polvere dall’acqua;  
ogni nodo non giusto sia sciolto nell’aria;  
ogni ombra cada nella terra senza nuocere;  
ogni forza disordinata si spenga nel fuoco puro.

Va' in pace, o Regina della notte.  
La parola è detta.  
Il cerchio della voce si chiude in quiete.  
Così sia.

---

## Bwiti

A Nzame,  
Tata Nzame,  
Nzame ye Mebeghe,  
Nzame a kana,  
Nzame a bota.

A Kombe,  
Tata Kombe,  
Kombe a langa nzila,  
Kombe a yene meso.

A mimbiri,  
A mimbiri ya Bwiti,  
A mikuku mia mvama,  
boya, boya, boya.

Me tele na miso ma Nzame,  
me tele na miso ma Kombe,  
me tele na miso ma mimbiri,  
me tele na miso ma mikuku.

Ngombi, ngombi, ngombi,  
vova mimbiri,  
vova nzila,  
vova motema.

Banzi ba Bwiti:  
A Nzame, e-e.  
A Kombe, e-e.  
A mimbiri, e-e.  
A mikuku, e-e.  
Bwiti, bwiti, bwiti.

愿此次 YC 申请被录取，BD 顺利通过；愿道路开启，心意清明，言辞端正，机缘相合；不夺他人福报，不损他人寿数，不以恶意求成，只愿障碍退散、正路显明。

Nzame,  
tala mambu,  
tala nzila,  
tala motema.

Mikuku mia mvama,  
bomba nzila,  
sukula motema,  
kangula nzila,  
kata mambu mabe na nzila.

A Nzame,  
A Kombe,  
A mimbiri,  
A mikuku,  
me tondi,  
me tondi,  
me tondi.

Bwiti a yene.  
Bwiti a vova.  
Bwiti a kangula nzila.  
Ayo.

---

## Religio Romana / Cultus Deorum

Favete linguis; pura mente, pura prece, recta voluntate ad sacrum accedo.  

Mercuri, te precor quaesoque uti sies volens propitius  
mihi,  
domo familiaeque meae,  
rebusque meis.

Quod bonum faustum felix fortunatumque sit  
mihi  
domo familiaeque meae.

Uti tu morbos visos invisosque,  
viduertatem vastitudinemque,  
calamitates intemperiasque prohibessis  
defendas averruncesque  
a me,  
a domo familiaque mea,  
ab hac petitione atque hoc negotio.

Uti tu, si fas est et aequum est,  
petitionem YC receptam facias,  
atque transitum BD lenem, ordinatum, prosperumque sinas;  
ut verba recta, consilia clara, responsa opportuna,  
fides bona et fortuna honesta adsint.

Ne cuiquam bona eripiantur,  
ne cuius vita minuatur,  
ne alterius sors iniuste prematur;  
sed obstacula sine iniuria avertantur,  
et quod iustum est bene proveniat.

Harumce rerum ergo,  
Mercuri,  
macte hac laude pia esto.  
Macte virtute esto.  
Preces nuncupo, non mercedem, non pactum:  
haec verba tibi pie dicata sunto  
pro bono, fausto, felici, fortunatoque eventu.

Mercuri,  
uti sies volens propitius  
mihi,  
domo familiaeque meae,  
ita te precor quaesoque.

Pax deorum mecum,  
pax deorum domo familiaeque meae,  
pax deorum rebus meis adsit.

Si quid tibi in hoc sacro  
neque rite factum neque dictum est,  
si quid vitii factum est,  
hac prece piaculari piaculum esto.  
Sive deus sive dea es,  
quoium illud sacrum est,  
uti tibi ius est  
hac prece piaculari piaculum facere,  
illiusce sacri coercendi ergo,  
harumce rerum ergo,  
macte hac prece piaculari esto.

---

## Bori

Gaisuwa gare ku, iskokin bori.  
Gaisuwa gare ku, iyayen iska.  
Gaisuwa gare ku, masu gida.  

Ya Sarkin Rafi, mai sanin hanya,  
ku ji gaisuwa,  
ku ji magana,  
ku ji murya mai ladabi.  

Ya Sarkin Rafi,  
ba mu zo da gardama ba.  
Ba mu zo da raini ba.  
Ba mu zo da tilasta sauka ba.  
Mun zo da gaisuwa,  
mun zo da natsuwa.  

Ya mai rafi, ya mai hanya,  
hanya ta yi ruwa,  
hanya ta yi santsi,  
hanya ta buɗe ga mai tafiya da gaskiya.  

Maganarmu ita ce:  
a karɓi wannan neman YC da alheri,  
BD kuma ya wuce lafiya,  
ba tare da hayaniya ba,  
ba tare da ruɗani ba,  
ba tare da cutar da wani ba.  

Zuciya tana neman daidaito.  
Hankali yana neman haske.  
Hanya tana neman buɗewa.  
Magana tana neman zama daidai a gaban masu duba ta.  

Ya Sarkin Rafi,  
ku karɓi gaisuwa.  
Ku karɓi magana.  
Ku karɓi alkawarin ladabi:  
ba mu neman kwace rabon wani,  
ba mu neman rage arzikin wani,  
ba mu neman cutar da wani,  
sai dai a kau da cikas,  
a haskaka hanya,  
a tabbatar da abin da ya dace da alheri.  

Ku kawar da sharri.  
Ku raba mu da tsoro.  
Ku raba mu da hayaniya.  
Ku raba mu da ruɗani.  
Ku sa zuciya ta zauna.  
Ku sa baki ya yi daidai.  
Ku sa takardu su yi haske.  
Ku sa hanya ta buɗe cikin aminci.  

Idan magana ta yi nauyi, ku sauƙaƙa ta.  
Idan hanya ta rufe, ku buɗe ta.  
Idan tunani ya rikice, ku daidaita shi.  
Idan lokaci ya matso, ku sa natsuwa ta tsaya.  

Ya Sarkin Rafi,  
mun gode da jin gaisuwa.  
Ku koma lafiya.  
Ku bar hanya lafiya.  
Ku bar gida lafiya.  
Ku bar zuciya lafiya.  

Waka ta tsaya.  
Murya ta yi shiru.  
Ba a kiran sauka.  
Ba a motsa doki.  
Idan kalma ta kuskure, a lafa ta.  
Idan hanya ta buƙaci gyara, mai-bori ya gyara da ladabi.  
Gaisuwa ta cika.  
Magana ta rufe.  
Amin.

---

## 坎东布雷 Candomblé

Agô, agô, agô.

Èṣù, mo júbà.  
Laróyè Èṣù.

Mojúbà àwọn àgbà.  
Mojúbà ilé àṣẹ.

Mojúbà Èṣù.  
Laróyè Èṣù.

Èṣù, gbọ́ ohùn wa.  
Kí ire wá.  
Kí àlàáfíà wà ní ọ̀nà yìí.  
Kí àṣẹ rere wá sí ìbéèrè YC.  
Kí ìbéèrè YC gba ìtẹ́wọ́gbà.  
Kí BD kọjá lọ́nà rere.  
Dáàbò bo ọ̀nà, ṣí ọ̀nà, mú ìdènà kúrò láì ṣe ibi fún ẹnikẹ́ni.  
Kí ìre yìí má gba ìre ẹlòmíràn; kí ó má dín ayé ẹnikẹ́ni kù.

Laróyè Èṣù.  
Èṣù mo júbà.  
Agô, Èṣù.

Àṣẹ.  
Àṣẹ.  
Àṣẹ.

---

## Hellenismos / YSEE

[Καθαρμός]  
Χέρνιψ· καθαρὸς/καθαρὰ προσέρχομαι.  
Ἀπὸ μιάσματος καθαίρομαι, καὶ ἐν εὐσεβείᾳ ἵσταμαι.

[Ἐπίκλησις]  
Κλῦθί μου, ὦ Ἑρμῆ, Διὸς καὶ Μαίας υἱέ, Κυλλήνιε, διάκτορε, ἐριούνιε, ἄγγελε ἀθανάτων.  
Ἵλαθι καὶ δέξαι τήνδε εὐχήν.

[Ὕμνος]  
Ὁμηρικὸς Ὕμνος ΙΗʹ εἰς Ἑρμῆν.

Ἑρμῆν ὕμνει, Μοῦσα, Διὸς καὶ Μαίης υἱόν,  
Κυλλήνης μεδέοντα καὶ Ἀρκαδίης πολυμήλου,  
ἄγγελον ἀθανάτων, ἐριούνιον, ὃν τέκε Μαῖα,  
νύμφη ἐϋπλόκαμος, Διὸς ἐν φιλότητι μιγεῖσα.  
Καὶ σὺ μὲν οὕτω χαῖρε, Διὸς καὶ Μαίης υἱέ·  
σεῦ δ’ ἐγὼ ἀρξάμενος μεταβήσομαι ἄλλον ἐς ὕμνον.  
Χαῖρ’, Ἑρμῆ, χαριδῶτα, διάκτορε, δῶτορ ἐάων.

[Προσφορά]  
Ὦ Ἑρμῆ, δέξαι θυμίαμα καθαρὸν καὶ σπονδὴν ὕδατος ἢ οἴνου·  
σπονδὴν καθαρὰν προσφέρω, οὐκ ὡς ἐμπόριον, ἀλλ’ ἐν τιμῇ καὶ χάριτι.

[Εὐχή]  
Χαῖρε, ὦ Ἑρμῆ.  
Δὸς τὴν νῦν αἴτησιν πρὸς YC εὐμενῶς δεχθῆναι,  
καὶ τὸ BD εὖ, ὀρθῶς, ἀκωλύτως περατωθῆναι.  
Δὸς λόγον σαφῆ, νοῦν ταχύν, ὁδὸν εὐθεῖαν, καιρὸν ἀγαθόν,  
καὶ τὰ μηνύματα, τὰς κρίσεις, τὰς συντυχίας ἐν τάξει γενέσθαι.  
Μὴ ἀφαιρούμεθα ἀλλοτρίαν μοῖραν, μὴ βλάπτοιμεν ἄλλον,  
ἀλλὰ τὸ συμφέρον ἐν δίκῃ καὶ σωφροσύνῃ γένοιτο.  
Εἴη τάδε κατὰ κόσμον καὶ μὴ παρὰ θέμιν.

[Χάρις καὶ τελευτή]  
Χάριν σοι ἔχω, ὦ Ἑρμῆ, διάκτορε καὶ ἐριούνιε.  
Φύλασσε τὴν ὁδὸν ταύτην ἐν εὐσεβείᾳ, σωφροσύνῃ καὶ δίκῃ.  
Ἀπέστω ὕβρις, ἀπέστω ἀσέβεια, ἀπέστω πᾶν μίασμα·  
καθαρὸς/καθαρὰ προσέρχομαι, καθαρῶς ἀπέρχομαι.  
Χαῖρε, καὶ αὖθις χαῖρε.

---

## Candomblé de Caboclo

Agô, licença.  
Okê Caboclo.  
Okê Aruanda.  
Salve a mata.  
Salve a aldeia.  
Salve os caboclos de pena.  
Salve os caboclos de couro.  
Salve os caboclos de luz.

Venho com respeito, sem demanda e sem mentira.  
Que minha palavra seja direita, que meu coração seja limpo,  
que meu caminho não pise segredo de casa alheia.

Okê Caboclo!  
Okê Caboclo!  
Okê Caboclo!  
Caboclo chegou na aldeia,  
Caboclo chegou no gongá.  
Okê, okê, okê,  
Okê Caboclo no seu jacutá.

Eu vi chover, eu vi relampear,  
Mas mesmo assim o céu estava azul.  
Okê Caboclo, firma sua banda,  
Na força da mata, na luz de Aruanda.

Trago diante dos caboclos este pedido de caminho aberto:  
que esta candidatura à YC seja recebida com bom olhar,  
que a entrevista, a avaliação e a decisão encontrem clareza,  
que o BD passe com firmeza, conversa certa e oportunidade justa.  
Que venha aprovação se estiver no direito, no merecimento e na paz,  
sem tomar o que não é meu,  
sem fechar estrada de ninguém,  
sem diminuir o axé, o pão, a sorte ou a vida de outra pessoa.

Caboclo não tem caminho para caminhar.  
Caminha por cima das folhas,  
Caminha por baixo das folhas,  
Caminha em qualquer lugar.  
Okê Caboclo, abre caminho,  
abre caminho para esta passagem de evento,  
abre caminho para a candidatura à YC,  
abre caminho para o BD passar,  
sem quebrar justiça,  
sem prender vontade de ninguém,  
sem mentira e sem soberba.

Seu Pena Verde, onde é sua aldeia?  
É na mata virgem, onde a lua clareia.  
A sua flecha é certeira,  
Seu bodoque não falha, não.  
Firma, Caboclo, firma a palavra,  
firma a cabeça,  
firma o coração,  
firma a estrada deste pedido.

Salve os caboclos da mata.  
Salve os caboclos da aldeia.  
Salve os caboclos de Aruanda.  
Okê Caboclo.  
Que o que é de paz fique em paz.  
Que o que é de verdade fique em verdade.  
Que o que é de caminho aberto se cumpra no direito e no merecimento.

Caboclo vai embora,  
vai embora para Aruanda.  
Vai com Deus e Nossa Senhora,  
vai firmando a sua banda.  
Okê Caboclo.  
Okê Aruanda.

Recebam somente esta saudação simples e pública,  
sem incorporação, sem consulta, sem obrigação, sem ebó,  
sem segredo de casa, sem folha, sem fumo, sem bebida, sem vela e sem corte.  
Que a palavra volte limpa,  
que a mata guarde em paz,  
que a aldeia abençoe sem excesso,  
e que tudo se encerre com licença, respeito e gratidão.  
Agô, licença.

---

## Akan Akɔmfoɔ

Agoo, agoo, agoo.

Nana Bosom Pa,  
yɛfrɛ wo, yɛfrɛ wo, yɛfrɛ wo.  
Yɛba w’anim wɔ asomdwoe mu.  
Yɛba w’anim a atoro nni yɛn ano.  
Yɛba w’anim a ɔhaw nni yɛn koma mu.

Asɛm a yɛde aba w’anim ne eyi:  
ma此次 YC application no nnye tom wɔ kwan pa so;  
ma BD no ntwam dwoodwoo,  
ma nsɛm a wɔhwehwɛ no nyɛ fann,  
ma adwene pa, kasa pa, ne kwan pa mmue.

Nana Bosom Pa,  
yɛde nsuo kronkron ba w’anim wɔ mpaebɔ mu.  
Gye, tie, na hwɛ.  
Sɛ yɛn ano yɛ nokware a, gye yɛn kasa.  
Sɛ yɛn adwene yɛ fann a, teɛ no ma ɛnyɛ dwoodwoo.  
Sɛ kwan bi yɛ den a, ma ɛnyɛ mmerɛ.  
Sɛ ɔfasu bi wɔ kwan mu a, yi no fi hɔ a obiara renhu amane.

Nana Bosom Pa,  
siw bɔne kwan.  
Yi musuo.  
Yi aniwuo.  
Yi basabasayɛ.  
Ma asomdwoe.  
Ma nkwa.  
Ma adwene pa.  
Ma kasa mu nokware.  
Ma wɔn a wɔhwɛ asɛm no nhu nea ɛyɛ papa.  
Ma nea ɛsɛ sɛ ɛda adi no nna adi fann.

Yɛmpɛ sɛ yɛgye obi nhyira.  
Yɛmpɛ sɛ yɛte obi nkwa so.  
Yɛmpɛ sɛ yɛhaw obi a ɔnyɛɛ bɔne.  
Yɛpɛ kwan pa, adwuma pa, ne nkɔsoɔ a ɛwɔ nokware mu.

Nana Bosom Pa,  
asɛm yi yɛ akwantuo ne asɛm-pɔtee mpaebɔ.  
Mepa wo kyɛw, tie yɛn nne.  
Mepa wo kyɛw, gye yɛn mpaebɔ.  
Mepa wo kyɛw, ma ɛnyɛ dwoodwoo.

Sɛ asɛm yi yɛ nokware na ɛwɔ kwan pa so a, ma ɛnyɛ yiye.  
Sɛ asɛm yi nni kwan pa so a, san no, dwudwo no,  
na ma yɛnhu kwan pa a ɛkyɛn no.

Nana Bosom Pa,  
yɛnka ntam kwa.  
Yɛnni atoro wɔ w’anim.  
Yɛremfa wo din nyɛ bɔne.  
Yɛremfa wo din nhaw obi.  
Akyiwadeɛ a ɛyɛ wo de, ma yɛnte ase na yɛnto so.

Agoo.  
Nana Bosom Pa, gye.  
Nana Bosom Pa, tie.  
Nana Bosom Pa, ma asomdwoe.

Sɛ yɛafom wɔ kasa mu, ma kasa no nnwodwo.  
Sɛ yɛafom wɔ adwene mu, ma adwene no nhohoro.  
Sɛ akyiwadeɛ bi aka yɛn a, ma yɛnnya akɔmfoɔ mpaebɔ ne adwira,  
na asɛm no nsan ntena ne kwan pa so.

Yɛda wo ase.  
Ɛnyɛ dwoodwoo.  
Asomdwoe, asomdwoe, asomdwoe.

---

## Celestial Church

In the name of the Father, and of the Son, and of the Holy Spirit. Amen.

Hallelujah. Hallelujah. Hallelujah.  
Halleluyah, Halleluyah, Halleluyah.

O Lord God of Celestial Church of Christ, Father of our Lord Jesus Christ, receive our praise and thanksgiving. Let every word of this prayer rise before Thee in humility, faith, and peace.

Have mercy upon us, O God, according to thy lovingkindness: according unto the multitude of thy tender mercies blot out our transgressions.  
Wash us throughly from mine iniquity, and cleanse us from my sin.  
Create in us a clean heart, O God; and renew a right spirit within us.

Our Father which art in heaven,  
Hallowed be thy name.  
Thy kingdom come.  
Thy will be done in earth, as it is in heaven.  
Give us this day our daily bread.  
And forgive us our debts, as we forgive our debtors.  
And lead us not into temptation,  
but deliver us from evil:  
For thine is the kingdom, and the power, and the glory, for ever.  
Amen.

Baba wa ti mbẹ li ọrun,  
Ki a bọ̀wọ̀ fun orúkọ rẹ.  
Ki ìjọba rẹ dé.  
Ti ìfẹ́ rẹ ni ki a ṣe ni ayé, bí ti ọrun.  
Fún wa li òní oúnjẹ wa ojoojúmọ́.  
Dárí gbèsè wa jì wa, bí awa ti ń dárí gbèsè àwọn onígbèsè wa jì wọ́n.  
Má sì fà wa sinu ìdánwò,  
ṣùgbọ́n gbà wa lọwọ ibi.  
Nítorí tirẹ ni ìjọba, àti agbára, àti ògo, lailai.  
Amin.

I lift up mine eyes unto the hills,  
from whence cometh my help.  
My help cometh from the LORD,  
which made heaven and earth.  
He will not suffer thy foot to be moved:  
he that keepeth thee will not slumber.  
Behold, he that keepeth Israel  
shall neither slumber nor sleep.  
The LORD is thy keeper:  
the LORD is thy shade upon thy right hand.  
The sun shall not smite thee by day,  
nor the moon by night.  
The LORD shall preserve thee from all evil:  
he shall preserve thy soul.  
The LORD shall preserve thy going out and thy coming in  
from this time forth, and even for evermore.

The LORD is my shepherd; I shall not want.  
He maketh me to lie down in green pastures:  
he leadeth me beside the still waters.  
He restoreth my soul:  
he leadeth me in the paths of righteousness for his name's sake.  
Yea, though I walk through the valley of the shadow of death,  
I will fear no evil:  
for thou art with me;  
thy rod and thy staff they comfort me.  
Thou preparest a table before me in the presence of mine enemies:  
thou anointest my head with oil;  
my cup runneth over.  
Surely goodness and mercy shall follow me all the days of my life:  
and I will dwell in the house of the LORD for ever.

O Lord Jesus Christ, Son of the living God, look with mercy upon this event: 愿此次 YC 申请被录取，BD 顺利通过. Let Thy help and guidance stand. Let every required step be ordered in truth, wisdom, clarity, favor, and peace. Open the right door according to Thy holy will; remove obstacles without harm, without injustice, and without taking blessing, life, or rightful portion from another.

Lord, give wisdom where decisions must be made, courage where answers must be given, patience where waiting is required, and a peaceful heart in all outcomes. Let goodness and mercy follow this matter, and let the work be established by Thy grace.

Hallelujah. Hallelujah. Hallelujah.  
Halleluyah, Halleluyah, Halleluyah.

O Lord, receive thanksgiving. Keep this prayer within the faith of the Father, the Son, and the Holy Spirit. Let all be sealed by Thy mercy, by Thy holy will, and in the name of our Lord Jesus Christ.

Amen. Amen. Amen.

---

## Mami Wata 信仰

I stand by clean water with cool heart.  
Mami Wata, Mammy Water, Nne mmiri, Yeye Omi,  
I call only your name for this prayer.

Mami Wata o, Mami Wata o,  
bia, nuru olu m.  
Nne mmiri, nne oma,  
mmiri di ọcha, mmiri ndu.

Mammy Water, I hail you.  
Fine lady for water, mother for river,  
she wey sabi deep water,  
she wey hold mirror for truth,  
she wey cool hot heart.

Mami Wata o,  
for this YC application, make road open;  
for BD, make the passing smooth and clean.  
Make water clean, make road open,  
make bad mouth cool,  
make true word enter the right ear.  
No be to take another person blessing,  
no be to spoil another person road;  
only honest favor, clear judgment, and peaceful success I ask.

Yeye Omi, iya omi,  
bo this matter pelu omi funfun.  
Omi tutu, omi alaafia,  
ko si ija, ko si iro,  
alaafia ni mo pe.

Mami Wata o, Mammy Water o,  
no vex, no trouble.  
If any word don pass wrong,  
make wrong word fall for water.  
If any fear don rise,  
make cool water carry am go.  
Let mirror show truth,  
let river carry this request with peace.

Mmiri oma, kuru ihe ojoo laa.  
Mmiri ndu, mee ka obi di jụụ.  
Nne mmiri, nara olu m,  
nara mmiri a,  
nara okwu udo a.

Mami Wata o,  
I no call another spirit for this same mouth.  
Only Mami Wata name dey here.  
Peace for water,  
peace for road,  
peace for house,  
peace for this application path.

Clean water, cool water,  
wash away wrong calling, wrong promise, wrong fear.  
Make every improper request return to silence.  
Make only clean prayer stand.  
Let water make peace; let heart make peace; let road make peace.

Mammy Water, I thank you.  
Nne mmiri, daalu.  
Yeye Omi, mo dupe.  
Alaafia. Udo. Peace.

---

## Kimbanguism

Na nkombo ya Tata, ya Mwana mpe ya Molimo Mosantu. Amen.

Nzambi Tata, na miso na yo, biso bato na yo toyangani na motema moko mpo na likambo oyo: ete bosengi ya YC endimama, mpe ete BD eleka malamu na kimia, bosembo, mpe mwinda na yo.  
Yesu Kristo, Nkolo na biso, yamba losambo oyo, mpe tika Molimo Mosantu akamba makanisi, maloba, mikano, mpe misala nyonso.

Na loyembo ya kondima mpe ya kimia, tozongisi mitema na biso epai na yo, Nkolo.  
Bolingo.  
Mibeko.  
Misala.

Nkolo, toboyi kindoki, biloko ya nkisi, lokuta, koyina, koboma motema, kobebisa basusu, mpe misala nyonso ya molili.  
Tika ete motema na biso ezala peto liboso na yo.  
Tolingi elonga oyo kozanga kobotola lipamboli ya moto mosusu, kozanga kobebisa nzela ya moto mosusu, mpe kozanga kosenga pasi mpo na moto ata moko.

Tata na biso, ozali na likoló,  
nkombo na yo ezala mosantu,  
bokonzi na yo eya,  
mokano na yo esalema  
awa na mabele lokola na likoló.  
Pesa biso lelo bilei na biso ya mokolo.  
Limbisa biso masumu na biso,  
lokola biso mpe tolimbisaka baoyo basali biso mabe.  
Kotika biso te tokwea na komekama,  
kasi bikisa biso na moto mabe.  
Mpo na yo bokonzi, nguya mpe nkembo,  
libela na libela. Amen.

Nzembo 121:  
Nakotombola miso na ngai na bangomba:  
lisungi na ngai ekouta wapi?  
Lisungi na ngai ekouta epai ya Yawe,  
ye oyo asalaki likoló mpe mabele.  
Akotika lokolo na yo ekita te;  
mobateli na yo akolala pongi te.  
Tala, mobateli ya Isalaele  
akolala pongi te, akolala mpɔngi te.

Nkolo Nzambe, tala bosengi ya YC mpe likambo ya BD.  
Pesa bwanya, kimia, bososoli, maloba ya solo, mpe nzela ya bosembo.  
Soki ezali na mokano na yo, fungola ekuke ya kondimama, longola mikakatano kozanga kobebisa moto, mpe tika ete mosala nyonso esalema na pole, na bolingo, na mibeko, mpe na misala ya sembo.

Tika ete nyonso esalema na mokano na yo,  
na nkombo ya Yesu Kristo Nkolo na biso.

Nkolo, bomba biso na peto ya motema, na boyokani ya libota mpe ya lisanga, na bomoi ezangi masanga mabe, makaya, bangi, kindoki, mpe misala ya molili.  
Tika ete nkembo nyonso ezonga epai na yo moko, Tata, Mwana, mpe Molimo Mosantu.

Amen.

---

## Espiritismo Cruzado

En el nombre del Padre, y del Hijo, y del Espíritu Santo. Amén.

Dios todopoderoso, Padre de misericordia, ante tu presencia se pone esta oración para pedir luz, verdad, caridad y buen camino en este emprendimiento lícito: que la presente solicitud a YC sea recibida favorablemente, que pueda alcanzar admisión si conviene al bien, y que el paso de BD transcurra con claridad, orden y buen resultado.

Pater noster, qui es in caelis,  
sanctificetur nomen tuum;  
adveniat regnum tuum;  
fiat voluntas tua,  
sicut in caelo et in terra.  
Panem nostrum cotidianum da nobis hodie;  
et dimitte nobis debita nostra,  
sicut et nos dimittimus debitoribus nostris;  
et ne nos inducas in tentationem;  
sed libera nos a malo. Amen.

Ave Maria, gratia plena, Dominus tecum;  
benedicta tu in mulieribus,  
et benedictus fructus ventris tui, Iesus.  
Sancta Maria, Mater Dei,  
ora pro nobis peccatoribus,  
nunc et in hora mortis nostrae. Amen.

Creo en Dios, Padre todopoderoso,  
Creador del cielo y de la tierra.  
Creo en Jesucristo, su único Hijo, nuestro Señor,  
que fue concebido por obra y gracia del Espíritu Santo,  
nació de Santa María Virgen,  
padeció bajo el poder de Poncio Pilato,  
fue crucificado, muerto y sepultado,  
descendió a los infiernos,  
al tercer día resucitó de entre los muertos,  
subió a los cielos  
y está sentado a la derecha de Dios, Padre todopoderoso.  
Desde allí ha de venir a juzgar a vivos y muertos.  
Creo en el Espíritu Santo,  
la santa Iglesia católica,  
la comunión de los santos,  
el perdón de los pecados,  
la resurrección de la carne  
y la vida eterna. Amén.

Con licencia de Dios, con licencia de los buenos espíritus, con licencia del cuadro espiritual de luz, se saluda a los mayores de luz, a los ancestros buenos y a los guías protectores que caminan en caridad.

Moyuba Olofi, moyuba Olodumare, moyuba Olorun.  
Moyuba eggun, moyuba ara onu.  
Moyuba mi ile, moyuba awon agba.  
Eleguá agó, Eleguá agó, Eleguá agó.  
Eshu Elegbara, Laroyé.

Ángel de la Guarda, dulce compañía, no desampares ni de noche ni de día; pon paz en la mente, claridad en la palabra, firmeza en el trabajo y alegría con todos los santos, Jesús, José y María.

Espíritus protectores, guías de luz, buenos muertos, misioneros espirituales y cordón de caridad, si es voluntad de Dios y por el bien del alma, atiendan esta súplica: que esta solicitud a YC encuentre puertas lícitas, juicio justo, comunicación clara y recepción favorable; que el paso de BD sea ordenado, honesto, convincente y sin tropiezo injusto.

Ángel de la Guarda y guías protectores, acompañad este evento; abrid camino lícito, cerrad tropiezo injusto y sostened la mente, la palabra y el cuerpo en paz. Que no se busque despojar a nadie de su bien, mérito, oportunidad ni sustento; que el éxito pedido no nazca del daño ajeno, sino del trabajo recto, la verdad y la misericordia de Dios.

Dios mío, si esta petición conviene al adelanto espiritual y al bien común, concédela por tu misericordia; si no conviene, cambia el deseo en luz, paciencia, aprendizaje y entendimiento.

Hermanos que sufrís, hermanos confundidos, no se os manda ni se os desprecia; se os ofrece oración, caridad y camino. En nombre de Dios, recibid luz, dejad la perturbación, apartaos en paz y seguid a los buenos guías que os conduzcan.

Padre nuestro que estás en el cielo,  
santificado sea tu Nombre;  
venga a nosotros tu Reino;  
hágase tu voluntad  
en la tierra como en el cielo.  
Danos hoy nuestro pan de cada día;  
perdona nuestras ofensas,  
como también nosotros perdonamos a los que nos ofenden;  
no nos dejes caer en la tentación,  
y líbranos del mal. Amén.

Dios te salve, María,  
llena eres de gracia;  
el Señor es contigo.  
Bendita tú eres entre todas las mujeres,  
y bendito es el fruto de tu vientre, Jesús.  
Santa María, Madre de Dios,  
ruega por nosotros pecadores,  
ahora y en la hora de nuestra muerte. Amén.

Eleguá agó, Eleguá agó, Eleguá agó.  
Laroyé, Laroyé, Laroyé.

A los buenos espíritus se les da gracias; a los muertos de luz se les da luz; a los guías se les da respeto; a los ancestros buenos se les da memoria; a Dios se le da gloria. Que todo quede en paz, sin deuda, sin violencia, sin mandato y sin oscuridad.

Paz para los vivos, luz para los muertos, caridad para todos.  
En el nombre del Padre, y del Hijo, y del Espíritu Santo. Amén.

---

## 马达加斯加 Famadihana

Ry Razana malala,  
Ry Razambenay ao amin’ny tranon-drazana,  
ry razana nitahiry ny anarana sy ny fihavanana,  
henoy izahay taranakareo.

Izahay avy amin’ny ankohonana velona,  
mijoro eto amim-panajana,  
mitondra teny malemy sy fo madio,  
tsy hanadino anareo,  
tsy hanary ny lova,  
tsy hanapaka ny fihavanana.

Ry havanay nodimandry,  
anarana tsy very,  
ra tsy ritra,  
fahatsiarovana tsy maty,  
mipetraha am-piadanana eo anilan’ny razana,  
ary aoka ny fifankatiavana no hampifamatotra ny velona sy ny lasa.

Ry Razana,  
izao no teninay:  
mitondra fangataham-pitahiana izahay  
amin’ity raharaha lehibe ity:  
ny fangatahana YC mba horaisina,  
ary ny BD mba handalo tsara sy amim-pilaminana.

Mangataka tsodrano izahay,  
mangataka fitahiana,  
mangataka hasina,  
mangataka saina mazava sy lalana mahitsy.  
Aoka hisokatra ny varavarana mety,  
aoka hazava ny teny sy ny porofo,  
aoka ho marina ny fanapahan-kevitra,  
aoka ho tonga amin’ny soa ny ezaka.

Tsy mangataka hahavery anjaran’olona izahay,  
tsy mangataka hanimba ny lalan’ny hafa,  
tsy mangataka haka ny hasin’ny hafa;  
fa mangataka ny anjara mendrika,  
ny lalana madio,  
ary ny fitahiana tsy mandratra na iza na iza.

Aoka tsy hisy teny ratsy eto,  
aoka tsy hisy fifandirana eto,  
aoka tsy hisy fanadinoana eto.  
Ny razana hajaina,  
ny velona hifankatia,  
ny taranaka hitohy,  
ary ny asa atao hifanaraka amin’ny fahamarinana sy ny fihavanana.

Ry Razana,  
raiso ny fanajanay,  
raiso ny fahatsiarovanay,  
raiso ny teninay sy ny fo madio,  
ary omeo tsodrano izahay.

Tsodrano, tsodrano, tsodrano:  
ho tsara lalana ny fangatahana YC,  
ho milamina sy ho tanteraka soa ny BD,  
ho mazava ny saina,  
ho mahery ny fo,  
ho voatahy ny ezaka,  
ho miray hina ny ankohonana.

Misaotra, ry Razana.  
Mitoera am-piadanana ao amin’ny tranon-drazana.  
Izahay kosa hitahiry ny anarana,  
hitahiry ny fihavanana,  
hitahiry ny fomban-drazana,  
tsy hihoatra ny tenin’ny loholona,  
tsy hikasika izay masina raha tsy amin’ny fanajana sy ny firaisan’ny fianakaviana.

Ho an’ny razana ny haja,  
ho an’ny velona ny fihavanana,  
ho an’ny taranaka ny lalana mahitsy.  
Amin’ny fanajana sy ny fihavanana.

---

## Hoodoo / Rootwork

In the name of the Father, and of the Son, and of the Holy Ghost. Amen.

I stand before the Most High God with clean speech and a steady heart.  
Let this prayer be for this petition: 愿此次 YC 申请被录取，BD 顺利通过.  
Let no falsehood, coercion, wrongful hand, or proud demand be in it.

שִׁיר לַמַּעֲלוֹת אֶשָּׂא עֵינַי אֶל־הֶהָרִים מֵאַיִן יָבֹא עֶזְרִי׃  
עֶזְרִי מֵעִם יְהוָה עֹשֵׂה שָׁמַיִם וָאָרֶץ׃  
אַל־יִתֵּן לַמּוֹט רַגְלֶךָ אַל־יָנוּם שֹׁמְרֶךָ׃  
הִנֵּה לֹא־יָנוּם וְלֹא יִישָׁן שׁוֹמֵר יִשְׂרָאֵל׃  
יְהוָה שֹׁמְרֶךָ יְהוָה צִלְּךָ עַל־יַד יְמִינֶךָ׃  
יוֹמָם הַשֶּׁמֶשׁ לֹא־יַכֶּכָּה וְיָרֵחַ בַּלָּיְלָה׃  
יְהוָה יִשְׁמָרְךָ מִכָּל־רָע יִשְׁמֹר אֶת־נַפְשֶׁךָ׃  
יְהוָה יִשְׁמָר־צֵאתְךָ וּבוֹאֶךָ מֵעַתָּה וְעַד־עוֹלָם׃

As the eyes are lifted to the hills, let help come from the Lord.  
Let the road of this application be opened in righteousness.  
Let the proper door be seen, the proper word be spoken, the proper judgment be made.  
Let confusion be cleared away, delay be loosened, and needless hindrance be cut from the path.  
Let favor come by honest merit, true preparation, clean communication, and right timing.

I speak no harm into the innocent.  
I bind no unwilling heart.  
I seek no one’s dispossession, no one’s loss, no shortening of another life, and no taking of another’s rightful blessing.  
If this petition touches reviewers, partners, officers, readers, or decision-makers, let it touch them only in justice, clarity, mercy, and truthful discernment.

Set this petition under the judgment of the Most High.  
What is righteous, establish it.  
What is crooked, remove it.  
What is not mine to command, return it to God.  
Guard the going out and the coming in of this matter from this time forth, and even for evermore.

חָנֵּנִי אֱלֹהִים כְּחַסְדֶּךָ כְּרֹב רַחֲמֶיךָ מְחֵה פְשָׁעָי׃  
הֶרֶב כַּבְּסֵנִי מֵעֲוֹנִי וּמֵחַטָּאתִי טַהֲרֵנִי׃  
לֵב טָהוֹר בְּרָא־לִי אֱלֹהִים וְרוּחַ נָכוֹן חַדֵּשׁ בְּקִרְבִּי׃

I take back every crooked word, every anxious command, every petition not fit to stand before God.  
Cleanse this work, cleanse this road, cleanse this tongue, and let only what is lawful, merciful, and rightly ordered remain.

Amen. Amen. Amen.

---

## 约鲁巴 · Ifa / Òrìṣà 崇拜

Ìbà Olódùmarè.  
Ìbà Ilẹ̀.  
Ìbà Orí mi.  
Ìbà àwọn Egúngún ara òrun.  
Ìbà Èṣù Láàlú, Elegbára, onílé ọ̀nà.  
Ìbà Òrúnmìlà, Ẹlẹ́rìí ìpín.

Orí mi, àpẹrẹ.  
Orí mi, gbé mi.  
Orí mi, má ṣe mí.  
Orí mi, má gbàgbé mi.  
Orí mi, jẹ́ kí n rí ire.  
Orí mi, jẹ́ kí n kọjá ibi.

Òrúnmìlà, Ẹlẹ́rìí ìpín,  
Ìbikejì Olódùmarè,  
A-jé-jù-ogun,  
A-tún-orí-ti-kò-sùnwọ̀n ṣe,  
Ọlọ́gbọ́n tí ń mọ ọjọ́ ikú,  
Ọlọ́gbọ́n tí ń mọ ọjọ́ àìkú,  
Bàbá mi, Òrúnmìlà, gbọ́ ohùn mi.

Mo dúró níwájú rẹ̀ pẹ̀lú ìrẹ̀lẹ̀.  
Mo wá fún ire ìṣẹ́lẹ̀ yìí:  
kí ìbéèrè YC jẹ́ gbígbà,  
kí BD kọjá lọ́nà rere,  
kí ọ̀nà ìmúṣẹ ṣí,  
kí ọgbọ́n, ìwà pẹ̀lẹ́, àti àlàáfíà bá gbogbo ìgbésẹ̀ rẹ̀ lọ.

Jẹ́ kí ire àṣeyọrí wọlé.  
Jẹ́ kí ibi ìdènà kúrò.  
Jẹ́ kí ọ̀nà mi ṣí.  
Jẹ́ kí ọkàn mi balẹ̀.  
Jẹ́ kí Orí mi gba ire.  
Kí ire yìí má gba ire ẹlòmíràn.  
Kí àṣeyọrí yìí má dín ẹ̀mí ẹnikẹ́ni kù.  
Kí ohun gbogbo wá ní ìbámu pẹ̀lú ayé rere, ìwà rere, àti ìpín rere.

Mo dúpẹ́, Olódùmarè.  
Mo dúpẹ́, Orí mi.  
Mo dúpẹ́, àwọn Egúngún.  
Mo dúpẹ́, Èṣù Elegbára.  
Mo dúpẹ́, Òrúnmìlà.

Kí Orí mi má jẹ́ kí n rú eewọ.  
Kí ọ̀rọ̀ mi má kọjá àṣẹ tí ó tọ́.  
Bí ìtúnṣe bá yẹ níwájú Ifá,  
kí ọ̀nà rẹ̀ ṣí sí ọwọ́ ẹni tí a kọ́,  
pẹ̀lú ìrẹ̀lẹ̀, ìmọ̀, àti ìwà pẹ̀lẹ́.

Àṣẹ.  
Àṣẹ.  
Àṣẹ.

## Cherubim and Seraphim

In the name of the Father, and of the Son, and of the Holy Spirit. Amen.

Halleluyah.  
Halleluyah.  
Halleluyah.

Oluwa Ọlọrun Olódùmarè, Baba wa, a wá síwájú rẹ ní ìrẹ̀lẹ̀ àti ní ìgbàgbọ́.  
A jẹ́wọ́ ẹ̀ṣẹ̀ wa níwájú rẹ; wẹ̀ wa mọ́, tún ọkàn wa ṣe, kí o sì dá ẹsẹ̀ wa sí ọ̀nà ìmọ́lẹ̀ rẹ.

Baba wa ti mbẹ li ọrun,  
Ki a bọ̀wọ̀ fun orukọ rẹ;  
Ki ijọba rẹ de;  
Ifẹ tirẹ ni ki a ṣe ni aiye bi ti ọrun.  
Fun wa li oni onjẹ ojo wa.  
Dari ẹ̀ṣẹ̀ wa ji wa,  
bi awa ti dari ji awọn ti o ṣẹ̀ wa.  
Má ṣe fà wa sinu idanwo,  
ṣugbọn gbà wa lọwọ ibi.  
Nitori tirẹ ni ijọba, ati agbara, ati ogo, lailai. Amin.

The LORD is my shepherd; I shall not want.  
He maketh me to lie down in green pastures:  
he leadeth me beside the still waters.  
He restoreth my soul:  
he leadeth me in the paths of righteousness for his name’s sake.

I will lift up mine eyes unto the hills, from whence cometh my help.  
My help cometh from the LORD, which made heaven and earth.  
He will not suffer thy foot to be moved: he that keepeth thee will not slumber.

Ẹmi Mimọ, sọ̀kalẹ̀.  
Ẹmi Mimọ, wá bá wa gbe.  
Ẹmi Mimọ, tọ́ wa sí ọ̀nà ọgbọ́n, àlàáfíà, àti ìmọ́lẹ̀.

Oluwa Jesu Kristi, ní orúkọ rẹ ni a gbé ìbéèrè yìí wá:  
kí ìwé-ìbéèrè YC yìí rí ojú rere, kí ilẹ̀kùn rere ṣí,  
kí BD sì kọjá lọ ní ìrọ̀rùn, ní ìtẹ́lọ́run, àti ní àlàáfíà.

Baba, jẹ́ kí gbogbo ìpinnu, ìtúpalẹ̀, ìjíròrò, àti ìgbésẹ̀ tó wà níwájú rẹ̀ jẹ́ ní ìbámu pẹ̀lú ìfẹ́ rẹ.  
Jẹ́ kí ọgbọ́n, ìtẹ́lọ́run, ìmọ̀ràn rere, àti ìtẹ́sí rere bá gbogbo ọ̀nà yìí lọ.  
A kò bẹ̀bẹ̀ fún ìbùkún tí yóò gba ti ẹlòmíràn, a kò sì fẹ́ kí ẹnikẹ́ni bàjẹ́ nítorí ìbéèrè wa;  
ṣùgbọ́n jẹ́ kí o ṣí ọ̀nà tí ó mọ́, tí ó tọ́, tí ó sì ń mú ogo wá fún orúkọ rẹ.

No weapon that is formed against this righteous journey shall prosper;  
and every tongue that shall rise against it in judgment thou shalt condemn,  
not for harm to any person, but that confusion, fear, and needless obstacle may be removed.

Ní orúkọ Jesu Kristi, a fi gbogbo ìṣẹ̀lẹ̀ yìí lé ọwọ́ rẹ.  
Jẹ́ kí àánú rẹ ṣáájú wa, kí ìtọ́sọ́nà rẹ bá wa rìn,  
kí àwọn angẹli rẹ sin ọ nípa pípa ọ̀nà wa mọ́ ní àlàáfíà.

A dúpẹ́ lọwọ rẹ, Oluwa.  
A yin orúkọ rẹ.  
A gba pé ìfẹ́ rẹ dára, ìdájọ́ rẹ tọ́, àti àánú rẹ ń bẹ títí láé.

Oluwa, pa wa mọ́ ní ìwà mímọ́, ní ìrònúpìwàdà, ní ìrẹ̀lẹ̀, àti ní ìbáṣepọ̀ rere pẹ̀lú ìjọ rẹ.  
Má jẹ́ kí a yí adura sí ohun ìṣòwò, ìbẹ̀rù, tàbí ìfẹ́ ara wa;  
ṣùgbọ́n jẹ́ kí adura wa wà nínú Bibeli, nínú ìmọ́lẹ̀ Jesu Kristi, àti nínú ẹ̀rí rere ti Ẹmi Mimọ.

Amen.  
Halleluyah.  
Halleluyah.  
Halleluyah.

## 基库尤 Mungiki

Ngai wa Kĩrĩnyaga,  
Ngai wa Gĩkũyũ na Mũmbi,  
Thai, thathaiya Ngai, thai.

Ngai, nĩ tũrĩ haha na ngoro njega,  
tũgũkũhoya ũigua ihooya rĩitũ.  
Thai, thathaiya Ngai, thai.

Ngai, rora ũhoro wa YC application,  
ũhe njĩra ĩtheru, ũmenyo, na ũthingu,  
nĩguo ĩamũkĩrwo na thayũ.  
Rora o na ũhoro wa BD,  
ũhe gũthiĩ mbere wega na gũhĩtũka kũrĩa kwega.  
Thai, thathaiya Ngai, thai.

Ngai, tũtiũria kũnyiita irathimo cia andũ angĩ,  
tũtiũria kũhinyia mũoyo kana mũciĩ wa andũ angĩ.  
Heana thayũ,  
heana ũiguano,  
heana ũthingu,  
heana ũtheri wa njĩra ĩno.  
Thai, thathaiya Ngai, thai.

Ngai wa Kĩrĩnyaga,  
Ngai wa maithe maitũ,  
Ngai wa maithe ma maithe maitũ,  
tũiguĩre, tũrathime, tũhe thayũ.  
Iga ciugo ici irĩ na thayũ,  
iga njĩra ĩno irĩ na ũtheri,  
iga moko maitũ matikahingie ũũru.  
Thai, thathaiya Ngai, thai.
